# astro-ph.HE [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Fluxes of Generic Extreme-Mass-Ratio Inspirals with a Spinning Secondary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18075)
*Qiuxin Cui,Wen-Biao Han*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究构建了极端质量比旋进（EMRI）系统中含次级天体自旋的引力波通量和波形模型，在线性自旋近似下推导了运动基本常数的轨道平均演化方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极端质量比旋进（extreme mass-ratio inspirals, EMRIs）是未来空间引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）观测的关键目标。将次级天体的自旋纳入波形模型不仅能提高测量精度，还能为恒星质量天体的自旋分布提供重要见解。

Method: 在Kerr背景下采用线性自旋近似（linear-spin approximation），利用辐射处方（radiative prescription，即半推迟场减半超前场）推导了运动基本常数（能量、角动量、类Carter常数和平行自旋分量）的轨道平均演化方程。

Result: 构建了含自旋次级天体的EMRI通量和波形框架，该框架为生成包含次级自旋的波形提供了可处理的途径，并具备未来进一步简化的潜力。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个包含次级天体自旋的EMRI波形建模框架，为未来引力波观测中精确测量恒星质量天体自旋分布奠定了基础。

Abstract: Extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs), comprising a stellar-mass compact object (CO) orbiting a supermassive black hole (BH), are key targets for future space-based gravitational-wave (GW) observatories. Incorporating the spin of the secondary body into waveform models not only enhances measurement precision but also offers insight into the spin distribution of stellar-mass objects. In this work, we construct the flux and waveform for an EMRI with a spinning secondary in a Kerr background under the linear-spin approximation. Using the radiative prescription (half-retarded minus half-advanced field), we derive orbit-averaged evolution equations for the fundamental constants of motion, including the energy, angular momentum, Carter-like constant, and the parallel spin component. This framework provides a tractable route to generating waveforms that incorporate the secondary spin, with the potential for further simplification in future work.

</details>


### [2] [Probing Kerr black hole in a uniform Bertotti-Robinson magnetic field through astrophysical quasi-periodic oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18129)
*Hamza Rehman,Sanjar Shaymatov,Saddam Hussain,Tao Zhu*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了浸没在均匀Bertotti-Robinson磁场中的Kerr黑洞周围高频准周期振荡（QPOs）的行为。通过贝叶斯推断和马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）分析，利用多个黑洞X射线双星观测数据约束黑洞参数，发现磁场参数虽小但不可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解均匀Bertotti-Robinson磁场中Kerr黑洞周围的高频准周期振荡行为，探究磁场对测试粒子运动、轨道动力学以及QPO共振机制的影响。

Method: 通过确定测地线方程并计算相应的轨道、径向和垂直向心频率来分析测试粒子运动。基于参数共振和强迫共振机制构建QPO模型理论框架，利用多个黑洞X射线双星观测数据，通过贝叶斯推断和马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）分析约束黑洞参数。

Result: 在参数共振模型框架下，对于X射线双星GRO J1655-40、GRS 1915+105、H1743-322和M82~X-1，在68%置信水平下获得了无量纲参数b=Bm的非零值，而其他源仅获得90%置信水平的上限。在强迫共振模型中，所有考虑的X射线双星源的磁场参数仅获得90%置信区间的上限。

Conclusion: 分析表明磁场参数值虽小但不可忽略，对粒子动力学和向心频率产生微小修正。在MCMC分析推断的允许参数范围内，进一步通过最内稳定圆轨道性质和薄吸积盘的辐射特性（包括能流和温度分布）检验了磁场的影响。

Abstract: In this study, the behavior of high-frequency quasi-periodic oscillations (QPOs) is investigated around a Kerr black hole immersed in a uniform Bertotti-Robinson magnetic field. The motion of the test particle is analyzed by determining the geodesic equations and evaluating the corresponding orbital, radial, and vertical epicyclic frequencies. These fundamental frequencies are used to construct the theoretical framework of QPO models based on parametric and forced resonance mechanisms. Observational data obtained from several black hole X-ray binaries (GRO J1655-40, XTE J1550-564, XTE J1859+226, GRS 1915+105, H1743-322, M82~X-1, and Sgr~A$^{*}$) are used to constrain the black hole parameters through Bayesian inference and Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) analyses. For the X-ray binaries GRO J1655-40, GRS 1915+105, H1743-322, and M82~X-1, nonzero values of the dimensionless parameter $b=Bm$ are obtained at the $68\%$ confidence level within the framework of the parametric resonance model, while only upper bounds at the $90\%$ confidence level are obtained for the remaining sources. In contrast, in the case of the forced resonance model, only an upper bound at the $90\%$ confidence interval is obtained for the magnetic field parameter for all considered X-ray binary sources. The analysis indicates that the value of the magnetic field parameter is small but not negligible, producing minor modifications to particle dynamics and epicyclic frequencies. The influence of the magnetic field is further examined through the properties of the innermost stable circular orbit and the radiative properties of the thin accretion disk, including the energy flux and temperature profiles, within the allowed parameter range inferred from the MCMC analysis.

</details>

# math.OA [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Spectral continuity of almost commutative manifolds for the $C^1$ topology on Riemannian metrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19128)
*Frederic Latremoliere*

Main category: math.OA

TL;DR: 该论文证明了在几乎可交换模型中，狄拉克算符（Dirac operator）的谱作为黎曼度规（Riemannian metric）的函数具有连续性，并基于谱邻近性（spectral propinquity）发展了一种新方法，同时将该方法应用于量子环面（quantum tori）和量子螺线管（quantum solenoids）等完全非交换情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于粒子物理标准模型（standard model of particle physics）中几乎可交换模型（almost commutative models）的基本问题：狄拉克算符的谱对度规变化的依赖性。由于系统的物理性质根本上编码于该谱中，因此需要研究这些模型的几何或物理内容的稳定性。

Method: 采用基于谱邻近性（spectral propinquity）的新方法证明狄拉克算符谱的连续性。该方法允许黎曼度规（在C¹拓扑中）和有限维因子的狄拉克算符同时变化，并将结果应用于完全非交换的示例族。

Result: 证明了几乎可交换模型中狄拉克算符的谱作为底层黎曼度规的函数具有连续性。该结果也提供了经典结论的新证明，并成功应用于量子环面（quantum tori）和量子螺线管（quantum solenoids）等完全非交换情形。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明几乎可交换模型的几何或物理内容具有稳定性，同时发展的谱邻近性方法具有广泛适用性，不仅为经典结果提供了新证明，还能处理完全非交换的量子几何示例。

Abstract: Almost commutative models provide a framework for Connes' work on the standard model of particle physics. These models are constructed as products of a the canonical spectral triple of a compact connected spin manifold with a finite dimensional spectral triple. Motivated by the fundamental question of the dependence of the spectra of Dirac operators under change of metrics, we prove the continuity of the spectra of Dirac operators for almost commutative models as functions of the underlying Riemannian metric. We allow both the Riemannian metric (in the $C^1$ topology) and the Dirac operator of the finite-dimensional factor to vary simultaneously. Since the physics of the system is fundamentally encoded in this spectrum, this result is a form of stability result regarding the geometry, or physical, content of these models. This result is based upon a novel approach to prove continuity of spectra of Dirac operators using the spectral propinquity. Notably, this method provides a new, different proof of the classical results as well. To illustrate the versatility of our new method, we also apply our results to completely non-commutative family of examples, including quantum tori and quantum solenoids.

</details>

# math.OC [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Optimal strategies for controlled growth in metastable Kawasaki dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18903)
*Simone Baldassarri,Maike C. de Jongh*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该研究为二维正方晶格有限区域内的低温亚稳态伊辛模型（Ising model）建立了马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）框架，分析外部控制器如何通过适时添加和移动粒子引导系统达到全占据态。研究构建了约束于单簇构型的简化MDP，并比较了两种奖励结构下的最优策略差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析外部控制器如何引导低温亚稳态伊辛模型（Ising model）在川崎动力学（Kawasaki dynamics）下演化至全占据态。通过建立马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）框架，探讨在有限二维晶格中通过控制粒子添加和移动来指导系统演化的可能性。

Method: 方法包括：为低温亚稳态伊辛模型（Ising model）建立马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）框架；构建约束于单簇构型（single cluster）的简化MDP，该区域粒子附着（attachment）概率高于脱离（detachment）；分析两种奖励结构：仅依赖到达目标构型时间的效率标准，以及包含动作相关能量成本的能量奖励函数。

Result: 研究结果表明，在两种奖励结构下获得了精确的最优策略（optimal policies），但这些策略表现出不同行为：基于效率的标准促进从簇边界中心（boundary centers）生长，而基于能量的奖励函数则倾向于在簇的角落（corners）生长。

Conclusion: 结论显示，在马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）框架下，外部控制器可以通过不同策略引导系统演化，具体策略取决于奖励结构的设计。效率优化和能量优化的目标会导致系统采取不同的生长模式，这为控制复杂系统的演化提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this paper, we develop a Markov decision process (MDP) formulation for the low--temperature metastable Ising model evolving according to Kawasaki dynamics in a finite box of the two--dimensional square lattice. We analyze how an external controller can guide the system to the all--occupied state by appropriately adding and moving particles at specified moments in time. To this end, we construct a reduced MDP on a constrained family of configurations having a single cluster, a regime where particle attachment is more likely than detachment. We investigate two reward structures: one that depends solely on the time to reach the target configuration, and another that incorporates action--dependent energy costs. Within this MDP framework, we characterize the exact optimal policies under both reward structures, which turn out to have a different behavior: while a purely efficiency--based criterion promotes the growth from the boundary centers of the cluster, an energy--based reward function favours the growth at the corners of the cluster.

</details>

# physics.flu-dyn [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [Reduction of Triadic Interactions Suppresses Intermittency and Anomalous Dissipation in Turbulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19180)
*Anikat Kankaria,Ritwik Mukherjee,Sugan Durai Murugan,Marco Edoardo Rosti,Samriddhi Sankar Ray*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该研究通过系统性地缩减傅里叶空间三元相互作用网络，发现三维湍流的统计特征发生显著变化：间歇性被抑制，大雷诺数极限下平均耗散率趋于零，表明异常耗散并非不可压缩湍流的固有属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究三维湍流（three-dimensional turbulence）的统计特征如何响应傅里叶空间（Fourier-space）三元相互作用网络（triadic interaction network）的系统性缩减，特别是异常耗散（anomalous dissipation）现象是否依赖于完整的非线性相互作用组合。

Method: 采用直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulations）方法，分别对分形（fractally）和均匀（homogeneously）稀疏化的纳维-斯托克斯（Navier-Stokes）动力学进行模拟，通过渐进式稀疏化活动模态集合来研究湍流特征变化。

Result: 随着活动模态的渐进稀疏化，间歇性（intermittency）被系统性地抑制，大雷诺数（Reynolds-number）极限下平均耗散率趋于零；结构函数指数（structure-function exponents）坍缩到其量纲值，多重分形奇异性谱（multifractal singularity spectrum）收缩，从指数谱尾提取的解析宽度单调增加，表明速度场得到显著正则化。

Conclusion: 研究结果直接证明不可压缩湍流中的异常耗散并非纳维-斯托克斯方程的普适属性，而是需要其完整的三元非线性相互作用组合的丰富性；湍流的异常统计特征高度依赖于相互作用网络的复杂性。

Abstract: We investigate how the defining statistical features of three-dimensional turbulence respond to systematic reductions of the Fourier-space triadic interaction network. Using direct numerical simulations of both fractally and homogeneously decimated Navier-Stokes dynamics, we show that progressive thinning of the set of active modes leads to a systematic suppression of intermittency and, most strikingly, to the vanishing of the mean dissipation rate in the large-Reynolds-number limit. Structure-function exponents collapse onto their dimensional values, the multifractal singularity spectrum contracts, and the analyticity width extracted from the exponential spectral tail increases monotonically with decimation-each indicating a substantial regularization of the velocity field. Together, these results provide direct evidence that anomalous dissipation in incompressible turbulence is not a generic property of the Navier-Stokes equations, but instead requires the full combinatorial richness of their triadic nonlinear interactions.

</details>

# cond-mat.supr-con [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Light induced magnetization in d-wave superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18134)
*Maxim Dzero,Vladyslav Kozii*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文开发了d波超导体中逆法拉第效应的微观理论，使用扩展的Keldysh-Nambu准经典形式计算了由外部单色辐射诱导的直流电流密度，并评估了诱导静态磁化的大小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在建立d波超导体中逆法拉第效应（inverse Faraday effect）的微观理论，以理解外部辐射如何诱导直流响应和静态磁化。

Method: 采用扩展的Keldysh-Nambu准经典形式（quasiclassical formalism），计算了由外部单色辐射诱导的直流电流密度分量，并分析了分支布居不平衡（branch population imbalance）对非线性非局域直流响应的贡献机制。

Result: 理论明确展示了分支布居不平衡如何产生非零的非线性和非局域直流响应，评估了诱导电流的大小并获得了诱导静态磁化（static magnetization）的估计值。

Conclusion: 简要讨论了该理论的实验意义以及未来工作的扩展方向，为d波超导体中光诱导磁化现象提供了微观理论框架。

Abstract: We develop a microscopic theory of the inverse Faraday effect in d-wave superconductors. An extended version of the Keldysh-Nambu quasiclassical formalism is used to compute the dc-component of the current density induced by an external monochromatic radiation. Our work explicitly demonstrates how branch population imbalance produces nonvanishing nonlinear and nonlocal dc-response. We evaluate the magnitude of the induced current and obtain estimates for the induced static magnetization. Experimental implications of our theory and future extensions of our work are briefly discussed.

</details>


### [7] [Ultrafast dynamics and light-induced superconductivity from first principles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18182)
*Alejandro Simon,James Shi,Eva Kogler,Reed Foster,Dominik Spath,Emma Batson,Pedro N. Ferreira,Mihir Sahoo,Rohit Prasankumar,Phillip D. Keathley,Karl K. Berggren,Christoph Heil*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种从头算（ab-initio）模型，用于描述光辐照超导薄膜的非平衡响应，能够定量再现泵浦-探测实验中的光学响应，并预测光诱导超导态可在更多材料中实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导材料在远离平衡态时展现出独特的涌现性质，但缺乏能够定量描述实验观测的第一性原理处理方法。本研究旨在填补这一空白，为光辐照超导薄膜的非平衡响应提供理论框架。

Method: 在传统电子-声子介导超导性框架内，开发了从头算模型，利用新的数值技术直接在实频轴上求解Migdal-Eliashberg方程。该方法应用于Pb、LaH₁₀、K₃C₆₀和CaC₆等材料体系。

Result: 模型成功定量再现了Pb和LaH₁₀在泵浦-探测实验中的微分反射率测量结果。对K₃C₆₀的计算揭示了在足够强度的超快中红外脉冲辐照后会产生光诱导超导态，其增强机制源于准粒子被激发到与最强电子-声子耦合共振的能量区域。对CaC₆的计算预测了类似的光诱导超导能隙。

Conclusion: 光诱导超导性可在比先前认识更多的材料中实现。该研究不仅解释了光诱导超导态的性质，还阐明了后续的准粒子和声子动力学，为理解非平衡超导现象提供了定量理论框架。

Abstract: Experiments on superconducting materials have unveiled unique emergent properties when they are driven far from equilibrium. However, a quantitative first-principles treatment that describes experimental observations is lacking. In this work, we develop an ab-initio model for the nonequilibrium response of optically irradiated superconducting films within the framework of conventional electron-phonon-mediated superconductivity, leveraging new numerical techniques to solve the Migdal-Eliashberg equations directly on the real-frequency axis. This enables us to quantitatively reproduce the optical response of superconducting films in pump-probe experiments and validate our approach on measurements of the differential reflectance of Pb and LaH$_{10}$ in response to a pump excitation. Similar calculations performed on the alkali-doped fulleride K$_3$C$_{60}$ reveal that a photo-induced superconducting state is generated after irradiation by an ultrafast mid-infrared pulse of sufficient intensity, as reported in prior experimental work. The enhancement in this framework is attributed to the excitation of quasiparticles to energies resonant with the strongest electron-phonon coupling in K$_3$C$_{60}$, in close analogy to the mechanism for enhancement of superconductivity under microwave irradiation, explaining the nature of the photo-induced superconducting state and elucidating the subsequent quasiparticle and phonon dynamics. Our results suggest that photo-induced superconductivity is accessible in more materials than previously recognized. We demonstrate this by performing calculations on calcium-intercalated graphite, CaC$_6$, and predict a similar photo-induced superconducting gap.

</details>


### [8] [Fast Real-Axis Eliashberg Calculations: Full-bandwidth solutions beyond the constant density of states approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18199)
*Alejandro Simon,James Shi,Dominik Spath,Eva Kogler,Reed Foster,Emma Batson,Pedro N. Ferreira,Mihir Sahoo,Phillip D. Keathley,Warren E. Pickett,Rohit Prasankumar,Karl K. Berggren,Christoph Heil*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在实频率轴上直接求解有限温度Migdal-Eliashberg方程的方法，避免了传统虚轴计算所需的解析延拓步骤，能够更直接地获取实验相关的光谱函数和输运性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验相关的超导特征需要获取实频率量，如光谱函数和输运性质，但传统的Migdal-Eliashberg计算通常在虚轴上进行，然后进行解析延拓，这一步骤数值上不稳定且可能掩盖物理相关的光谱特征。

Method: 提出了一种在实频率轴上直接求解有限温度Migdal-Eliashberg方程的实用方法，保留了全带宽电子结构效应。该方法通过能量依赖的电子态密度考虑粒子-空穴不对称性，避免了实轴计算中常用的常数态密度近似，并包含了静态屏蔽库仑贡献。引入了一种高效的数值技术来求解Migdal-Eliashberg积分，其计算成本与实频率网格呈线性关系。

Result: 将该方法应用于H₃S体系，其中费米能级附近的范霍夫奇点产生了强烈的粒子-空穴不对称性。全带宽解产生的光谱与常数态密度近似有明显差异，并使超导能隙和线形与实验更加吻合，突显了能带结构细节的重要性。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法使得高分辨率、全带宽实轴计算变得可行，无需解析延拓即可直接获取相互作用格林函数和衍生可观测量。此外，这些方法为在Eliashberg理论框架内进行时间依赖、非平衡模拟打开了大门。

Abstract: Experimentally relevant signatures of superconductivity require access to real-frequency quantities, such as the spectral functions, optical response, and transport properties, yet Migdal-Eliashberg calculations are commonly performed on the imaginary axis and then analytically continued, a step that is numerically delicate and can obscure physically relevant spectral features. Here we present a practical route to solving the finite-temperature Migdal-Eliashberg equations directly on the real-frequency axis, while retaining the effects from the full-bandwidth electronic structure. Our formulation accounts for particle-hole asymmetry through an energy-dependent electronic density of states, avoiding the constant density of states approximation often used in real-axis calculations, and includes a static screened Coulomb contribution. We introduce an efficient numerical technique to solve the Migdal-Eliashberg integrals whose computational cost scales linearly with the real-frequency grid, making high-resolution, full-bandwidth real-axis calculations feasible and providing direct access to the interacting Green's function and derived observables without analytic continuation. As an illustration, we apply the method to H$_{3}$S, where a van-Hove singularity near the Fermi level produces strong particle-hole asymmetry. The full-bandwidth solution yields noticeably different spectra than the constant density of states approximation and brings the superconducting gap and lineshapes into closer agreement with experiment, highlighting when band-structure details are essential. Furthermore, the methods presented here open the door to time-dependent, nonequilibrium simulations within Eliashberg theory.

</details>


### [9] [Nb$_3$Sn Films Exhibiting Continuous Supercurrent Across a Diffusion Bonded Seam](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18351)
*Andre Juliao,Wenura Withanage,Nikolya Cadavid,Anatolii Polyanskii,Lance D Cooley*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种通过Nb蒸气溅射沉积在加热条件下实现青铜件扩散连接的方法，同时形成跨越接缝的均匀Nb₃Sn超导薄膜，为磁体导体和射频腔应用中的Nb₃Sn材料连接提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在开发一种连接Nb₃Sn超导材料的新方法，特别是在磁体导体和射频腔（RF cavity）应用中。传统方法在连接Nb₃Sn材料时面临挑战，需要探索能够实现超电流自由跨越接缝的可靠连接技术。

Method: 采用热青铜（hot bronze）方法：将多对青铜件沿共同接缝连接，在约715°C加热条件下通过溅射沉积（sputter deposition）暴露于Nb蒸气中形成扩散连接（diffusion bond）。通过抛光和调整使表面垂直于Nb通量，接缝平行于Nb通量。同时进行Nb向Nb₃Sn的转化，形成覆盖青铜表面并跨越接缝的均匀薄膜。

Result: 通过磁光成像（magneto-optical imaging）表征超导性能显示，在9K冷却并屏蔽或捕获低磁场时，多个样品中超电流（supercurrent）能够自由跨越接缝流动。预涂层方法（pre-coating method）产生的接缝覆盖程度不一，且质量均不及热青铜方法获得的样品。

Conclusion: 热青铜方法成功实现了青铜件的扩散连接并同时形成均匀的Nb₃Sn薄膜，使超电流能够自由跨越接缝。该方法为磁体导体和射频腔应用中Nb₃Sn材料的连接提供了有前景的新途径，而预涂层方法的效果相对较差。

Abstract: Multiple pairs of bronze pieces were joined along a common seam and then exposed to Nb vapor via sputter deposition during heating at $\sim$715 $^\circ$C to form a diffusion bond between the pieces. Polishing and alignment of the pieces created smooth surfaces normal to the Nb flux with seams perpendicular to the surface (i.e. parallel to the Nb flux). Conversion of Nb to Nb$_3$Sn took place simultaneously with diffusion bonding, resulting in Nb$_3$Sn thin films that coated bronze surfaces and spanned seams with uniform thickness. Characterization of superconducting properties via magneto-optical imaging suggests that supercurrent flows freely across the seam in several examples when cooled to 9 K and shielding or trapping low magnetic field. Modification of the process to coat the pieces with Nb prior to diffusion bonding and Nb$_3$Sn formation resulted in varying degrees of seam coverage by the resultant Nb$_3$Sn films. The pre-coating method did not produce any example with quality comparable to the examples obtained by the hot bronze approach. This work could enable new approaches to joining Nb$_3$Sn materials in magnet conductor and RF cavity applications.

### [10] [Weak Localization and Magnetoconductance in Percolative Superconducting Aluminum Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18684)
*Kazumasa Yamada,Bunjyu Shinozaki,Takashi Kawaguti*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验测量了二维铝薄膜的片电阻（sheet resistance）随温度T和磁场H的变化。通过将理论拟合到接近临界温度Tc的磁导（magnetoconductance）数据，使用扩散常数D(T)作为拟合参数，获得了反常的温度依赖扩散常数。进一步从D(T)分析中提取了渗流理论中的电子扩散指数θ。

Result: 研究发现片电阻R□与扩散指数θ的关系中，θ值在约1.5kΩ附近发生突变，这一行为表明存在从均匀到非均匀的交叉转变。对于渗流薄膜，在5T磁场下发现了预因子αT与片电阻的强依赖关系，关系αT∝1/R□可以通过渗流标度律模型进行定性解释。

Conclusion: 研究证实了二维铝薄膜中存在从均匀行为到非均匀（渗流）行为的交叉转变，这一结果与先前通过上临界场温度依赖关系获得的结果相似。渗流薄膜中预因子与电阻的反比关系支持了渗流标度律模型的适用性。

Abstract: In order to investigate the crossover from the homogeneous behavior to inhomogeneous (percolative) one, the temperature $T$ and magnetic field H dependence of the sheet resistance $R_\square$ have been measured for two-dimensional granular aluminum films. Fitting the theory to data of magnetoconductance near $T_C$ with use of the diffusion constant $D(T)$ as a fitting parameter, we have obtained the anomalous $T$-dependent diffusion constant $D$. From the analysis of $D(T)$, the electron diffusion index $θ$, a certain critical exponent in percolation theory, has been obtained. In the relation $R_\square-θ$, the value of $θ$ varies abruptly near $1.5kω$. This behavior suggesting the above mentioned crossover is similar to our previous results determined from the temperature dependence of the upper critical field. For percolative films in $H = 5\mathrm{T}$, we have found the strong $R_\square$ dependence of the prefactor $α_T$ in the expression$σ=[α_T e^2/(2π^2\hbar)]\ln T+σ_0$. The relation $α_T\propto1/R_\square$ can be explained qualitatively by a model of scaling law for percolation.

Conclusion: 尽管两种Nb₃Sn涂层在磁通流电阻率和钉扎机制上表现不同，但表面电阻相当，这揭示了超导薄膜优化需要在不同性能参数之间寻找平衡点。

Abstract: In this work, microwave measurements carried out in dielectric-loaded resonators exposed to high magnetic fields are exploited to yield the surface impedance of Nb$_3$Sn superconducting coatings deposited via two different techniques: vapor tin diffusion, and DC magnetron sputtering. The obtained data lead to qualitative interpretations on both the Nb$_3$Sn superconducting properties, and vortex-dynamics and pinning, of each coating separately, as well as simple distinctive features when comparing those. When examining the respective surface impedances at varying field, it is expected that the studied films perform at substantially diverse magnitudes of flux-flow resistivity, but also in well-differentiated pinning regimes, yet the obtained surface resistances of both samples are comparable, thus demonstrating that there is room for film optimization at the expense of certain compromise between the parameters involved.

### [12] [Axions at the meV Crossroads: Theory, Cosmology, Astrophysics, and Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18167)

Method: 本文采用综述方法，全面概述meV轴子在理论、宇宙学、天体物理和实验领域的现状。基于"meV质量轴子前沿：挑战与机遇"研讨会的讨论成果，系统梳理了当前研究进展和开放性问题。

Result: 综述涵盖了meV轴子的理论基础、宇宙学和天体物理特征，以及多样化的实验策略，包括日光望远镜（helioscopes）、晕望远镜（haloscopes）、准粒子系统和大型切伦科夫探测器等。这些方法的汇聚凸显了meV质量范围在未来轴子发现中的关键地位。

Conclusion: meV轴子被视为检验超越标准模型物理的关键探针，其研究领域的多学科融合强调了该质量范围在未来几年轴子发现中的核心作用。本文旨在概述当前研究努力、动机和社区的研究目标。

Abstract: The meV mass range has emerged as a focal point in axion physics, where advances in theory, cosmology, astrophysics, and experimental techniques converge. Axions in this mass range are theoretically well motivated, can arise in ultraviolet-complete models, and can have significant cosmological impacts as dark matter or dark radiation. In parallel, their efficient production in stellar and supernova environments provides powerful astrophysical probes. Here, we provide a comprehensive overview of meV axions across these domains, highlighting both established results and open questions. We discuss the theoretical underpinnings of meV axions, their cosmological and astrophysical signatures, and the diverse experimental strategies -- ranging from helioscopes and haloscopes to quasiparticle systems and large-volume Cherenkov detectors -- that aim to explore this regime. The convergence of these approaches emphasizes the pivotal role of the meV mass range for axion discovery in the coming years, identifying meV axions as a key probe for testing beyond-Standard-Model physics. This review document is the direct outcome of the discussions at the dedicated workshop "The meV Mass Axion Frontier: Challenges and Opportunities", held at Laboratori Nazionali di Frascati (IT) on 27--28 October 2025, and organized by the EU funded COST Action "Cosmic WISPers in the Dark Universe: Theory, astrophysics, and experiments" (CA21106, https://www.cost.eu/actions/CA21106). Its aim is to provide an overview of current efforts in meV axion research, their motivations, and the research goals that animate the community involved in this search.

### [13] [Higgs boson decay to massive bottom quarks at order $α_s^4$ induced by top-quark Yukawa couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18576)
*Jian Wang,Xing Wang,Yefan Wang*

TL;DR: 该研究计算了希格斯玻色子衰变为有质量底夸克过程中，由顶夸克汤川耦合诱导的次领头阶贡献，发现其对衰变宽度的修正达到0.4%，超过未来轻子对撞机的实验精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 希格斯玻色子衰变为有质量底夸克具有最大的分支比，但现有计算主要基于无质量底夸克近似。由顶夸克汤川耦合（top-quark Yukawa coupling）诱导的贡献从α_s^2阶开始，表现出对数和对数幂次增强，导致微扰展开收敛缓慢，需要更高阶计算。

Method: 计算了希格斯玻色子衰变为有质量底夸克过程中，包含两个顶夸克汤川耦合的平方振幅在α_s^4阶的贡献。该方法考虑了底夸克质量效应，而非传统的无质量近似。

Result: α_s^4阶的顶夸克汤川耦合贡献使衰变宽度相对于α_s^3阶结果增加0.4%，这一修正超过了未来轻子对撞机的实验精度。同时，该计算显著降低了尺度依赖性至0.4%。

Conclusion: 对于希格斯玻色子衰变为有质量底夸克的过程，包含顶夸克汤川耦合的α_s^4阶贡献具有重要物理意义，其修正效应在实验可探测范围内，且显著改善了理论预测的稳定性。

Abstract: The Higgs boson decay to massive bottom quarks has the largest branching ratio. The decay is mainly induced by the bottom-quark Yukawa coupling with the decay rate calculated up to $\mathcal{O}(α_s^4)$ assuming the massless final-state bottom quark. The top-quark Yukawa coupling induced contribution starts at $\mathcal{O}(α_s^2)$, and exhibits logarithmic and power enhancements, making the perturbative expansion converge slowly. We present a calculation of such contributions at $\mathcal{O}(α_s^4)$ to the decay into massive bottom quarks in which the squared amplitudes contain two top-quark Yukawa couplings. We find that they increase the decay width, relative to the result up to $\mathcal{O}(α_s^3)$, by $0.4\%$, larger than the experimental precision at future lepton colliders, and reduce the scale dependence significantly down to $0.4\%$.

### [14] [A Systematic Approach to Finite Multiloop Feynman Integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18691)
*Prasanna K. Dhani,Konstantinos Pyretzidis,Selomit Ramírez-Uribe,José Ríos-Sánchez,German F. R. Sborlini,Surabhi Tiwari,Germán Rodrigo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于圈-树对偶（Loop-Tree Duality, LTD）的系统性方法，用于识别和构造有限费曼积分（finite Feynman integrals），并通过引入广义积分集合来改善紫外（UV）区域的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限费曼积分因其优越的解析和数值性质，被认为是构建多圈计算中主积分（master integrals）基底的理想组件。然而，现有方法构造的积分在紫外（UV）区域常表现出快速增长的不良行为，需要改进。

Method: 本文利用圈-树对偶（LTD）在积分层次上清晰分离红外（infrared）和阈值（threshold）奇点的特性，提出了一种基于分子（numerator）和提升传播子（raised propagator）试探解（Ansätze）的新策略。进一步引入了在LTD框架内完全定义的广义积分集合。

Result: 新策略以更清晰、紧凑的方式获得了与其他方法相似的结果。更重要的是，新引入的广义积分集合本质上是红外有限的，且通常没有阈值奇点，为高阶计算提供了一个更通用的框架。

Conclusion: 圈-树对偶（LTD）是系统性识别有限积分的有效工具。通过引入广义积分集合，不仅保持了红外有限性，还显著改善了紫外（UV）行为，为高效的多圈计算提供了更优的基底构造方案。

Abstract: Finite Feynman integrals have been advocated as the optimal components for constructing a basis of master integrals in multiloop calculations, due to their improved analytic and numerical properties. In this paper, we show how the Loop-Tree Duality (LTD) is particularly well suited for systematically identifying finite integrals, as it makes the origin of infrared and threshold singularities fully transparent at the integrand level. This clear separation of singular and non-singular contributions enables a more efficient strategy for isolating and promoting finite integrals, thereby streamlining both reduction and numerical evaluation. We present a new strategy based on numerator and raised propagator Ansätze that provides results similar to other methods, although in a clearer and compact way. While this construction and other approaches establish a robust foundation, they often produce integrands that exhibit a rapid growth in the ultraviolet (UV) regime. To mitigate this bad UV behaviour, we introduce a generalized set of integrands fully defined within LTD. This new set is inherently infrared-finite and frequently free of threshold singularities, offering a more versatile framework for high-order calculations.

</details>


### [15] [Probing the Color-Octet Mechanism via Dihadron Fragmentation in $χ_b$ Decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18874)
*Zhi-Guo He,Guanghui Li,Yu-Jie Tian,Xin-Kai Wen,Bin Yan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出利用P波底偶素态χ_{b2}强子衰变中的Artru-Collins不对称性作为色八重态机制的直接探针，为提取色八重态与色单态矩阵元之比ρ_8提供了新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 色八重态（color-octet, CO）机制是非相对论量子色动力学（non-relativistic QCD）的基石，但其长程矩阵元（long-distance matrix elements）信息有限，阻碍了对该理论的严格检验。需要新的实验观测方法来直接探测色八重态动力学。

Method: 研究聚焦于P波底偶素态χ_{b2}的强子衰变中的Artru-Collins不对称性，该不对称性仅来源于色八重态衰变通道。通过分析Belle实验中的e^+e^-→Υ(2S)→γχ_{b2}过程，利用不对称束流构型在实验室系中保留该不对称性，避免了质心系中的强烈压低效应。

Result: Artru-Collins不对称性为色八重态机制提供了明确证据，因为色单态（color-singlet, CS）贡献仅影响非极化衰变率。该可观测量为提取色八重态与色单态矩阵元之比ρ_8提供了新途径，利用Belle II数据集可达到足够精度。

Conclusion: 该方法能够以足够精度确定ρ_8，有望解决格点计算（lattice calculations）与唯象确定（phenomenological determinations）之间长期存在的差异，为色八重态机制提供严格检验。

Abstract: The color-octet (CO) mechanism is a cornerstone of non-relativistic QCD, yet its long-distance matrix elements remain limited, preventing stringent tests of the theory. We demonstrate that the Artru-Collins asymmetry in hadronic decays of the $P$-wave bottomonium state $χ_{b2}$ provides a direct probe of CO dynamics. The asymmetry arises exclusively from the CO decay channel, whereas the color-singlet (CS) contribution affects only the unpolarized rate, so that a nonzero signal constitutes unambiguous evidence of the CO mechanism. This observable provides a novel way to extract the ratio $ρ_8$ between CO and CS matrix elements. Focusing on $e^+e^-\toΥ(2S)\toγ\,χ_{b2}$ at Belle, we show that the asymmetric beam configuration preserves the asymmetry in the laboratory frame and avoids the strong suppression present in the center-of-mass frame. With the Belle II dataset, $ρ_8$ could be determined with sufficient precision to address the long-standing discrepancy between the lattice calculations and phenomenological determinations.

</details>


### [16] [Transverse spin effects and light-quark dipole moments at colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18951)
*Xin-Kai Wen,Bin Yan,Zhite Yu,C. -P. Yuan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究提出在电子-离子对撞机和轻子对撞机上，通过测量双强子方位角不对称性来探测轻夸克偶极相互作用的新方法，该方法能显著提高现有约束1-2个数量级，并能分离上下夸克偶极矩及其实部和虚部。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索轻夸克偶极相互作用（light-quark dipole interactions）的新探测方法，以增强对超出标准模型物理的约束能力。当前方法存在局限性，需要更精确、更灵敏的探测手段来研究高能物理中的新物理效应。

Method: 研究方法包括：(1) 在电子-离子对撞机（Electron-Ion Collider）上，测量非极化质子靶半单举深度非弹性轻子散射中双强子的方位角不对称性；(2) 在轻子对撞机上，利用与额外强子$h^\prime$伴随产生的双强子$(h_1 h_2)$的方位角不对称性。

Result: 这些方位角不对称性（azimuthal asymmetries）能够独特地观测横向极化夸克，它们源于量子干涉效应，并且在新物理能标的主导阶次上对偶极相互作用具有排他性敏感度。因此，它们表现出对偶极耦合的线性依赖，不受其他新物理效应的污染。

Conclusion: 该方法有望将现有约束提高1-2个数量级，通过结合所有可能的$h^\prime$通道，能够分离上下夸克偶极矩。通过控制电子纵向极化和质心能量，可以分离光子与弱玻色子介导的贡献，同时确定偶极耦合的实部和虚部，为研究高能$CP$破坏效应提供了新途径。

Abstract: In this talk, we present novel methods to investigate light-quark dipole interactions at colliders. Our approach includes: (1) measuring azimuthal asymmetries of a collinear dihadron in semi-inclusive deep inelastic lepton scattering off an unpolarized proton target at the Electron-Ion Collider, and (2) utilizing azimuthal asymmetries of dihadron $(h_1 h_2)$ produced in association with an additional hadron $h^\prime$ at lepton colliders. These asymmetries provide a unique means to observe transversely polarized quarks, which arise from quantum interference and are exclusively sensitive to dipole interactions at the leading power of the new physics scale. Consequently, they exhibit a linear dependence on the dipole couplings, free from contamination by other new physics effects. This approach has the potential to significantly strengthen current constraints by one to two orders of magnitude. By combining all possible channels of $h^\prime$, this novel approach enables the disentanglement of the up- and down-quark dipole moments. Additionally, by controlling the electron's longitudinal polarization and the center-of-mass energy, it separates the contributions mediated by photon and weak boson. Furthermore, it allows for a simultaneous determination of both real and imaginary parts of the dipole couplings, offering a new avenue for investigating potential $CP$-violating effects at high energies.

</details>


### [17] [The impact of prescriptions in phenomenological extractions of Transverse Momentum Dependent distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19088)
*Matteo Cerutti,Andrea Simonelli*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了Collins-Soper-Sterman（CSS）方法中唯象处理对横向动量分布（TMDs）全局提取的影响，发现不同的$b_*$处理方式在低能Drell-Yan数据拟合中表现相似，但在中间横向动量区域产生显著差异，影响高能Drell-Yan过程预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨CSS方法中唯象处理（phenomenological prescriptions）对横向动量分布（Transverse Momentum Distributions, TMDs）全局提取的影响，特别是$b_*$处理方式带来的理论不确定性。

Method: 采用CSS框架对低能Drell-Yan数据进行拟合，比较不同$b_*$处理方式（$b_*$ prescription）对TMD提取的影响，并分析其对不同能量尺度数据的预测能力。

Result: 结果显示不同$b_*$处理方式在低能Drell-Yan数据拟合中都能获得良好一致性，且在小部分子横向动量区域产生相似的TMDs；但在中间横向动量区域出现显著差异，严重影响高能Drell-Yan过程的预测。

Conclusion: $b_*$处理方式代表了CSS方法中固有的理论不确定性来源，对TMD提取及其解释引入系统性影响；同时强调了不同能量尺度数据在评估CSS框架中唯象处理效果时的相互作用。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of phenomenological prescriptions in the Collins-Soper-Sterman (CSS) approach for global extractions of Transverse Momentum Distributions (TMDs). We show that fits to low-energy Drell-Yan data with different choices of $b_*$ prescription yield equally good agreement with data and similar TMDs at small partonic transverse momentum. In contrast, sizable differences emerge at intermediate transverse momentum region, significantly affecting the predictions for high-energy Drell-Yan processes. Our results demonstrate that the $b_*$ prescription represents an intrinsic source of theoretical uncertainty in the CSS approach, introducing systematic effects that influence TMD extractions and their interpretation. At the same time, our analysis emphasizes the interplay between data at different energy scales in assessing the effect of phenomenological prescriptions in TMD fits adopting the CSS framework.

### [18] [Hidden-charm pentaquarks: Electromagnetic structure in a diquark--diquark--antiquark model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19151)
*U. Ozdem*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究系统分析了隐粲五夸克态（hidden-charm pentaquark states）的磁偶极矩（magnetic dipole moments），采用QCD光锥求和规则（QCD light-cone sum rules）与四种不同内插流（interpolating currents），发现磁矩对内部夸克构型与自旋排列高度敏感，可作为区分不同结构模型的有效探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于系统探究内部结构尚不确定的奇特态（exotic states）的电磁性质，特别是隐粲五夸克态。由于不同模型对这些态的结构提出了不同解释，需要通过电磁观测量来区分竞争的结构模型。

Method: 研究方法采用QCD光锥求和规则，并构建了四种不同的内插流。分析同时考虑了轻夸克与粲夸克（charm quark）部分的贡献，以及高维算符（higher-dimensional operators）的影响，确保了算符乘积展开（operator product expansion）的收敛性与基态极点（ground-state pole）的主导性。

Result: 结果显示，磁矩对内部夸克构型与自旋排列（spin alignments）具有强烈依赖性。尽管夸克成分与量子数相同，不同内插流得到的磁矩值存在显著差异。与现有研究比较表明，分子型（molecular-type）预测基本一致，而紧致构型（compact configurations）则给出明显不同的值，包括符号与量级的显著差异。

Conclusion: 结论强调电磁观测量对奇特强子（exotic hadrons）内部结构的高度敏感性，凸显了其作为探针在区分自旋宇称（spin-parity assignments）分配和底层夸克动力学（underlying quark dynamics）的竞争结构模型方面的潜力。

Abstract: We systematically investigate the electromagnetic properties of exotic states whose internal structures remain uncertain and for which different models have been proposed. In this work, we focus on the magnetic dipole moments of hidden-charm pentaquark states using QCD light-cone sum rules with four distinct interpolating currents. The analysis accounts for contributions from both light and charm quark sectors, as well as higher-dimensional operators, ensuring convergence of the operator product expansion and dominance of the ground-state pole. Our results demonstrate a strong dependence of the magnetic moments on the internal quark configurations and spin alignments, revealing substantial variations among the different currents despite identical quark content and quantum numbers. Comparisons with existing studies indicate that while molecular-type predictions show general agreement, compact configurations yield markedly different values, including significant differences in sign and magnitude. These findings therefore underscore the sensitivity of electromagnetic observables to the internal structure of exotic hadrons and highlight their potential as probes to discriminate between competing structural models for spin-parity assignments and underlying quark dynamics.

### [19] [A global analysis of Energy-Energy Correlation data: determination of $α_S$ and non-perturbative QCD parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19162)
*Ugo Giuseppe Aglietti,Giancarlo Ferrera,Lorenzo Rossi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文对电子-正电子湮灭为强子的能量-能量关联（EEC）数据进行了全面的全局分析，涵盖了7.7-91.2 GeV的质心能量范围。通过将N³LL精度的对数增强贡献与α_S³阶固定阶计算相匹配，并结合重夸克质量效应和非微扰修正，实现了对实验数据的精确描述，并测得了强耦合常数α_S(m_Z²)=0.119±0.002。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在通过分析电子-正电子湮灭为强子的能量-能量关联（Energy-Energy Correlation, EEC）数据，精确测定量子色动力学（QCD）中的强耦合常数（strong coupling constant）α_S。研究覆盖了7.7-91.2 GeV的宽能量范围，首次在全局拟合中包含了ALEPH和AMY合作组的数据集。

Method: 在背对背（back-to-back）双喷注区域，将对数增强贡献重求和（resum）至次次次领头对数（next-to-next-to-next-to-leading logarithmic, N³LL）精度。重求和结果与α_S³阶固定阶计算（fixed-order calculations）一致匹配。重求和形式还包含了主导的重夸克质量效应（heavy-quark mass effects），并通过解析色散方法（analytic dispersive approach）建模非微扰幂次修正（non-perturbative power corrections）。

Result: 同时拟合（simultaneous fit）在所有能量范围内对实验数据提供了极佳的描述，实现了对强耦合常数α_S(m_Z²)=0.119±0.002的精确测定。同时确定了非微扰参数（non-perturbative parameters），包括表征Collins-Soper演化核（Collins-Soper evolution kernel）的参数。

Conclusion: 本研究通过全面的全局分析，结合高精度重求和与固定阶计算，成功描述了宽能量范围内的EEC数据，为强耦合常数和非微扰参数提供了精确的测定结果。首次在全局拟合中包含ALEPH和AMY数据集增强了分析的可靠性。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive global analysis of Energy-Energy Correlation (EEC) data in electron-positron annihilation into hadrons, spanning a wide range of center-of-mass energies ($7.7\,\,\text{GeV}\!\leq\!\sqrt{s}\!\leq\! 91.2\,\,\text{GeV})$. In the back-to-back (two-jet) region, we resum to all orders the logarithmically-enhanced contributions up to next-to-next-to-next-to-leading logarithmic (N$^3$LL) accuracy. The resummed results are consistently matched to fixed-order calculations up to $\mathcal{O}(α_S^3)$. Our resummation formalism also incorporates dominant heavy-quark mass effects and models non-perturbative power corrections by means of an analytic dispersive approach. A simultaneous fit yields an excellent description of experimental data across all energies, enabling a precise determination of the strong coupling, $α_S(m_Z^2) = 0.119 \pm 0.002$, as well as the non-perturbative parameters, including those characterizing the Collins--Soper evolution kernel. Our analysis includes, for the first time in a global fit, datasets from the ALEPH and AMY collaborations.

Abstract: We explore the idea of quark-lepton unification at low energies. In particular, we discuss the minimal framework for matter unification at the multi-TeV scale, in which neutrino masses are necessarily generated via the inverse seesaw mechanism. To assess the testability of this theory for physics beyond the Standard Model, we analyze current experimental constraints and derive the corresponding lower bound on the symmetry breaking scale. We reexamine the impact of existing limits from lepton number violating meson decays, taking into account the freedom associated with unknown quark-lepton mixing angles. Furthermore, we study the correlation between bounds from meson decays and $μ\to e$ conversion. In our framework, the LSV parameters are introduced as members of a non-dynamical superfield. As a consequence, we show that naturally there appears a mixing term between the gauge boson and the gaugino, which can be readily seen in the superspace/superfield approach. Bounds on the strength of the fermionic LSV background are can be set by invoking the energy loss argument and the solar data we adopt.

### [23] [Formation and Decay of Oscillons in Einstein-Cartan Higgs Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19178)

Method: 论文采用综述分析方法，整合近期关于希格斯场在暴胀结束后非平衡演化的研究。该演化由快子不稳定性（tachyonic instabilities）和非线性自相互作用驱动，导致暴胀子凝聚体（inflaton condensate）碎裂并形成局域化的振荡子构型。

Result: 早期研究表明可能形成长寿命振荡子并导致延长的物质主导阶段，但近期分析显示小场值下的自相互作用使这些结构具有瞬态性，最终触发其衰变并开启辐射主导阶段。这一动力学过程对宇宙热历史、暴胀可观测量和随机引力波（stochastic gravitational waves）的产生具有重要影响。

Conclusion: 爱因斯坦-嘉当框架下的希格斯暴胀预加热阶段涉及复杂的非平衡动力学，其中瞬态振荡子的形成与衰变是关键特征。这一过程决定了从暴胀结束到辐射主导的过渡，并对宇宙学观测信号（如引力波）产生可观测的后果。

Abstract: We review recent progress in the understanding of the preheating stage of Higgs inflation formulated within the Einstein-Cartan framework of gravity. This setup smoothly interpolates between the metric and Palatini formulations of the theory, leading to a distinctive phenomenology in an intermediate regime. Following the end of inflation, the Higgs field undergoes a non-trivial out-of-equilibrium evolution driven by tachyonic instabilities and nonlinear self-interactions, which fragment the inflaton condensate and give rise to well-localized oscillon configurations. While early studies suggested the formation of long-lived oscillons and the possibility of an extended matter-dominated phase, more recent analyses show that self-interactions at small field values render these objects transient, eventually triggering their decay and the onset of radiation domination. We discuss the implications of this dynamics for the thermal history of the Universe, the inflationary observables, and the generation of stochastic gravitational waves.

Motivation: 研究动机在于探索标准模型中尺度不变性最小非线性实现的宇宙学后果。该框架旨在为普朗克尺度与电弱尺度之间的巨大层级（hierarchy）提供技术性自然（technically natural）解释，同时仅引入最少的额外场——一个轻的伸缩子场。

Method: 研究方法基于标准模型中尺度不变性的最小非线性实现框架。该框架在SM粒子之外仅引入了一个轻的、微弱耦合的伸缩子场。研究使用简化近似（simplified approximations）详细探讨了该模型的宇宙学后果。

Result: 研究发现，该模型的宇宙学后果与最小标准模型（minimal SM）存在显著差异。电弱希格斯场（electroweak Higgs field）在宇宙冷却到极低温度（约28 MeV）前，一直被困在对称相（symmetric phase）中。此时，一阶QCD手征对称性破缺相变（first-order QCD chiral symmetry-breaking phase transition）触发电弱相变（electroweak phase transition）。

Conclusion: 该模型为原初黑洞（primordial black holes）、低频引力波（low-frequency gravitational waves）以及多夸克和轻子块（multi-quark and lepton nuggets）的产生提供了有趣的可能性。尽管在低能下与最小标准模型几乎无法区分，但其宇宙学后果却截然不同。

Abstract: We study the cosmological implications of the minimal non-linear realisation of scale invariance within the Standard Model (SM). This framework provides a technically natural explanation for the hierarchy between the Planck scale and the electroweak scale and introduces only a light, feebly coupled dilaton field beyond the SM particles. Although the model is almost indistinguishable from the minimal SM at low energies, its cosmological consequences differ dramatically. In particular, the electroweak Higgs field remains trapped in the symmetric phase until the Universe cools to very low temperatures, $T_c^{(χ)}\sim 28$ MeV, where the first-order QCD chiral symmetry-breaking phase transition triggers the electroweak phase transition. This scenario offers intriguing possibilities for the production of primordial black holes, low-frequency gravitational waves, and multi-quark and lepton nuggets, which we explore in some detail using simplified approximations.

</details>


### [25] [Cosmological Implications of the Slingshot Effect: Gravitational Waves, Primordial Black Holes and Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18512)
*Maximilian Bachmaier,Gia Dvali,Juan Sebastián Valbuena-Bermúdez,Michael Zantedeschi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了"弹弓效应（slingshot effect）"这一普遍现象，即局域源（如单极子、夸克或D膜）穿越分隔禁闭相（希格斯相）和非禁闭相（库仑相）的畴壁时，会伴随产生束缚源的拉伸"弦"。该效应在多种物理场景中出现，并可能产生引力波、暗物质和原初黑洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探索弹弓效应（slingshot effect）这一普遍物理现象的含义。该效应发生在局域源（如单极子（monopole）、夸克或D膜（D-brane））穿越分隔禁闭相（希格斯相（Higgsed））和非禁闭相（库仑相（Coulomb））的畴壁（domain wall）时。

Method: 研究采用理论分析方法，探讨弹弓效应在不同物理设置下的表现。这些设置包括导致禁闭（confinement）的相变（phase transitions）（包括电性和磁性），以及弦理论（string theoretic）中涉及D膜的暴胀（inflation）场景。

Result: 研究发现弹弓效应伴随产生适当维度的拉伸"弦"（stretched "string"），将源束缚在畴壁上。该现象在产生引力波（gravitational waves）和以卡鲁扎-克莱因引力子（Kaluza-Klein gravitons）形式存在的暗物质（dark matter）方面具有重要作用。

Conclusion: 弹弓效应可导致在观测上感兴趣的暗物质和高能宇宙射线（high-energy cosmic rays）质量范围内形成原初黑洞（primordial black holes）。该效应为理解多种物理现象提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: In this paper, we explore the implications of the so-called slingshot effect. It represents a rather general phenomenon occurring when a localized source, such as a monopole, quark, or a $D$-brane, crosses a domain wall separating the confined (Higgsed) and unconfined (Coulomb) phases of the crossing source. The crossover is accompanied by a stretched ``string'' of proper co-dimensionality that confines the source to the domain wall. The effect takes place for different setups, such as phase transitions leading to confinement, both electric and magnetic, as well as in string theoretic inflation with $D$-branes. We discuss the role of the phenomenon in sourcing gravitational waves and dark matter in the form of Kaluza-Klein gravitons. We also show that the slingshot effect can lead to the formation of primordial black holes in observationally interesting mass ranges for dark matter and high-energy cosmic rays.

</details>


### [26] [From N- to (p,N)- Inflationary Attractors in view of ACT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18826)
*C. Pallis*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文回顾了两种分数型Kähler势，它们在暴胀路径上简化为特定形式，并与混沌暴胀势共存于非线性σ模型中，形成一类(p,N)-暴胀吸引子，其可观测量与ACT DR6数据兼容。这些模型可在超引力框架下实现，使用两个手征超场和单项式超势，并引入平移对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在研究分数型Kähler势（fractional Kähler potentials）在暴胀模型中的应用，特别是探索这些势函数如何与混沌暴胀势（chaotic inflationary potentials）在非线性σ模型（non-linear sigma model）中共存，并产生与观测数据兼容的暴胀吸引子。

Method: 方法包括回顾两种分数型Kähler势，它们在暴胀路径上简化为$N/(1-φ^{q_{\rm M}})^{p}$形式，其中$q_{\rm M}=1$或$2$，$0.1\leq p\leq10$。将这些势与混沌暴胀势$φ^n$（$n=2$或$4$）结合在非线性σ模型中，形成(p,N)-暴胀吸引子。在超引力（supergravity）框架下，通过引入两个手征超场（chiral superfields）、单项式超势（monomial superpotential）以及平移对称性（shift symmetry）来实现这些模型。

Result: 研究确定了与$q_{\rm M}$和$n$无关的一类(p,N)-暴胀吸引子，其可观测量（observables）与ACT DR6数据兼容。虽然暴胀发生在亚普朗克尺度（subplanckian）的暴胀子值域，但对于某些$N$值，张量-标量比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）可能在不久的将来被观测到。

Conclusion: 分数型Kähler势与混沌暴胀势在非线性σ模型中的共存产生了一类具有观测兼容性的暴胀吸引子。这些模型可在超引力框架下实现，且某些参数下的张量-标量比具有未来可观测的潜力，为暴胀模型构建提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We review two types of fractional Kaehler potentials $K$ which reduce, along the inflationary path, to the form $N/(1-φ^{q_{\rm M}})^{p}$ with $q_{\rm M}=1$ or $2$ and $0.1\leq p\leq10$. Their coexistence, within a non-linear sigma model, with chaotic inflationary potentials of the form $φ^n$ (where $n=2$ or $4$) determines, independently from $q_{\rm M}$ and $n$, a class of $(p,N)$-inflationary attractors which leads to observables compatible with the ACT DR6. An implementation of these models in the context of supergravity can be also achieved by introducing two chiral superfields and a monomial superpotential, linear with respect to the inflaton-accompanying field, and supplementing the $K$'s above with a shift symmetry. Although inflation is attained for subplanckian inflaton values, the tensor-to-scalar ratio obtained for certain $N$ values can be possibly observable in the near future.

### [27] [Statistical Mechanics of Random Hyperbolic Graphs within the Fermionic Maximum-Entropy Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18170)
*M. Ángeles Serrano*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文回顾并整合了双曲随机图（hyperbolic random graph）在统计力学框架下的推导，将其置于复杂网络最大熵原理（maximum-entropy principle）的广泛框架中，为网络结构分析提供了理论基础和分析工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然和人造系统中元素间的复杂关系形成多尺度交互网络，这些网络具有共同的基本结构特性。双曲空间网络模型家族是解释这些特性的最先进框架之一，但相关推导分散在不同文献中，需要系统整合。

Method: 在统计力学框架下，通过最大化图集合的吉布斯熵（Gibbs entropy）并施加观测约束来推导模型，其中网络链接表现为费米子（fermionic particles）。本文回顾并补充了这些分散的推导。

Result: 将双曲随机图置于复杂网络统计力学最大熵原理的广泛框架中，提供了对核心网络特性的最小偏差预测。建立了分析网络结构的原则性框架，为理论和实证研究提供了新视角和强大分析工具。

Conclusion: 双曲随机图模型在最大熵原理框架下得到了系统整合，这一方法为网络结构分析提供了理论基础，能够预测网络的基本结构特性，并为理论和实证研究提供了新的分析视角。

Abstract: The intricate relations between elements in natural and human-made systems sustain the complex processes that shape our world, forming multiscale networks of interactions. These networks can be represented as graphs composed of nodes connected by links and, regardless of their domain, they share a set of fundamental structural properties. The family of network models in hyperbolic space constitutes one of the most advanced frameworks accounting for such properties, including sparsity, the small-world property, heterogeneity and hierarchical organization, high clustering, and scale invariance under network renormalization transformations. These geometric models also exhibit other intriguing phenomena, such as an anomalous, temperature-dependent phase transition between a geometric and a non-geometric phase. In simple graph representations, where network links are unweighted, the model can be derived within a statistical-mechanics framework by maximizing the Gibbs entropy of the graph ensemble subject to constraints imposed by observations, with links effectively behaving as fermionic particles. In this topical review, I revisit these derivations previously scattered across different sources and complement them, in order to properly contextualize and consolidate hyperbolic random graphs within the broad framework of the maximum-entropy principle in the statistical mechanics of complex networks. The approach presented here represents the least-biased prediction of the fundamental set of core network properties and establishes a principled framework for analyzing network structure, offering new perspectives and powerful analytical tools for both theoretical and empirical studies.

</details>

Result: 证明了与特征值相关的拓扑不变量变化恰好对应于特征向量从非厄米趋肤效应到安德森局域化的交叉转变，为局域化行为建立了普适性判据。

Abstract: We illuminate the fundamental mechanism responsible for the transition between the non-Hermitian skin effect and defect-induced Anderson localization in the bulk via the study of Lyapunov exponents.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Phase transitions in a modified Nishimori model, including the model considered by Kitatani, on a two-dimensional square lattice are investigated using a tensor-network-based sampling scheme. The results provide clear numerical evidence that the spin-glass and ferromagnetic transitions are separated on the Nishimori line, supporting the existence of an intermediate Mattis-like spin-glass phase. This finding is consistent with the reentrant transition numerically observed in the two-dimensional Edwards-Anderson (EA) model. Furthermore, critical exponents estimated via finite-size-scaling analysis indicate that the universality class of the transitions differs from that of the standard independent and identically distributed EA model.

### [30] [When do real observers resolve de Sitter's imaginary problem?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18068)
*Ahmed Farag Ali*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了de Sitter路径积分中的普遍相位如何阻碍Gibbons-Hawking熵的态计数解释，并确定了能够重组该相位的"真实观测者"所需满足的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: de Sitter路径积分中的普遍相位$\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$阻碍了对Gibbons-Hawking熵的态计数（state-counting）解释。基于Maldacena关于特定黑洞观测者可以重组该相位的提议，需要确定此类"真实观测者"能够成功的一般约束条件。

Method: 通过区分引力观测者（gravitational observers）与拓扑旁观者（topological spectators），分析在de Sitter鞍点处红外有效作用量（infrared effective action）与度规无关的扇区。使用禁闭SU(3)规范理论和拓扑序（topological orders）作为具体示例进行论证。

Result: 研究发现，任何在de Sitter鞍点处红外有效作用量与度规无关的扇区都会在路径积分中因子化：$\Ztot = \Zgrav^{(\text{obs})}\Ztop$，导致虚相位持续存在。信息承载时钟是必要条件但不足够：只有其涨落与共形因子（conformal factor）的负模式共享的观测者属于能够移除de Sitter相位的特殊类别。

Conclusion: 仅当观测者的涨落与共形因子的负模式共享时，才能成功重组de Sitter路径积分中的普遍相位，从而实现对Gibbons-Hawking熵的态计数解释。信息处理能力本身不足以确保相位移除。

Abstract: The universal phase $\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$ of the Euclidean de Sitter path integral obstructs a straightforward state-counting interpretation of the Gibbons--Hawking entropy. Building on Maldacena's proposal that specific black-hole observers can reorganize this phase, we derive a general constraint on when such ``real observers'' can succeed. By distinguishing \emph{gravitational observers} from \emph{topological spectators}, we show that any sector whose \emph{infrared effective} action is metric independent at the de Sitter saddle factorizes in the path integral, $\Ztot = \Zgrav^{(\text{obs})}\Ztop$, so the imaginary phase persists regardless of the sector's information-processing capabilities. Using confining $\SU(3)$ gauge theory and topological orders as examples, we demonstrate that an information-bearing clock is necessary but insufficient: only observers whose fluctuations share the negative modes of the conformal factor belong to the special class that can remove the de Sitter phase.

</details>


### [31] [End-of-the-World Singularities: The Good, the Bad, and the Heated-up](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18133)
*José Calderón-Infante,Gongrui Cheng,Alvaro Herráez,Thomas Van Riet*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了驱动标量场在模空间（moduli space）中趋于无限距离的余维一（codimension-one）世界终结曲率奇点（End-of-the-World curvature singularities），并基于多个判据评估其物理可接受性。研究提出了一种新的几何化判据，该判据能容纳EFT弦（EFT strings）和D7膜（D7-branes），同时拒绝了IIA型强耦合奇点。此外，研究还探讨了具有近极端视界（near-extremal horizon）推广的流（flows），并提出了关于场空间距离与温度关系的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在重新评估在动力学边界（dynamical cobordisms）背景下出现的余维一世界终结曲率奇点的物理可接受性。这些奇点驱动标量场在模空间中趋于无限距离，其命运与奇点附近所探测的无限距离极限（infinite-distance limit）紧密相关。

Method: 研究采用并扩展了多个已有的物理奇点判据，包括Gubser的视界判据（horizon criterion）和势判据（potential criterion），以及Maldacena-Nuñez判据（Maldacena-Nuñez criterion）。通过分析具体的弦理论实现（如Klebanov-Tseytlin和Klebanov-Strassler解），并受动力学边界启发，提出了一种新的几何化判据，该判据通过限制里奇标量（Ricci scalar）在场空间趋于无限距离时的发散来评估奇点。

Result: 模空间流（moduli-space flows）不满足Gubser的视界判据，但满足其势判据，并在代表性弦实现中满足十维的Maldacena-Nuñez判据。EFT弦和D7膜虽然具有合理的紫外完备性（UV completion），却未能通过Gubser的势判据。新提出的几何化判据则能容纳这些例子，同时拒绝了IIA型强耦合世界终结奇点（massive Type IIA strong coupling End-of-the-World singularity）。对于可推广至近极端视界的黑Dp膜（black Dp-branes），研究发现温度与场空间距离之间存在指数关系。

Conclusion: 研究表明，某些驱动场空间无限距离的余维一奇点可能具有物理意义，不应被简单摒弃。新提出的几何化判据比Gubser判据更具包容性，为评估此类奇点提供了新视角。温度与场空间距离的指数关系暗示了动力学边界背景下距离猜想（Distance Conjecture）可能存在有限温度扩展（finite-temperature extension）。

Abstract: We revisit codimension-one End-of-the-World curvature singularities that drive scalars to infinite distance in field-space and have appeared in the context of dynamical cobordisms. We confront them with Gubser's horizon and potential criteria and with the Maldacena--Nuñez criterion. Moduli-space flows do not admit a near-extremal horizon generalization. Still, they satisfy Gubser's potential criterion and, in representative string realizations, the Maldacena--Nuñez criterion in ten dimensions. Together with an explicit uplift of this type of solution to a consistent string theory background, this suggests that such singularities should not be discarded. For flows with non-trivial scalar potential, we argue that the fate of the singularity is tied to the infinite-distance limit probed near the singularity. The Klebanov--Tseytlin and Klebanov--Strassler solutions illustrate that a modification that obstructs or modifies the field excursion should not be understood as a UV-resolution of the original singularity. We show that EFT strings and D7-branes fail Gubser's potential criterion despite having a sensible UV completion. Motivated by this, and inspired by dynamical cobordisms, we propose a novel criterion that bounds the divergence of the Ricci scalar as the flow explores infinite distance in field-space. Our criterion can be viewed as a geometrization Gubser's one that, while capturing all examples accepted by the latter, also admits EFT strings and D7-branes. Both criteria reject the massive Type IIA strong coupling End-of-the-World singularity. Finally, we analyze black D$p$-branes reduced to codimension one as representatives of flows that admit near-extremal generalizations, and find an exponential relation between temperature and field-space distance. This suggests a finite-temperature extension of the Distance Conjecture for dynamical cobordisms.

</details>


### [32] [The Resolved Elliptic Genus and the D1-D5 CFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18138)
*Marcel R. R. Hughes,Masaki Shigemori*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在arXiv:2509.19425基础上扩展，为T^4上的D1-D5共形场论引入新的超对称指数——解析椭圆亏格（REG），作为标准修正椭圆亏格（MEG）的单参数推广。新形式体系基于Schur-Weyl对偶，在黑洞阈值以下展示了CFT与超引力的精确对应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准修正椭圆亏格（MEG）在黑洞阈值以下的物理区域基本平凡，无法有效描述该区域的CFT-超引力对应。需要发展新的超对称指数来揭示低于黑洞阈值的微观结构，并为理解黑洞微观态提供新工具。

Method: 基于Schur-Weyl对偶发展新形式体系，将对称轨道（symmetric orbifold）CFT的希尔伯特空间分解为对称性扇区。通过研究由精确边际算符形变的超荷在相关对称代数上的作用，提出支配BPS态提升过程的超选择规则，并据此构造解析椭圆亏格（REG）。

Result: 解析椭圆亏格（REG）在黑洞阈值以下展示了CFT与超引力的详细对应，而MEG在该区域基本平凡。在阈值以上，REG由黑洞微观态主导，这些态分布在MEG无法探测的多个不同扇区中。

Conclusion: 新形式体系和解析椭圆亏格（REG）为研究黑洞微观态结构提供了有用工具，可能对理解CFT中黑洞微观态的"fortuity program"具有相关性。REG作为MEG的单参数推广，能够揭示标准指数无法探测的物理信息。

Abstract: This paper is a follow-up to the short paper arXiv:2509.19425, greatly expanding the discussion with examples and providing derivations and justifications of results presented there.
  We introduce a new supersymmetry index for the D1-D5 CFT on $T^4$, which we call the resolved elliptic genus (REG). It is a one-parameter generalisation of the standard supersymmetry index, the modified elliptic genus (MEG), and arises naturally in the free symmetric orbifold description of the theory within a new formalism, based on Schur-Weyl duality, that we develop. In this formalism, the Hilbert space of the symmetric orbifold CFT is decomposed into symmetry sectors in which the structure of the states contributing to the MEG is transparent. By examining the action of the supercharge deformed by an exactly marginal operator on the relevant symmetry algebra, we propose a superselection rule governing the lifting process of BPS states, and use it to construct the REG by summing only over those symmetry sectors that can mix according to this rule. The REG exhibits detailed agreement between the CFT and supergravity below the black-hole threshold, a regime in which the MEG is essentially trivial. Above the threshold, the REG is dominated by black-hole microstates, which are now distributed amongst distinct sectors that are invisible to the MEG. We expect both the new formalism and the REG to provide useful new tools for studying the structure of black-hole microstates. In particular, we comment on their possible relevance to the fortuity program for understanding black-hole microstates within CFT.

</details>


### [33] [Moments in the CFT Landscape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18140)
*Li-Yuan Chiang,David Poland,Gordon Rogelberg*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新颖的数值自举（numerical bootstrap）方法，通过定义在共形数据上的加权平均矩可观测量（moment observables），为幺正、交叉对称的共形场论（conformal field theories）提供全局粗粒度谱探测框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数值自举方法在探索共形场论（conformal field theories）的某些区域存在困难，需要开发新的框架来揭示难以通过传统方法访问的自举解和集体结构。

Method: 该方法基于矩可观测量（moment observables）——在共形数据上的加权平均，利用标准半正定规划（semidefinite programming）技术对算符分布提供数值严格界限，形成矩自举（moment bootstrap）框架。

Result: 在重关联子（heavy correlator）区域，界限保持稳健并快速收敛于解析推导的幂律；有限外维度下，低阶矩捕获对解析重极限结果的修正。矩自举揭示了自举景观（bootstrap landscape）中先前未探索区域的新特征，包括在2<d<6范围内持续存在的两个连续尖点族（continuous families of kinks）。

Conclusion: 矩变量（moment variables）能够揭示传统数值方法难以访问的自举解和集体结构，这些尖点族反映了与底层算符退耦现象（operator decoupling phenomena）相关的非平凡谱重组。

Abstract: We develop a novel numerical bootstrap for unitary, crossing-symmetric conformal field theories, focusing on moment observables defined as weighted averages over conformal data. Providing a global and coarse-grained probe of the operator spectrum, this framework yields numerically rigorous bounds on the operator distribution using standard semidefinite programming techniques. In the heavy correlator regime, these bounds remain robust and converge rapidly towards analytically-derived power laws. At finite external dimensions, low-lying moments capture corrections to analytic heavy limit results, while reproducing familiar bootstrap solutions such as Ising-model kinks on the boundary of moment space. Most importantly, the moment bootstrap reveals new features in previously unexplored regions of the bootstrap landscape. The lower bounds on moment variables exhibit two continuous families of kinks persisting across $2 < d < 6$, reflecting nontrivial spectral reorganizations connected to underlying operator decoupling phenomena. These results demonstrate that moment variables uncover bootstrap solutions and collective structures that are difficult to access within traditional numerical approaches.

</details>

Abstract: We study ${\cal N}=4$ super Yang-Mills theory compactified on a circle at zero temperature, with VEVs for two scalar bilinears and three independent current sources. The current sources correspond in (2+1) dimensions to Q-ball charge densities for $U(1)^3\subset SO(6)_R$, and are geometrically realized as twists along three angular directions of the $S^5$. We further show that such theories admit stealth black hole solutions, and we recover weak gravitational potentials, thus passing the solar system experiments. ### [37] [A menagerie of Schwarzians: coadjoint orbits of Virasoro and near-dS$_2$ quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18154)
*Henry Maxfield*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分类所有Virasoro共伴随轨道，这些轨道与恒定正曲率二维洛伦兹几何的模空间（moduli space）一致。理论定义涉及振荡路径积分，并考虑变化"耦合函数"（重整化伸缩子），同时处理一阶涨落算符非本质自伴性带来的模糊性。

Result: 成功分类并求解了所有可能的广义Schwarzian理论，包括具有新颖特征的洛伦兹理论。路径积分通过费米子局域化（fermionic localisation）保持一阶精确，但需要超越Duistermaat-Heckman定理的额外输入。实现了对所有理论和所有耦合的精确路径积分计算。

Abstract: The Schwarzian theory, which governs the universal low-energy dynamics of near-extremal black holes and the SYK model, can be characterised as an integral over a particular coadjoint orbit of the Virasoro group. We describe and solve a complete classification of all possible generalised Schwarzian theories, defined by integrals over any Virasoro coadjoint orbit, including new classes of theories with qualitatively novel features. The classification of coadjoint orbits coincides with the moduli space of constant positive curvature two-dimensional Lorentzian geometries, and the associated Schwarzian theories govern associated wavefunctions in asymptotically near-dS$_2$ gravity (Jackiw-Teitelboim gravity in particular). The novel theories are inherently Lorentzian, defined by oscillatory path integrals weighted by $e^{iI}$ and force consideration of varying `coupling functions' (renormalised dilaton) which may not have definite sign. The definition of the theories involves an ambiguity, arising because the operator describing quadratic fluctuations at one loop fails to be essentially self-adjoint. This requires a choice of boundary condition, and also forces us to allow certain singularities in configurations and classical solutions. The choice is justified from the realisation in JT gravity, which naturally regulates these singularities. The path integral remains one-loop exact via fermionic localisation, but this requires additional input beyond the Duistermaat-Heckman theorem. This allows an exact computation of the path integral for all theories and all couplings, including new results for the original Schwarzian theory.

Abstract: We consider four-derivative superinvariants of five-dimensional $\mathcal N=2$ supergravity coupled to $n_v\le 2$ vector multiplets, which we obtain from both the superconformal tensor calculus approach and dimensional reduction. However, for the case of one vector multiplet, after field redefinitions, we find that there are three independent superinvariants, one of which is a vector superinvariant that does not contain any curvatures and takes the form of a supersymmetrization of $F^4$. Similarly, for the two vector multiplet case, corresponding to the STU model, we find three gravitational superinvariants and two $F^4$-type vector superinvariants. Moreover, we find that these vector superinvariants do not affect the two- and three-charge static BPS black hole solutions. Abstract: The interplay between quantum orientation entanglement and Wigner rotation plays a fundamental role in understanding the behavior of spin angular momentum in quantum states. To analyze the quantum orientation entanglement of the relativistic helicity states interpolating between the Jacob-Wick helicity and the light-front helicity, we examine the relative angle between the particle's momentum direction and the spin orientation for the interpolating helicity states. For this analysis, we introduce a novel method for expanding the interpolating helicity states in terms of the Jacob-Wick helicity. The corresponding probabilistic coefficients follow the structure of the Wigner d-matrix elements, which we use for the interpretation of the quantum orientation entanglement manifested in the angular distributions of the interpolating scattering helicity amplitudes. As an explicit demonstration, we compute the interpolating helicity amplitudes for the pair production of spin-1 (vector) particles in the annihilation of two spin-0 (scalar) particles, focusing primarily on their contact interaction. ### [40] [Type IIB Supergravity Action and Holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18248)
*Soumya Adhikari,Junho Hong,Chanyoung Joung,Geum Lee*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在AdS₅/CFT₄对应关系中，自由能通常从五维规范超引力的欧几里得壳上作用量计算，而非直接在十维中计算。传统IIB型赝作用量在AdS₅×S⁵背景上恒为零，阻碍了第一性原理的全息比较。

Method: 基于Pasti-Sorokin-Tonin表述，将Kurlyand-Tseytlin的拓扑修正推广到更广泛的IIB型背景，在更温和条件下引入广义拓扑修正项，涵盖一般维度的AdS几何和非零2-形式势。

Abstract: In the prototypical AdS$_5$/CFT$_4$ correspondence, the free energy of $\mathcal{N}=4$ SU$(N)$ super Yang-Mills theory is commonly reproduced from the Euclidean on-shell action of five-dimensional gauged supergravity -- a consistent truncation of Type IIB supergravity -- rather than computed directly in ten dimensions. A longstanding obstacle to the latter is that the conventional Type IIB pseudo-action evaluated on the $AdS_5\times S^5$ background vanishes identically, apparently precluding a first-principles holographic comparison. A recent proposal by Kurlyand and Tseytlin, based on the Pasti-Sorokin-Tonin formulation, resolves this issue for a special class of backgrounds including the $AdS_5\times S^5$ vacuum by introducing a topological term required for consistency, yielding a non-vanishing on-shell value in agreement with holography. In this work we extend this refinement to a broader class of Type IIB backgrounds by introducing a generalized topological correction under milder conditions, encompassing AdS geometries of generic dimension and non-vanishing 2-form potentials. We test the proposal on non-trivial solutions such as the Lunin-Maldacena background and the $AdS_4$ $S$-fold solution, and find agreement with the corresponding lower-dimensional gauged supergravity on-shell actions and thereby with the expected holographic observables. Our results place direct holographic comparisons within the ten-dimensional Type IIB framework on firmer ground.

### [41] [Multifield dark energy: Interplay between curved field space and curved spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18341)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弦紧致化（string compactifications）激发的指数quintessence模型自然涉及在弯曲场空间中演化的伸缩子标量场（dilatonic scalar）及其轴子伙伴（axionic partner）。空间曲率扩大了宇宙学相空间，可能影响晚期动力学，因此需要系统分析这一最小双场指数系统。

Result: 在标量主导极限下，非测地线轨迹（non-geodesic trajectories）可以在陡峭势能上维持加速膨胀，而在弯曲宇宙中，标度-曲率固定点（scaling-curvature fixed point）原则上可以软化加速要求。然而，这些机制出现在不同的不变流形（invariant manifolds）中，在背景流体存在时无法同时实现。在观测可行的解冻机制（thawing regime）下，轴子不追踪背景流体，空间曲率变得动态次要，导致有效的单场演化。研究还识别出曲率效应与标量场动力学之间的简并性（degeneracy）。

Abstract: Exponential quintessence models motivated by string compactifications naturally involve both a dilatonic scalar and its axionic partner evolving on a curved field space, while spatial curvature enlarges the cosmological phase space and may affect late-time dynamics. In the scalar-dominated limit, non-geodesic trajectories can sustain accelerated expansion on steep potentials, and in curved universes a scaling-curvature fixed point can in principle soften the requirements for acceleration. However, we show that these mechanisms arise in distinct invariant manifolds and cannot be simultaneously realized in the presence of a background fluid: no non-geodesic scaling fixed point exists within an open region of parameter space. As a consequence, in the observationally viable thawing regime the axion does not track the background fluid and spatial curvature becomes dynamically subdominant, leading to an effectively single-field evolution. We further identify a degeneracy between curvature effects and scalar-field dynamics that limits their independent impact on late-time cosmology. Confronting the model with current cosmological background data (Planck 2018 distance priors, Pantheon+, BAO, and cosmic chronometers), we obtain an upper bound $λ\lesssim 0.75$ (95 percent CL) on the potential slope. Our results demonstrate that even in the minimal multifield setup with spatial curvature, sustained late-time acceleration requires a sufficiently flat potential, so that the tension between cosmic acceleration and quantum gravity expectations persists within this framework.

Abstract: We study soft emission in QED during scattering of Faddeev-Kulish dressed states. The incoming and outgoing charged particles are accompanied by coherent clouds of soft photons with energies below a characteristic infrared scale $E_d$. We focus on explicit processes that allow the dependence of the soft factors on the hard particles' momenta and total angular momenta to be displayed clearly. We argue that the dressings remove the infrared divergences in hard amplitudes order by order in perturbation theory, effectively regulating the contributions from virtual soft photons at the scale $E_d$. Essentially, the Faddeev-Kulish hard amplitudes become equivalent to the infrared-finite part of the corresponding Fock-basis amplitudes. Finally, tree-level soft-photon emission is found to be suppressed once the dressings are extended to subleading order in the soft-momentum expansion, as prescribed in recent work by Choi and Akhoury.

Abstract: The M-theoretic Emergence Proposal claims that all of the terms in the low-energy action arise from quantum effects. By examining the spectrum of the dilatation operator as a function of complex Nc, we identify a network of Exceptional Points (EPs) -- non-Hermitian degeneracies where anomalous dimensions degenerate and operator eigenstates coalesce. We demonstrate that these EPs act as topological defects in complex Nc-space, generating non-Abelian geometric phases and enforcing nontrivial monodromies among gauge-invariant operators. Moreover, we establish a correspondence between the spontaneous breaking of an emergent PT symmetry of the dilatation operator and the fundamental spacetime PT symmetry of the underlying gauge theory. In the vicinity of EPs, the resulting non-Hermitian dynamics produces logarithmic scaling behavior in correlation functions, characteristic of logarithmic conformal field theories. *D. M. van Egmond,L. C. Ferreira,A. D. Pereira,G. Peruzzo,S. P. Sorella*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在最大阿贝尔规范（maximal Abelian gauge）中引入类质量项（mass-like term）的有效性，通过单圈计算（one-loop computation）验证了该方法能够准确描述SU(2)规范理论中非阿贝尔（non-Abelian）和对角（diagonal）胶子传播子（gluon propagator）的红外行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在朗道规范（Landau gauge）中引入胶子类质量项已被证明能有效重现微扰计算（perturbative computations）中规范固定关联函数（gauge-fixed correlation functions）的格点结果（lattice results）。由于这些量具有规范依赖性（gauge dependent），需要探究该方案在不同规范中描述胶子和法捷耶夫-波波夫鬼（Faddeev-Popov ghost）传播子红外行为（infrared behavior）的普适性。

Method: 研究在最大阿贝尔规范中系统性地探讨了该问题，该规范无法形变为朗道规范且已在规范固定格点模拟（gauge-fixed lattice simulations）中得到研究。计算了SU(2)规范理论下单圈非阿贝尔和对角胶子传播子，并对格点数据进行了拟合。

Result: 结果表明，非阿贝尔胶子传播子的横向分量（transverse component）以及对角胶子传播子，在红外区域与格点数据吻合良好（in good agreement with lattice data in the infrared）。

Conclusion: 在最大阿贝尔规范中引入类质量项的方法能够有效描述胶子传播子的红外行为，验证了该方案在不同规范中的适用性，为理解杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theories）的红外特性提供了新的视角。

Abstract: The inclusion of a mass-like term for the gluon in Yang-Mills theories quantized in the Landau gauge has proven to be an effective way of reproducing lattice results for gauge-fixed correlation functions within perturbative computations. Since those quantities are gauge dependent, it is natural to question how general this prescription is for describing the infrared behavior of gluon and Faddeev-Popov ghost propagators in different gauges. In this work, we provide a systematic investigation of this issue in the maximal Abelian gauge, which cannot be deformed into the Landau gauge and has been investigated in gauge-fixed lattice simulations. We compute the one-loop non-Abelian and diagonal gluon propagators and perform fits to lattice data in the case of $SU(2)$. Our results show that the transverse component of the non-Abelian gluon propagator as well as the diagonal gluon propagator, are in good agreement with lattice data in the infrared.

</details>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [51] [ADAMOS: Axion Daily Modulation Searches for Dark Matter at 20 GHz](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18006)
*Marios Maroudas,Toma-Stefan Cezar,Antonios Gardikiotis,Dieter Horns*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: ADAMOS项目旨在通过新型轴子晕镜实验探索暗物质本质，在20GHz频率下采用创新的"薄壳"设计，同时搜索三类轴子信号，开辟暗物质探测新通道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该项目旨在探索暗物质（dark matter, DM）的本质，通过新型轴子晕镜（axion haloscope）实验开辟暗物质探测的新通道，特别是在先前未探索的频率区域。

Method: 采用创新的"薄壳"（thin-shell）设计构建固定频率20GHz的腔体谐振器，安装在现有的14T超导磁体中，并连接具有连续原位校准功能的高灵敏度射频链（RF chain），以消除温度相关的增益漂移。

Result: 该方法基于先前尝试的经验教训进行了重要改进，能够在先前未探索的频率区域建立稳健、校准且多功能的实验装置。

Conclusion: ADAMOS项目将同时搜索三类轴子信号，包括传统冷暗物质轴子、相对论性轴子以及流暗物质瞬态增强信号，从而在暗物质探测领域开辟新的发现通道。

Abstract: The ADAMOS (Axion Daily Modulation Searches) project aims to explore the nature of dark matter (DM) through a novel axion haloscope experiment. We propose to construct a fixed-frequency cavity resonator operating at 20 GHz at the University of Hamburg, using an innovative "thin-shell" design that preserves a large detection volume at high frequencies. The experiment will be installed in an existing 14 T superconducting magnet and connected to a highly sensitive RF chain with continuous in situ calibration to eliminate temperature-dependent gain drifts, constituting an essential improvement based on lessons learned from previous attempts. ADAMOS will conduct simultaneous searches for three classes of axion signals: (1) conventional cold DM axions, (2) relativistic axions from axion quark nugget annihilations exhibiting daily modulations, and (3) transient enhancements from streaming DM. By targeting this unexplored frequency regime with a robust, calibrated, and versatile setup, ADAMOS will open new discovery channels in a previously unexplored region of the dark sector.

</details>


### [52] [A search for lepton-flavour violating $τ\to 3μ$ decays with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18099)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究利用ATLAS探测器在13 TeV质子-质子对撞中收集的数据，对τ→3μ衰变中的带电轻子味破坏过程进行搜索，未发现显著信号，给出了分支比的上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在寻找带电轻子味破坏（charged lepton flavour violation）过程τ→3μ衰变，这类过程在标准模型（Standard Model）中受到高度抑制，其观测将暗示新物理的存在。

Method: 研究利用ATLAS探测器在13 TeV质心能量下收集的137 fb⁻¹积分亮度数据，聚焦于电弱（electroweak）W→τν产生道。采用双μ子和三μ子触发，并运用多变量分析（multivariate analysis）分离信号与背景，最后对三μ子不变质量谱进行无分箱似然拟合（unbinned likelihood fit）。

Result: 数据与仅有背景的假设相符，未发现显著信号。观测到（预期）的分支比B(τ→3μ)在90%置信水平下的上限为8.7×10⁻⁸（7.5×10⁻⁸）。

Conclusion: 研究未发现τ→3μ衰变的证据，给出了该过程分支比的最严格上限，为寻找超出标准模型的新物理设定了重要约束。

Abstract: A search for charged lepton flavour violation in $τ\to 3μ$ decays is performed in $pp$ collisions at a centre-of-mass energy of 13 TeV using ATLAS data collected between 2016 and 2018, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 137 $\text{fb}^{-1}$. The search focuses on the electroweak $W \to τν$ production channel. Data are collected using two-muon and three-muon triggers and a multivariate analysis is used to separate the signal from the background. An unbinned likelihood fit is then performed to the resulting three-muon invariant mass spectrum and the data are found to be compatible with the background-only hypothesis. The observed (expected) limit on the branching ratio $B(τ\to3μ)$ is found to be $8.7\times 10^{-8}$ ($7.5\times 10^{-8}$) at $90\%$ CL.

</details>


### [53] [Reconstruction of overlapping electromagnetic showers in calorimeters using Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18172)
*Yuliia Maidannyk,Fabrice Couderc,Julie Malclès,Mehmet Özgür Sahin*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出基于深度学习的电磁量能器能量沉积聚类方法，包括两步策略和单步图变换器ClusTEX，在重叠簇射重建、能量分辨率等方面优于标准算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现代强子对撞机实验中，提升的拓扑结构和堆积效应导致重叠簇射和能量分配模糊，需要精确的电磁能量沉积聚类来重建光子和电子。

Method: 研究包括两种方法：两步策略先识别候选种子窗口，然后通过距离加权消息传递或注意力机制联合处理；单步图变换器ClusTEX在一个推理阶段同时完成候选选择和重建，采用新颖的位置编码方案分离图内局部坐标与全局探测器坐标。

Result: 在玩具量能器中，基于注意力的交互相对于标准算法和距离驱动消息传递改善了重叠簇射重建，同时保持孤立光子性能并减少分裂。对于提升的π⁰→γγ衰变，注意力模型保持双光子质量重建能力。在ECAL启发拓扑中，ClusTEX提供最佳整体性能，相比两步方法和标准算法改善了能量分辨率并减少分裂，且在局部探测器失效时保持鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 基于深度学习的聚类方法，特别是单步图变换器ClusTEX，在电磁量能器能量沉积重建中表现出优越性能，能够有效处理重叠簇射并保持对探测器失效的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Accurate clustering of electromagnetic energy deposits is essential for reconstructing photons and electrons in modern hadron collider experiments, where boosted topologies and pileup cause overlapping showers and ambiguous energy assignment. We present deep learning-based clustering approaches that reconstruct particle energy and position directly from calorimeter readout. The study includes a two-step strategy in which candidate seed windows are identified and then jointly processed via distance-weighted message passing or attention mechanism and a single-step graph transformer, ClusTEX, which performs candidate selection and reconstruction in one inference stage. ClusTEX uses a novel positional encoding scheme that separates local coordinates within the graph from global detector coordinates, enabling efficient, geometry-aware inference. Models are trained on GEANT4 simulations of a simplified (toy) and an ECAL-inspired topology with an explicit $η-φ$ dependence. Performance is evaluated using efficiency, energy and position resolutions and splitting rate - reconstruction of two objects for a single photon. In the toy calorimeter, attention-based interactions improve the reconstruction of overlapping showers relative to both the standard algorithm and distance-driven message passing, while maintaining performance on isolated photons and reducing splitting without multi-pass inference. For boosted $π^0\toγγ$, the attention-based model retains di-photon mass reconstruction capability, where the standard algorithm becomes inefficient. In the ECAL-inspired topology, ClusTEX provides the best overall performance, yielding improved energy resolution and reduced splitting compared to two-step approaches and the standard algorithm. It also remains robust under localized detector failures, showing improved stability and partial recovery of energy in non-responsive channels.

</details>
