Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: BESIII实验首次观测到$D_s^+ \to π^+π^0π^0η$衰变，测得$a_0(980)^+ f_0(500)$中间态的分支比为$(0.98 \pm 0.16_{\rm{stat.}} \pm 0.22_{\rm{syst.}})\%$，显著性超过$10σ$，为轻标量介子内部结构提供了新约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过分析$D_s^+$介子的稀有衰变过程，探索轻标量介子（light scalar mesons）的内部结构。实验利用BESIII探测器在质心能量4.128-4.226 GeV收集的数据，首次观测$D_s^+ \to π^+π^0π^0η$衰变模式。

Method: 实验采用BESIII探测器在$e^+e^-$对撞中收集积分亮度为7.33 fb$^{-1}$的数据集。通过分析$D_s^+ \to π^+π^0π^0η$衰变过程，测量了多个中间态的衰变分支比，包括$a_0(980)^+ f_0(500)$和$a_1(1260)^+η$等中间过程。

Result: 首次观测到$D_s^+ \to π^+π^0π^0η$衰变，测得$a_0(980)^+ f_0(500)$分支比为$(0.98 \pm 0.16_{\rm{stat.}} \pm 0.22_{\rm{syst.}})\%$（显著性$>10σ$）。主要中间过程$D_s^+ \to a_1(1260)^+η$分支比为$(1.77 \pm 0.21_{\rm stat.} \pm 0.12_{\rm syst.})\%$。同位旋对称性在$a_1(1260)^+$衰变中得到验证。

Conclusion: 该观测为轻标量介子内部结构提供了新的实验约束。测量结果将未探测的$D_s^+ \to ηX$衰变分支比限制在(0.1 $\pm$ 3.1)\%，显著降低了不确定性。实验验证了同位旋对称性在相关衰变过程中的适用性。

Abstract: We report the first observation of the decay $D_s^+ \to π^+π^0π^0η$ in a data set corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 7.33 fb$^{-1}$, collected in $e^+e^-$ collisions by the BESIII detector at center-of-mass energies between 4.128 and 4.226 GeV. An unexpectedly large branching fraction $\mathcal{B}( D_s^+ \to a_0(980)^+ f_0(500), a_0(980)^+ \to π^+η, f_0(500)\to π^0π^0) = (0.98 \pm 0.16_{\rm{stat.}} \pm 0.22_{\rm{syst.}})\%$ is measured with a significance exceeding $10σ$, offering new constraints on the internal structure of light scalar mesons. The dominant intermediate process is $D_s^+ \to a_1(1260)^+η, a_1(1260)^+\to ρ(770)^+π^0$ with a branching fraction of $(1.77 \pm 0.21_{\rm stat.} \pm 0.12_{\rm syst.})\%$. The isospin symmetry has been validated to the decays of $a_1(1260)^+\to ρ(770)^0π^+$ and $a_1(1260)^+\to ρ(770)^+π^0$. Moreover, the measured $\mathcal{B}(D_s^+\to π^+π^0π^0η|_{\rm{non}-η^\prime})=(2.97 \pm 0.23_{\rm stat.} \pm 0.14_{\rm sys.})$ reduces the undetected $D_s^+ \to ηX$ decay branching fractions to (0.1 $\pm$ 3.1)\%.

### [55] [Combined effective field theory interpretation of measurements sensitive to quartic gauge boson couplings in $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18630)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文通过结合ATLAS探测器在LHC上收集的质子-质子对撞数据，对反常四重电弱规范玻色子耦合（anomalous quartic electroweak gauge boson couplings）进行联合测量，并使用有效场论框架下的Éboli模型维度-8算符来约束这些反常耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于通过测量反常四重电弱规范玻色子自耦合来探索超出标准模型（Beyond Standard Model）的新物理效应。这些反常耦合可以通过有效场论中的高维算符来描述，为探测新物理能标提供了重要途径。

Method: 方法结合了多个分析：包括在多种末态中测量矢量玻色子散射（vector-boson scattering）以及三重玻色子测量。使用ATLAS探测器在LHC上收集的$\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV质子-质子对撞数据，并采用Éboli模型中的维度-8算符（dimension-8 operators）在有效场论框架下进行参数化。

Result: 结果以68%和95%置信水平区间呈现，参数化为一个或两个威尔逊系数（Wilson coefficients），包括应用和不应用幺正性约束的情况。同时展示了幺正性和正定性（unitarity and positivity）的理论界限，并提供了对所有威尔逊系数同时进行轮廓拟合得到的置信区间。

Conclusion: 该联合测量为反常电弱玻色子四重自耦合提供了约束，通过有效场论框架下的维度-8算符参数化，为探索超出标准模型的新物理效应建立了重要限制。结合幺正性和正定性理论界限的分析增强了结果的可靠性。

Abstract: A combination of measurements sensitive to anomalous quartic electroweak gauge boson couplings is presented using proton-proton collision data collected by the ATLAS detector at $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV at the LHC. Contributing analyses include measurements of vector-boson scattering in numerous final states as well as a tri-boson measurement. The combined measurement is used to constrain anomalous electroweak boson quartic self-couplings that result from dimension-8 operators in the Éboli model using an effective field theory. Results are presented as 68% and 95% confidence level intervals parameterised by one or two Wilson coefficients, both with and without unitarity constraints applied. Theoretical bounds from unitarity and positivity are overlaid where relevant. Confidence intervals obtained from simultaneous profiled fits to all Wilson coefficients are also presented.

</details>


### [56] [Measurement of the $\mathbf{B^0}$-meson production cross section in proton--proton collisions at $\mathbf{\sqrt{\textit{s}}=13.6}$ TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18904)
*ALICE Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: ALICE实验首次在LHC能量下测量了质心能量13.6 TeV质子-质子碰撞中B⁰介子的横向动量微分产生截面，测量范围延伸至p_T=1 GeV/c，结果与微扰量子色动力学模型一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在首次在LHC能量下测量B⁰介子在中快度区域（|y|<0.5）的横向动量微分产生截面，测量范围延伸至低横向动量区域（p_T=1 GeV/c），以检验微扰量子色动力学（perturbative quantum-chromodynamics）计算模型的准确性。

Method: 使用ALICE探测器在CERN LHC上进行质子-质子碰撞实验，质心能量为√s=13.6 TeV。通过B⁰→D⁻π⁺衰变通道重建B⁰介子及其电荷共轭态，随后D⁻→K⁺π⁻π⁻衰变用于次级重建。

Result: 测量结果显示B⁰介子在中快度区域的单位快度产生截面为dσ(B⁰)/dy|_{|y|<0.5} = 24.2 ± 1.4(统计) ± 2.6(系统)_{-0.3}^{+0.2}(外推) μb。横向动量微分产生截面在不确定性范围内与基于微扰量子色动力学的最新模型描述一致。

Conclusion: 该研究首次在LHC能量下实现了B⁰介子产生截面的低横向动量测量，为检验重夸克产生机制的理论模型提供了重要实验数据，同时通过与前向快度B⁺介子测量的比较，研究了产生截面的快度依赖性。

Abstract: This article reports the measurement of the transverse-momentum ($p_{\rm T}$) differential production cross section of B$^0$ mesons in proton-proton collisions at a centre-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV with the ALICE detector at the CERN LHC. For the first time, the B$^0$ production cross section is measured at midrapidity ($|y|<0.5$) down to $p_{\rm T}=1~\mathrm{GeV}/c$ at LHC energies. The B$^0$ mesons and their charge conjugates were reconstructed via the B$^{0}\to$D$^{-}π^+$ decay channel, followed by the D$^-\to$K$^+π^-π^-$ decay. The measured $p_{\rm T}$-differential production cross section is described within uncertainties by state-of-the-art models based on perturbative quantum-chromodynamics calculations. Its rapidity dependence is also studied by computing the $p_{\rm T}$-differential ratios between the ALICE measurement and the one of B$^+$ mesons performed by the LHCb Collaboration at forward rapidity. The B$^0$ production cross section per unit of rapidity at midrapidity is ${\rm d}σ({\rm B^0})/{\rm d} y|_{|y|<0.5} = 24.2 \pm 1.4~(\text{stat.}) \pm 2.6~(\text{syst.})_{-0.3}^{+0.2}~(\text{extrap.})~μ{\rm b}$.

### [57] [Spin-Charge Groups for Fermions in Fluids and Crystals: General Structures and Physical Consequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18125)
*Arist Zhenyuan Yang,Zheng-Xin Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文引入自旋-电荷群（spin-charge groups）来描述费米子系统的广义对称性，涵盖自旋、电荷与空间自由度的耦合，并展示了其在多种物理系统中的潜在应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对称群不足以处理费米子系统中自旋、电荷与空间自由度之间的各种耦合。为填补这一空白，需要引入更一般的对称性描述框架。

Method: 引入自旋-电荷群（spin-charge groups, SCG），该群由作为"内禀"对称性的自旋与电荷操作、作为"外禀"对称性的时空操作、它们之间的耦合以及投影扭曲（projective twists）组成。

Result: 自旋-电荷群能够产生额外的能带简并、陈数（Chern numbers）以及交叉自旋-电荷响应（如自旋超流）。该框架可用于分类和探索包含强相互作用的新物质相。

Conclusion: 自旋-电荷群为描述费米子系统最一般的对称性提供了框架，即使在包含强相互作用的情况下，也为分类和探索新物质相提供了途径。

Abstract: Known symmetry groups are not sufficient to handle various couplings between spin, charge and spatial degrees of freedom for fermions. To fill in this gap, we introduce the spin-charge groups (SCG) to describe the most general symmetries of fermionic systems. These groups are composed of the spin and charge operations as the `internal' symmetries, the spatial and temporal operations as `external' symmetries, couplings between them, and projective twists. After providing the general group structures of SCG, we study their potential applications in concrete physical systems, including $^3$He superfluids, charge-4e superconductors, collinear magnets with spin-fluxes, and superconductors with coexisting magnetic orders. We show that SCG can give rise to extra band degeneracies, Chern numbers and cross spin-charge responses like spin-supercurrents. Hence SCG provide a route to classify and explore new phases of matter even when strong interactions are included.

</details>


### [58] [Disentangling Shear and Compression Phonons: Route to Anomalous Magnetothermal Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18137)
*Haoting Xu,Antoine Matar,Hae-Young Kee*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了受挫磁体中磁热输运异常现象的微观机制：对称性约束的自旋-晶格耦合导致模式选择性自旋-声子相互作用，从而控制热输运，解释了自旋轨道耦合Mott绝缘体中场致输运异常的特征峰-谷-峰结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 各种受挫磁体（frustrated magnets）中的磁热输运（magnetothermal transport）表现出显著偏离传统磁振子（magnon）或声子（phonon）输运的场依赖异常现象，需要微观理论解释这些异常输运行为的物理机制。

Method: 在强自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）极限下，推导出有效自旋-声子哈密顿量（spin-phonon Hamiltonian），其中不同极化的声子选择性地耦合到不同的自旋算符；采用Landauer输运框架（Landauer transport framework）结合精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法，研究耦合到声子浴的自旋链。

Result: 对称性约束的自旋-晶格耦合导致模式选择性自旋-声子相互作用，压缩和剪切声子模式在不同磁场区域对自旋热流产生贡献；该机制在热流的场依赖关系中产生特征性的峰-谷-峰结构（peak-dip-peak structure）。

Conclusion: 该研究为自旋轨道耦合Mott绝缘体（spin-orbit-coupled Mott insulators）中场致输运异常提供了微观解释，揭示了模式选择性自旋-声子相互作用在控制磁热输运中的关键作用。

Abstract: Magnetothermal transport in various frustrated magnets exhibits striking field-dependent anomalies that deviate from conventional magnon or phonon transport. Here we show that symmetry-constrained spin-lattice coupling naturally leads to mode-selective spin-phonon interactions that control heat transport. In the strong spin-orbit coupling limit, we derive an effective spin-phonon Hamiltonian in which phonons with different polarizations couple selectively to distinct spin operators. As a result, compression and shear phonon modes contribute to spin heat current across different magnetic-field regimes. Using a Landauer transport framework combined with exact diagonalization of spin chains coupled to a phonon bath, we show that this mechanism produces a characteristic peak-dip-peak structure in the field dependence of heat current, providing a microscopic explanation for field-induced transport anomalies in spin-orbit-coupled Mott insulators.

</details>


### [59] [Removing nodal and support-mismatch pathologies in Variational Monte Carlo via blurred sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18148)
*Zhou-Quan Wan,Roeland Wiersema,Shiwei Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种称为"模糊采样（blurred sampling）"的方法，用于解决变分蒙特卡洛（VMC）和时变VMC（t-VMC）中由于波函数节点导致的统计病理问题，从而提高数值模拟的鲁棒性和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变分蒙特卡洛（VMC）作为优化和演化参数化多体波函数的有力方法，在实际应用中面临统计估计器不稳定或有偏的问题。这些问题源于量子波函数普遍存在的节点特征，导致连续空间中估计器出现重尾分布和方差发散，离散希尔伯特空间中采样分布可能遗漏支持集部分，从而影响优化轨迹和变分动力学的可靠性。

Method: 本文引入了模糊采样（blurred sampling）方法，该方法具有严格的理论性质，能够保证良好的行为、有效性和效率。作为一种后处理技术，它可以在不修改底层采样器的情况下使用，仅产生最小的计算开销。

Result: 该方法在多个标准采样方法已知会失效的代表性示例中展示了有效性，并成功应用于自旋动力学的大规模问题。这些结果表明模糊采样能够解决VMC和t-VMC中的统计病理问题。

Conclusion: 模糊采样方法为解决变分蒙特卡洛和时变变分蒙特卡洛中的统计病理问题提供了一个广泛适用的框架，显著提升了数值模拟的鲁棒性和可靠性，为大规模量子系统模拟提供了更稳定的计算基础。

Abstract: Variational Monte Carlo (VMC) is a powerful and fast-growing method for optimizing and evolving parameterized many-body wave functions, especially with modern neural-network quantum states. In practice, however, the stochastic estimators that form the backbone of the method can become unstable or biased due to the presence of nodes, a ubiquitous feature of quantum wave functions. In the continuum, this results in heavy-tailed estimators with potentially divergent variances, while in discrete Hilbert spaces the sampling distribution can miss parts of the support needed to form unbiased estimators. These statistical pathologies lead to unreliable optimization trajectories in stochastic reconfiguration or incorrect variational dynamics in time-dependent Variational Monte Carlo (t-VMC), and severely limit the power of the numerical simulations. We introduce blurred sampling to address these difficulties. The method has a number of rigorous properties that make it well-behaved, effective and efficient. Additionally it is a post-processing approach that can be used without modifying the underlying sampler and incurs only minimal overhead. We demonstrate its effectiveness on several representative examples where standard sampling approaches are known to fail, and apply it to large-scale problems in spin dynamics. This work establishes a broadly applicable framework for robust VMC and t-VMC calculations.

</details>


### [60] [Polaron-driven switching of octupolar order in doped 5d$^2$ double perovskite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18155)
*Dario Fiore Mosca,Lorenzo Celiberti,Leonid V. Pourovskii,Cesare Franchini*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在阐明掺杂诱导的小极化子对5d²双钙钛矿Ba₂CaOsO₆低温多极序的影响，特别是澄清先前实验中观察到的Na掺杂导致铁八极序（ferro-octupolar order）逐渐抑制和有序温度降低的模糊现象。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first principles）方法，计算了5d¹局域空穴极化子与5d²磁性离子之间的位点间交换相互作用（intersite exchange interactions），并求解相应的有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）。

Result: 研究发现掺杂导致主导的八极交换（octupolar exchange）从铁磁性（ferromagnetic）反转为反铁磁性（antiferromagnetic），这一反转解释了Na掺杂对铁八极序的渐进抑制和有序温度的降低。

Conclusion: 该研究澄清了先前模糊的实验观察，并证明以小型极化子形式进行的电荷掺杂为调控自旋轨道纠缠材料（spin-orbit-entangled materials）中的位点间交换相互作用提供了可行途径，从而能够实现新型量子序（quantum orders）的出现。

Abstract: We investigate how doping-induced small polarons impact the low-temperature multipolar orders of the $5d^2$ double perovskite Ba$_2$CaOsO$_6$. By computing intersite exchange interactions between 5d$^1$ localized hole polarons and 5d$^2$ magnetic ions from first principles, we demonstrate the reversal of the dominant octupolar exchange from ferromagnetic to antiferromagnetic. Solving the corresponding effective Hamiltonian we find this reversal to account for the progressive suppression of the ferro-octupolar order and the reduction of the ordering temperature upon Na doping. These findings clarify previously ambiguous experimental observations and demonstrate that charge doping in the form of small polarons offers a viable route to tuning intersite exchange interactions in spin-orbit-entangled materials, enabling the emergence of novel quantum orders.

</details>


### [61] [Tackling the Sign Problem in the Doped Hubbard Model with Normalizing Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18205)
*Dominic Schuh,Lena Funcke,Janik Kreit,Thomas Luu,Simran Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于归一化流（normalizing flows）和退火方案（annealing scheme）的新方法，用于解决有限化学势下Hubbard模型的符号问题（sign problem）和遍历性问题（ergodicity issues），相比现有方法显著降低了统计不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限化学势下的Hubbard模型是理解掺杂关联系统（doped correlated systems）的基础，但模拟受到符号问题（sign problem）的严重限制。在辅助场（auxiliary-field）表述中，自旋基（spin basis）虽能缓解符号问题，但严重的遍历性问题（ergodicity issues）限制了其应用。

Method: 本研究将半填充（half-filling）条件下的归一化流（normalizing flows）方法扩展到有限化学势，通过引入退火方案（annealing scheme）实现遍历性采样（ergodic sampling）。

Result: 与电荷基（charge basis）中最先进的混合蒙特卡洛（hybrid Monte Carlo）方法相比，该方法能准确再现精确对角化（exact diagonalization）结果，同时将统计不确定性降低了一个数量级。

Conclusion: 该方法为掺杂关联系统（doped correlated systems）的模拟开辟了新途径，解决了有限化学势下Hubbard模型的符号问题和遍历性问题。

Abstract: The Hubbard model at finite chemical potential is a cornerstone for understanding doped correlated systems, but simulations are severely limited by the sign problem. In the auxiliary-field formulation, the spin basis mitigates the sign problem, yet severe ergodicity issues have limited its use. We extend recent advances with normalizing flows at half-filling to finite chemical potential by introducing an annealing scheme enabling ergodic sampling. Compared to state-of-the-art hybrid Monte Carlo in the charge basis, our approach accurately reproduces exact diagonalization results while reducing statistical uncertainties by an order of magnitude, opening a new path for simulations of doped correlated systems.

</details>


### [62] [Symmetric Mass Generation in a Bilayer Honeycomb Lattice with $\mathrm{SU}(2)\times\mathrm{SU}(2)\times\mathrm{SU}(2)/\mathbb{Z}_2$ Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18278)
*Cheng-Hao He,Yi-Zhuang You,Xiao Yan Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模行列式量子蒙特卡罗（DQMC）模拟，为(2+1)维对称质量生成（SMG）提供了数值精确证据，发现了一个不破坏对称性的直接质量间隙相变，其临界指数与现有理论预测显著不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对称质量生成（SMG）是一种在不破坏对称性或产生拓扑序的情况下产生费米子系统质量间隙的机制，这对传统的朗道范式（Landau paradigm）构成了挑战。本文旨在为(2+1)维的SMG提供数值证据。

Method: 采用大规模行列式量子蒙特卡罗（determinant quantum Monte Carlo, DQMC）模拟双层蜂窝晶格模型，该模型具有$\mathrm{SU}(2)\times\mathrm{SU}(2)\times\mathrm{SU}(2)/\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性。通过系统搜索所有19个对称不等价的费米子双线性序参量来确认对称性是否破缺。

Result: 在临界耦合$J_c \approx 2.6$处观察到单粒子和玻色子间隙同时打开，相关长度指数为$ν= 1.14(2)$。所有费米子双线性序参量均未显示对称性破缺。费米子反常维度（anomalous dimension）估计为$η_ψ= 0.071(1)$，与现有理论预测显著偏离，表明属于不同的普适类（universality class）。

Conclusion: 研究为(2+1)维对称质量生成提供了数值精确证据，并揭示了纯非阿贝尔对称性（pure non-Abelian symmetry）在禁止双线性凝聚和强制执行直接SMG相变中的关键作用，通过与相关模型的对比进一步证实了这一机制。

Abstract: Symmetric mass generation (SMG) is a mechanism for generating mass gaps in fermionic systems without breaking any symmetries or developing topological order, challenging the conventional Landau paradigm. In this Letter, we provide numerically exact evidence for SMG in (2+1) dimensions through large-scale determinant quantum Monte Carlo (DQMC) simulations of a bilayer honeycomb lattice model with $\mathrm{SU}(2)\times\mathrm{SU}(2)\times\mathrm{SU}(2)/\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry. We observe the simultaneous opening of single-particle and bosonic gaps at a critical coupling $J_c \approx 2.6$ with correlation length exponent $ν= 1.14(2)$, while an exhaustive search over all 19 symmetry-inequivalent fermion bilinear order parameters confirms the absence of any symmetry breaking. We estimate the fermion anomalous dimension to be $η_ψ= 0.071(1)$, which deviates significantly from the large-$N$ prediction ($η_ψ\approx 0.595$) and variational Monte Carlo estimates ($η_ψ\approx 0.62$), pointing to a distinct universality class. By contrasting with a related $\mathrm{Spin}(5)\times\mathrm{U}(1)/\mathbb{Z}_2$ model that develops an intermediate excitonic phase, we demonstrate the crucial role of pure non-Abelian symmetry in prohibiting bilinear condensates and enforcing the direct SMG transition.

</details>

*Cheng-Hao He,Yi-Zhuang You,Xiao Yan Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种系统框架，用于分析多自由度相互作用费米子系统的连续对称性，并通过Majorana表示和半单李代数理论识别可能的序参量候选。

Motivation: 在具有多个内部自由度的相互作用费米子系统中，确定完整的连续对称群并分类可能的序参量仍然具有挑战性。对称性在现代物理学中扮演核心角色，从量子态分类到通过自发对称破缺表征物相。

Method: 通过将哈密顿量映射到Majorana表示，从与哈密顿量对易的算符的李代数中获取连续对称性的生成元。利用半单李代数理论识别该李代数的结构，并基于表示理论开发系统方法枚举序参量候选。

Result: 通过分解对称代数在Majorana空间上诱导的外幂表示，并结合离散晶格对称性，根据序参量破坏的对称性对它们进行分类。该方法能够系统地枚举候选序参量。

Conclusion: 该框架为分析多自由度相互作用费米子系统的连续对称性和识别候选序参量提供了系统方法，结合了Majorana表示、李代数理论和表示理论。

Abstract: Symmetry plays a central role in modern physics, from classifying quantum states to characterizing phases of matter through spontaneous symmetry breaking. In interacting fermionic systems with multiple internal degrees of freedom, however, determining the full continuous symmetry group and classifying possible order parameters remain challenging. In this work, we present a systematic framework for analyzing continuous symmetries and identifying candidate order parameters in such systems. By mapping the Hamiltonian to a Majorana representation, we obtain the generators of continuous symmetries from the Lie algebra of operators that commute with the Hamiltonian. We then identify the structure of this Lie algebra using the theory of semisimple Lie algebras. Building on representation theory, we further develop a systematic method for exhaustively enumerating candidate order parameters. By decomposing the exterior-power representations induced by the symmetry algebra on the Majorana space and incorporating discrete lattice symmetries, we classify these order parameters according to the symmetries they break. (Abridged. Please see the PDF manuscript for the complete abstract and specific model applications.)

### [64] [Spatially Indirect Exciton Condensation in Two-Dimensional Strongly Correlated Semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18445)
*Yao Zeng,Shi-Cong Mo,Wéi Wú*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）与行列式量子蒙特卡洛方法（determinant quantum Monte Carlo method）相结合，研究包含强在位相互作用（U）和轨道间相互作用（V）的双轨道和三轨道哈伯德模型（Hubbard models）。

Conclusion: 这些发现有助于解释TMCs材料中间接激子强结合能与相对较低转变温度之间的巨大差异，为理解和设计具有强关联d壳层电子的材料中的激子凝聚提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Identifying materials hosting an excitonic insulator ground state has been one of the major pursuits in condensed matter physics in recent years.
  Promising candidates in transition metal chalcogenide compounds (TMC), including $1T-\mathrm{TiSe_2}$, $\mathrm{Ta_2Pd_3Te_5}$, and $\mathrm{Ta_2NiSe_5}$, share a crucial common characteristic: their low-energy physics is governed by electrons in $d-$ orbitals subject to strong on-site Coulomb interactions.
  In this work, we investigate spatially indirect exciton condensation in two-dimensional semimetals on triangular lattice. Using a combination of dynamical mean-field theory and the determinant quantum Monte Carlo method, we study two- and three-orbital Hubbard models incorporating strong on-site ($U$) and inter-orbital interactions ($V$). Our results demonstrate that on-site Hubbard $U$ can strongly suppress the condensation temperature $T_c$, an effect that is particularly pronounced at higher electron-hole pair densities. This behavior contrasts sharply with the case without on-site $U$, where $T_c$ grows with pair density at fixed $V$.
  Moreover, we uncover competition among multiple electron-hole pairing channels in the three-orbital model, which also acts to suppress $T_c$ of exciton condensation. An orbital-selective electron-hole pairing state is identified. These findings may help explain the large discrepancy between strong binding-energy and relative low transition temperature for indirect excitons in TMCs materials, offering important insights for understanding and engineering exciton condensation in materials with strongly correlated $d-$ shell electrons.

Here we report the long-sought flat band resonance in the quasi-two-dimensional kagome bilayer material CsCr6Sb6. ### [67] [Photoemission Signatures of Photoinduced Carriers and Excitons in One-Dimensional Mott Insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18982)
*Taiga Nakamoto,Yuta Murakami,Naoto Tsuji*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该理论研究了一维莫特绝缘体（Mott insulators）中光掺杂（photodoped）载流子的光电子能谱（photoemission spectra），发现其光谱特征与半导体（semiconductors）存在本质差异，揭示了强关联系统中分数化元激发（fractionalized elementary excitations）对光谱响应的关键影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解光掺杂一维莫特绝缘体的光电子能谱特征，这些系统能够容纳激子（excitons），但其光谱特性与光掺杂半导体存在本质差异。强关联效应导致分数化元激发，从根本上改变了光电子响应。

Method: 研究方法结合了精确对角化（exact diagonalization）和奴隶粒子方法（slave-particle approach），用于阐明光谱特征的起源。通过这两种理论方法分析一维莫特绝缘体中光掺杂载流子的光电子能谱。

Result: 研究发现，当光掺杂载流子（双占据子（doublons）和空穴子（holons））未结合时，光电子能谱直接反映自旋子（spinons）的色散关系。当双占据子和空穴子形成激子束缚态时，莫特间隙内出现下哈伯德带（lower Hubbard band）的复制结构，同时包含自旋子和空穴子激发的贡献。间隙内信号的分布对双占据子-空穴子结合程度高度敏感。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，强关联电子系统中光诱导载流子和激子的光电子能谱可以提供关于磁性质和载流子结合性质的信息。这些结果为通过光电子能谱探测强关联系统的分数化激发和束缚态特性提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We theoretically study photoemission spectra for photodoped one-dimensional Mott insulators that can host excitons, and show that their spectral characteristics differ qualitatively from those of photodoped semiconductors. In conventional semiconductors, photoemission spectra are well understood; free charge carriers generate spectral weight near the bottom of the conduction band, while the formation of excitons leads to replica features of the valence band appearing inside the band gap. In one-dimensional Mott insulators, on the other hand, strong correlations give rise to fractionalized elementary excitations-spinons, holons, and doublons-which fundamentally modify the photoemission response. We find that when photodoped carriers, i.e., doublons and holons, remain unbound, the photoemission spectrum directly reflects the dispersion of spinons, i.e., magnetic elementary excitations. In contrast, when a doublon and a holon form an excitonic bound state, replica structures of the lower Hubbard band emerge inside the Mott gap, carrying contributions from both spinon and holon excitations. Importantly, the distribution of the in-gap signal depends sensitively on the degree of doublon-holon binding. The origin of these spectral features is clarified through a combination of exact diagonalization and the slave-particle approach. These results indicate that photoemission from photoinduced carriers and excitons in strongly correlated electron systems can provide information on magnetic properties and carrier-binding properties.

Herein, we report the synthesis and thermodynamic results on a frustrated magnet Co3ZnNb2O9. The Co2+ moments constitute buckled AB-type honeycomb layers in the ab-plane. The temperature-dependent magnetic susceptibility shows a sharp anomaly at 14 K, indicating the onset of long-range magnetic ordering. ### [69] [Computation of thermal entropy for the doped Hubbard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18998)
*Yu-Feng Song,Youjin Deng,Yuan-Yao He*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个高效框架，用于计算掺杂费米-哈伯德模型（doped Fermi-Hubbard model）在巨正则系综（grand-canonical ensemble）中的热熵（thermal entropy）。该框架包含四种计算方案，将熵表达为温度、相互作用强度和化学势参数空间中的路径积分，并通过数值无偏辅助场量子蒙特卡洛方法（auxiliary-field quantum Monte Carlo method）验证了其可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要开发一个高效且广泛适用的框架来计算掺杂哈伯德模型中的热熵，以促进对复杂关联态（complex correlated states）的热力学表征。现有方法在熵计算方面存在效率或适用性限制。

Method: 开发了包含四种计算方案的框架，将熵表达为温度、相互作用强度和化学势参数空间中的路径积分。积分核仅涉及总能量、费米子密度和双占据数等基本可观测量，这些量在多种理论和数值方法中易于获取。进一步推导了连接熵与其他量的麦克斯韦关系（Maxwell relations），并提供了直接评估巨势（grand potential）的实用公式。

Result: 使用数值无偏辅助场量子蒙特卡洛方法计算了二维和三维掺杂哈伯德模型的熵。测试结果显示不同方案之间具有极好的一致性，并定量验证了麦克斯韦关系，确认了框架的可靠性。在二维情况下，与图解蒙特卡洛计算（diagrammatic Monte Carlo calculations）的基准比较显示两种方法之间具有优异的定量一致性。

Conclusion: 该工作通过提供高效且广泛适用的熵评估途径，促进了掺杂哈伯德模型中复杂关联态的热力学表征。框架的可靠性和通用性通过多种验证得到确认，为研究强关联系统的热力学性质提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We develop a highly efficient framework for computing the thermal entropy in the doped Fermi-Hubbard model within the grand-canonical ensemble. The framework comprises four calculation schemes that express the entropy as path integrals in the parameter space of temperature, interaction strength, and chemical potential. The integrands involve only fundamental observables, including the total energy, fermion density, and double occupancy, which are readily accessible in a wide range of theoretical and numerical methods. We further derive useful Maxwell relations connecting the entropy to other quantities, and present practical formulas for directly evaluating the grand potential. As an application, we compute the entropy of the doped Hubbard model in two and three dimensions, using the numerically unbiased auxiliary-field quantum Monte Carlo method. The test results show excellent agreement across the different schemes and quantitatively verify the Maxwell relations, confirming the reliability of the framework. In two dimensions, we further benchmark our entropy results in physically relevant parameter regimes against diagrammatic Monte Carlo calculations and observe excellent quantitative consistency between the two approaches. By providing an efficient and broadly applicable route for entropy evaluation, our work facilitates the thermodynamic characterization of complex correlated states in the doped Hubbard model.

*Ilyas Noor Bhatti,Rachna Chaurasia,Kazi Rumanna Rahman,Sukhendu Sadhukhan,Amantulla Mansuri,Imtiaz Noor Bhatti*

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验分析了LSMO/SRO多层异质结构的结构、磁性和微波磁动力学特性，发现界面Ru-Mn交换耦合对系统的磁响应和动态行为起关键调控作用，多层重复可调节磁开关和阻尼特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究多层氧化物异质结构[LSMO/SRO]_n的界面耦合效应对其结构、磁性和微波磁动力学行为的影响，为探索自旋织构、磁畴行为和室温自旋电子学应用提供平台。

Method: 在SrTiO_3(001)衬底上生长了n=1和5的[LSMO/SRO]_n多层异质结构，采用X射线衍射(X-ray diffraction)验证晶体质量和原子级锐利界面，通过磁测量和铁磁共振(Ferromagnetic resonance, FMR)分析研究磁性和动态特性。

Result: X射线衍射证实了高结晶质量和原子级锐利界面；磁测量显示n=5结构存在明显的两步磁化开关，而n=1结构中该特征显著抑制；FMR分析显示宽线宽、显著的正磁各向异性，以及约10^{-2}量级的吉尔伯特阻尼(Gilbert damping)，且阻尼随多层重复次数增加而减小。

Conclusion: 界面Ru-Mn交换耦合对系统的磁响应和动态行为起关键调控作用，可调节的开关和阻尼特性表明此类氧化物异质界面是探索自旋织构、磁畴行为和室温自旋电子学应用的有前景平台。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the structural, magnetic, and microwave magnetic dynamics of multilayered \([{\rm LSMO}/{\rm SRO}]_n\) heterostructures \((n = 1 \text{ and } 5)\) grown on SrTiO\(_3\) (001) substrates. X-ray diffraction confirms high crystallinity and atomically sharp interfaces. Magnetic measurements reveal strong interfacial magnetic coupling, with a distinct two-step magnetization switching observed in the \(n = 5\) heterostructure, while this feature is significantly suppressed in the \(n = 1\) structure. Ferromagnetic resonance (FMR) analysis shows a broad linewidth, pronounced positive magnetic anisotropy, and Gilbert damping on the order of \(10^{-2}\), with damping decreasing as the number of multilayer repetitions increases. These observations demonstrate that Ru--Mn exchange coupling at the interface critically governs the magnetic response and dynamic behavior of the system. The tunable switching and damping properties highlight such oxide heterointerfaces as promising platforms for exploring spin textures, magnetic domain behavior, and room-temperature spintronic applications.

Using this generalized push-through structure, we classify one-dimensional SPT phases with modulated symmetries and formulate LSM-type constraints within the same MPS-based framework.

### [72] [Nonlinear Kirchhoff-Love shell models derived from the Ciarlet-Geymonat energy: modelling and well-posedness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18164)
*Ionel-Dumitrel Ghiba,Trung Hieu Giang,Catalina Ureche*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文从基于Ciarlet-Geymonat能量的三维模型出发，在可压缩各向同性材料的经典弹性理论框架内推导了非线性壳模型。通过结合渐近厚度缩减与辛普森求积规则，确保了能量泛函的下半连续性，并证明了所提壳模型能量泛函的适定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于从三维可压缩各向同性材料的经典弹性理论出发，推导非线性壳模型。特别关注壳的行为不仅受弹性系数影响，还受三维薄体初始几何形状的影响，以及确保能量泛函下半连续性的数学严谨性。

Method: 方法基于Ciarlet-Geymonat能量三维模型，通过渐近厚度缩减推导非线性壳模型。为避免纯渐近推导可能导致下半连续性不明确的问题，结合了厚度方向的渐近缩减与对纯体积能量项应用辛普森求积规则（Simpson's quadrature rule）。在证明中采用了壳理论中的多凸性（polyconvexity）概念。

Result: 结果表明，Neo-Hookean项导致能量依赖于变形中面的第一、第二和第三基本形式。所得壳模型系数依赖于三维材料的经典Lamé系数、壳厚度以及参考构型的平均曲率和Gauss曲率。纯体积Ciarlet-Geymonat贡献导致二维能量依赖于未变形和变形中面的平均曲率与Gauss曲率。

Conclusion: 本文成功建立了所提壳模型能量泛函的适定性（well-posedness），证明了所得泛函的强制性和下半连续性，并在适当的Sobolev空间中证明了极小值的存在性。证明的关键要素包括壳理论中的多凸性概念以及涉及变形中面平均曲率项弱收敛的相关结果。

Abstract: Starting from a three-dimensional model based on the Ciarlet-Geymonat energy, we derive nonlinear shell models within the classical elasticity theory of compressible isotropic materials. The Neo-Hookean term involving the norm of the deformation gradient leads to an energy depending on the first, the second, and the third fundamental forms of the deformed midsurface. The coefficients appearing in the resulting shell models depend on the classical Lamé coefficients of the three-dimensional material, on the thickness of the shell, and on the mean and Gaussian curvatures of the reference configuration. This shows that the behavior of the shell is influenced not only by the elastic coefficients but also by the initial geometry of the three-dimensional thin body. The purely volumetric Ciarlet-Geymonat contribution of the three-dimensional energy leads to two-dimensional energies depending on the mean and Gaussian curvatures of both configurations, namely the undeformed and the deformed midsurfaces. Since a purely asymptotic derivation may lead to nonlinear terms for which the lower semicontinuity of the resulting functionals is not clear, we combine the asymptotic reduction through the thickness with Simpson's quadrature rule applied to the purely volumetric energy terms, ensuring that the lower semicontinuity is inherited from the three-dimensional model. After deriving the model, we establish the well-posedness of the proposed shell energies. More precisely, we prove coercivity and lower semicontinuity property of the resulting functional and show the existence of minimizers in appropriate Sobolev spaces. A key ingredient in the proofs is a polyconvexity concept in the shell theory, together with some results concerning the weak convergence of terms involving the mean curvature of the deformed midsurface.

Our main result is the construction of solutions with single-frequency asymptotics of the Maxwell field in the case of quasiperiodic pumping. The asymptotics hold for solutions with harmonic initial values which are stationary states of averaged equations in the interaction picture. We calculate all harmonic states and analyse their stability. The calculations rely on the Bloch-Feynman gyroscopic representation of von Neumann equation for the density matrix. The asymptotics follow by application of the averaging theory of the Bogolyubov type.

We develop a decomposition technique to control the convergence of the integral by defining a new integral operator $RT_{\mathbb{C}}(k;x)$. The small norm condition of the operator is obtained to show that there exists a unique solution for the Dbar problem. Moreover, the Dbar dressing method is extended to construct the AKNS spectral problem and the potential construction is presented via the Dbar data. Prior estimates are given to show that the map from the Dbar data to the AKNS potential is Lipschitz continuous.

### [75] [Comment on: "Coherent perfect absorption: Zero reflection without linewidth suppression"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18057)
*Rui-Chang Shen,Jie Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该评论文章反驳了先前论文对极子-机械正常模式分裂（NMS）测量的质疑，指出质疑基于的错误或无关参数，并维护了原始实验测量的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回应Phys. Rev. Research 8, 013261 (2026)论文对Nat. Commun. 16, 5652 (2025)中极子-机械正常模式分裂（polaromechanical normal-mode splitting, NMS）测量的质疑。该质疑基于两个结果：线性尺度谱中无真实分裂，以及腔-磁子极化激元（cavity-magnon polariton）的总衰减率在相干完美吸收（coherent-perfect-absorption, CPA）条件下保持不变。

Method: 通过理论分析指出：1）在CPA频率附近的窄频率范围内，线性和对数尺度谱中均存在NMS；2）通过谱的极点（pole）定义的总衰减率无法表征CPA频率处消失的有效（effective）衰减率（即CPA的单色性），因此该参数与实验中CPA频率附近窄频率范围内测量的NMS无关。

Result: 证明质疑论文的两个结果要么是错误的，要么与所讨论的NMS测量无关。具体而言，NMS确实存在于CPA频率附近的窄频率范围内，而基于谱极点定义的总衰减率变化与CPA频率处的有效衰减率消失现象无关。

Conclusion: 质疑论文的结果无法支持其对原始实验中测量的极子-机械强耦合（polaromechanical strong coupling）的否定主张。原始实验在相干完美吸收（CPA）频率附近窄频率范围内测量的正常模式分裂（NMS）是有效的。

Abstract: A recent paper, Phys. Rev. Research 8, 013261 (2026), claims that the polaromechanical normal-mode splitting (NMS) measured in Nat. Commun. 16, 5652 (2025) is not true based on their two results: $i$) there is no true splitting in the linear-scale spectrum; $ii$) the total or intrinsic decay rate of the cavity-magnon polariton, set by the imaginary part of the pole of the total output spectrum, remains unchanged under the coherent-perfect-absorption (CPA) condition. In this comment, we indicate that $i$) there is NMS in both the linear and logarithmic scales of our spectra in {\it a narrow frequency range} around the CPA frequency; $ii$) the total decay rate defined via the {\it pole} of the spectrum cannot characterize the vanishing {\it effective} decay rate at the CPA frequency (known as the monochromaticity of the CPA), and thus this parameter is irrelevant to the NMS measured in our experiment in {\it a narrow frequency range} around the CPA frequency. Consequently, their results above are either false or irrelevant, and thus cannot support their claim on the polaromechanical strong coupling measured in our experiment.

</details>


### [76] [In-plane magnetic response and Maki parameter of alternating-twist multilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18194)
*Igor Vasilevskiy,Miguel Sánchez Sánchez,Khadija Challaouy,Dionisios Margetis,Guillermo Gómez-Santos,Tobias Stauber*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过解析方法分析了交替扭转（alternating-twist）四层和五层石墨烯系统的面内轨道磁响应，发现奇偶层数系统呈现显著差异：奇数层响应可忽略，而四层系统的响应可通过解耦的双层石墨烯（TBG）响应近似表达，且具有强烈的角度依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解交替扭转多层石墨烯系统在面内磁场下的轨道响应特性，特别是探索不同层数系统（四层和五层）的磁响应行为差异，以及这些系统在超导相变中的潜在应用。

Method: 采用Khalaf等人引入的幺正变换（unitary transformation），将交替扭转N层系统映射到N/2个解耦的扭转双层石墨烯（TBG）系统（具有不同有效扭转角），对于奇数N还包含一个单独解耦层，从而生成N/2个魔角（magic angles）的层次结构。

Result: 五层系统的轨道面内磁响应可忽略不计，且预期所有奇数层系统均具此性质。四层系统的面内轨道磁化率（orbital susceptibility）可近似用相应TBG响应表达：与自旋磁化率（spin susceptibility）相比很大，在魔角附近电荷中性点的清洁极限下甚至发散。响应具有强烈角度依赖性：在第一魔角处比TBG小约0.01倍，而在第二魔角处达到魔角TBG值的约3.6倍。

Conclusion: 研究引入了面内Maki参数（in-plane Maki parameter）作为正常态与超导态轨道磁化率差与顺磁Pauli磁化率（paramagnetic Pauli susceptibility）的比值，在TBG中魔角附近该值可达2。分析可扩展至其他响应函数，表明交替扭转多层系统中的不同有效魔角可能承载不同的超导相（superconducting phases）。

Abstract: We analytically study the orbital response of alternating-twist graphene systems with four and five layers to an in-plane magnetic field, using the unitary transformation introduced by Khalaf et al. (Phys. Rev. B 100, 085109 (2019)). This transformation maps an alternating-twist N-layer system onto N/2 decoupled twisted bilayer graphene (TBG) systems with distinct effective twist angles, together with a single decoupled layer for odd N, thereby generating a hierarchy of N/2 magic angles. For five layers, we find that the orbital in-plane magnetic response is negligibly small, and we expect this property to hold for all systems with an odd number of layers. For a tetralayer system, we approximately express the in-plane orbital susceptibility in terms of the corresponding TBG responses, which are large compared to the spin susceptibility and even diverge in the clean limit at charge neutrality near the magic angle. Remarkably, the in-plane magnetic response is strongly angle dependent: compared with TBG, it is about 0.01 times smaller at the first magic angle, whereas at the second it reaches about 3.6 times the value of magic angle TBG. We finally introduce the in-plane Maki parameter as the ratio between the difference in orbital susceptibility of the normal and superconducting states and the paramagnetic Pauli susceptibility. For TBG, we find values up to 2 near the magic angle. Our analysis can be extended to other response functions and suggests that the different effective magic angles in alternating-twist multilayers may host distinct superconducting phases.

</details>


### [77] [Topological superconductivity of a two-dimensional electron gas at the (001) LaAlO\textsubscript{3}/SrTiO\textsubscript{3} interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18621)
*Piotr Żeberek,Paweł Wójcik*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了LaAlO₃/SrTiO₃界面二维电子气中拓扑超导性和马约拉纳零模的出现，分析了二维和准一维几何结构中的拓扑相图，发现磁场取向和横向限制对拓扑相变和边缘模式性质有重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索LaAlO₃/SrTiO₃界面二维电子气中拓扑超导性和马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）的出现机制，特别关注不同几何结构和磁场条件对拓扑相变的影响。

Method: 采用包含t₂g轨道结构、原子自旋轨道耦合和Rashba自旋轨道耦合的现实多带紧束缚模型（multiband tight binding model），分析二维和准一维几何结构的拓扑相图，并研究不同宽度纳米线中的马约拉纳零模。

Result: 在二维极限下，需要有限的面外磁场分量驱动拓扑相变，临界场具有强能带依赖性；横向限制可放宽纯面内磁场无法诱导拓扑相变的约束；d_{yz/xz}轨道主导的子带表现出异常长的局域化长度，可能阻碍典型实验尺寸纳米线中马约拉纳束缚态的观测。

Conclusion: LaAlO₃/SrTiO₃界面系统的拓扑性质对几何结构和磁场取向高度敏感，d_{yz/xz}轨道主导子带的异常局域化特性对实验观测马约拉纳零模提出了挑战，为界面拓扑超导研究提供了重要理论指导。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of topological superconductivity and Majorana zero modes in the two-dimensional electron gas formed at the LaAlO$_3$/SrTiO$_3$ (001) interface. Using a realistic multiband tight binding model that incorporates the $t_{2g}$ orbital structure together with atomic and Rashba spin-orbit couplings, we determine the topological phase diagrams for both fully two-dimensional and quasi-one-dimensional geometries. In the two-dimensional limit, we show that a finite out-of-plane magnetic-field component is required to drive a topological phase transition. In this case, the critical field is strongly band dependent, and for higher-lying bands, it is controlled by the interplay of spin and orbital Zeeman effects, as well as atomic spin-orbit coupling. Although a purely in-plane field is insufficient to induce the topological transition in a full 2D system, we demonstrate that a lateral confinement relaxes this constraint. In this case, the character of the edge modes depends sensitively on the field orientation, with out-of-plane fields producing conventional counterpropagating chiral modes and transverse in-plane fields giving rise to co-propagating antichiral modes. Finally, Majorana zero modes in LAO/STO nanowires with varying widths are analyzed. We demonstrate that subbands predominantly composed of $d_{yz/xz}$ orbitals exhibit exceptionally long localization lengths, which may preclude the observation of Majorana bound states in nanowires of typical experimental dimensions.

</details>


### [78] [Extended saddle points govern long-lived antiskyrmions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18682)
*Megha Arya,Moritz A. Goerzen,Lionel Calmels,Shiwei Zhu,Bhanu Jai Singh,Stefan Heinze,Dongzhe Li*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现长寿命纳米磁孤子（magnetic solitons）面临核心挑战，因为其寿命通常随温度升高而急剧下降。研究旨在探索通过改变过渡态几何而非单纯提高能垒来增强孤子稳定性的新范式。

Method: 开发了基于自旋螺旋（spin spirals）的第一性原理方法，计算超越各向同性近似的DMI，解析其任意最近邻的完整方向依赖性。将该方法应用于实验可及的范德华磁体氧化Fe₃GeTe₂（FGT-O）。

Result: aDMI在低外磁场下稳定了能垒超过120 meV的纳米反斯格明子（antiskyrmions）。扩展鞍点完全抑制了激活速率中的熵贡献，使寿命基本与温度无关，在室温下比传统超薄膜斯格明子系统寿命提升超过五个数量级。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了一种通过过渡态几何（transition-state geometry）而非能垒高度来增强孤子稳定性的新范式，并确定了扩展鞍点出现的一般条件，为具有温度无关前置因子的孤子衰变路径建立了通用途径。

Abstract: Achieving long-lived nanoscale magnetic solitons remains a central challenge, as their lifetimes typically decrease rapidly with temperature. Here, we demonstrate that anisotropic Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction (aDMI) enables spatially extended saddle points (SPs) that fundamentally alter thermally activated decay. In contrast to conventional localized SPs, these extended configurations completely suppress the entropic contribution to the activation rate, rendering the lifetimes effectively temperature independent. To establish this mechanism, we develop a first-principles method based on spin spirals to compute DMI beyond the isotropic approximation, resolving its full directional dependence for arbitrary nearest neighbors. We apply this method to oxidized Fe$_3$GeTe$_2$ (FGT-O), an experimentally accessible van der Waals magnet. Oxygen adsorption simultaneously breaks inversion symmetry and lowers the in-plane crystalline symmetry, thereby generating a sizable aDMI. We demonstrate that aDMI stabilizes nanoscale antiskyrmions with energy barriers exceeding 120 meV at low external magnetic fields. Crucially, extended SPs enhance the lifetime in FGT-O by more than five orders of magnitude at room temperature compared to conventional ultrathin-film skyrmion systems. We further show that aDMI is not the only route to such extended SPs and identify the general conditions under which they emerge, establishing a general route to soliton decay pathways with temperature-independent prefactors. Our results uncover a new paradigm for enhancing soliton stability through transition-state geometry rather than energy-barrier height.

</details>


### [79] [Time reversal reserved spin valve and spin transistor based on unconventional $p$-wave magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18685)
*Ze-Yong Yuan,Jun-Feng Liu,Pei-Hao Fu,Jun Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出基于非常规p波磁体（UPMs）的自旋阀和自旋晶体管设计，利用各向异性自旋分裂实现无需净磁化或相对论性自旋轨道耦合的自旋电子功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非常规磁体中的各向异性自旋分裂（anisotropic spin splitting）为实现不依赖净磁化或相对论性自旋轨道耦合的自旋电子功能提供了新机遇。本研究旨在探索基于非常规p波磁体（unconventional p-wave magnets, UPMs）的自旋电子器件设计。

Method: 提出两种器件设计：自旋阀（spin valve）采用两个UPMs夹着正常金属的结结构，其交换场强度矢量（exchange-field strength vectors）垂直于结方向；自旋晶体管（spin transistor）则将中心正常金属替换为另一个UPM，该UPM具有纵向取向的强度矢量和垂直的自旋极化轴。

Result: 自旋阀的电导由两个UPMs的自旋排列决定：平行排列时自旋态对齐实现高效电子传输，呈现高电导态；反平行排列时相反的自旋取向抑制电导。自旋晶体管中的中心UPM使所有横向模式具有相同进动频率的均匀自旋进动（uniform spin precession）。两种器件均可通过调制UPMs的强度矢量进行电控。

Conclusion: 这些发现确立了UPMs作为开发无需净磁化或相对论性自旋轨道耦合的自旋电子器件的有前景平台，为新型自旋电子功能实现提供了替代方案。

Abstract: The anisotropic spin splitting in unconventional magnets opens new opportunities for realizing spintronic functionalities without relying on net magnetization or relativistic spin-orbit coupling. Here, we propose a spin valve and a spin transistor based on unconventional $p$-wave magnets (UPMs). The spin valve is realized in a junction where a normal metal is sandwiched between two UPMs whose exchange-field strength vectors are oriented transverse to the junction direction. The conductance of such a device is governed by the spin alignment between two UPMs: when their strength vectors are parallel, the spin-state alignment enables efficient electron transmission, leading to a high-conductance state; in contrast, the antiparallel configuration suppresses the conductance owing to the opposite spin orientations. Furthermore, the spin-valve can be extended to a spin transistor by replacing the central normal metal with another UPM with a longitudinally oriented strength vector and a perpendicular spin polarization axis. The central UPM enables uniform spin precession with the same precession frequency for all transverse modes. Both devices can be electrically controlled by modulating the strength vectors of UPMs. These findings establish UPMs as a promising platform for developing spintronic devices without net magnetization or relativistic spin-orbit coupling.

</details>


### [80] [Reversible Steady Domain-Wall Motion Driven by a Direct Current](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18722)
*K. Y. Jing,X. R. Wang,H. Y. Yuan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究发现在角动量补偿点附近的亚铁磁体中，畴壁可以在直流电流驱动下实现正向或反向的稳定传播，其运动方向仅由电流强度控制，打破了传统磁系统中惯性仅影响瞬态动力学的范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解和操控纳米尺度畴壁（domain wall, DW）动力学是磁学和自旋电子学领域的核心课题，因其在逻辑和存储器件中具有广阔应用前景。传统磁系统中惯性主要影响瞬态动力学，而长期畴壁运动仅由外加电流的大小和方向决定，本研究旨在探索这一范式在特定条件下的突破。

Method: 研究聚焦于角动量补偿点（angular momentum compensation point）附近的亚铁磁体（ferrimagnets），通过分析畴壁内部集体坐标（collective coordinate）的惯性动力学行为。该集体坐标表现为在电流依赖的双势阱（double-well potential）中演化的有质量物体，其稳定状态由驱动电流决定。

Result: 研究证明畴壁可以在直流电流（direct current）驱动下实现正向或反向的稳定传播，运动方向完全由电流强度控制。这一反常现象源于畴壁内部集体坐标的惯性动力学，系统会根据驱动电流弛豫到与相反运动方向相关的不同稳定状态。

Conclusion: 该发现揭示了惯性在非线性自旋动力学中的意外作用，为实现低能耗自旋电子学功能提供了新途径，包括灵敏的磁场检测和可重构的单端口器件（one-port devices）。

Abstract: Understanding and manipulating nanoscale domain wall (DW) dynamics is a central topic in magnetism and spintronics for its promising applications in logic and memory devices. In most magnetic systems, inertia affects only transient DW dynamics, while the long-time DW motion is uniquely determined by the magnitude and direction of the applied current. Here we show that this paradigm breaks down in ferrimagnets near the angular momentum compensation point. We demonstrate that a DW can propagate steadily either forward or backward even under a direct current, with the direction controlled solely by the current strength. This anomalous phenomenon originates from the inertial dynamics of an internal DW collective coordinate, which behaves as a massive object evolving in a current-dependent double-well potential. Depending on the driving current, the system relaxes into distinct stable states associated with opposite directions of motion. Our findings reveal an unexpected role of inertia in nonlinear spin dynamics, and enable low-energy spintronic functionalities including sensitive magnetic-field detection and reconfigurable one-port devices.

Conclusion: 该效应源于量子点中电子态的几何形状，电流受限于本征态相关的隧穿速率，即人工σ-耦合和π-耦合机制。

Abstract: We fabricated a quantum dot coupled laterally to a two-dimensional electron gas and vertically to a three-dimensional electron gas in order to investigate the eigenstate dependence of tunneling rate to these gases. We observed a bias-dependent ``geometric" current blockade. By tunneling via the asymmetric couplings, population inversion is induced and a dark metastable triplet state is revealed. The metastable state stops the current transport process, suppresses the current and asymmetrically widens the Coulomb diamond. By analyzing the current as a function of source-drain and gate voltage and the magnetic field, we concluded that this effect is due to the geometric shape of the electronic states in the dot and the current is limited by the tunneling rate due to the eigenstates, that is, artificial $σ$-coupling and $π$-coupling.

### [83] [Longitudinal Nonreciprocal Charge Transport with Time Reversal Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18823)
*Harsh Varshney,Amit Agarwal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新的纵向非互易电荷输运机制：在非磁性导体中，即使没有磁场和时间反演对称性破缺，通过无序诱导的不对称散射也能产生纵向非互易响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为纵向非互易电荷输运需要时间反演对称性破缺，通常存在于磁性材料或外加磁场中。本研究旨在探索在非磁性导体中实现纵向非互易性的可能性，挑战现有理论框架。

Method: 采用半经典玻尔兹曼（Boltzmann）框架，建立了一个通用理论，其中斜散射（skew-scattering）和侧跳（side-jump）过程产生非线性纵向电流。通过系统对称性分析识别了42个允许这种外禀机制的点群。

Conclusion: 研究确立了无序驱动的不对称散射作为晶体导体中体纵向非互易电荷输运的通用机制，扩展了非互易输运现象的理论基础，为时间反演对称系统中的非线性输运提供了新视角。

Abstract: Longitudinal nonreciprocal charge transport is widely believed to require time-reversal symmetry breaking, either in magnetic materials or through external magnetic fields. Here, we show that longitudinal nonreciprocity can arise even in nonmagnetic conductors without magnetic fields through disorder-induced asymmetric scattering. Using a semiclassical Boltzmann framework, we develop a general theory in which skew-scattering and side-jump processes generate a nonlinear longitudinal current that remains finite even in time-reversal-symmetric systems. A systematic symmetry analysis identifies 42 point groups that permit this extrinsic mechanism. As a concrete realization, we demonstrate that Bernal-stacked bilayer graphene exhibits a large and gate-tunable longitudinal nonreciprocal response with a sizable nonreciprocity factor near its Lifshitz transition. These results establish disorder-driven asymmetric scattering as a general mechanism for bulk longitudinal nonreciprocal charge transport in crystalline conductors.

*Wei Jia*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究发现仅用欧拉特征数（Euler characteristic）$χ_F$不足以完整表征费米海（Fermi sea）拓扑结构，提出了结构分辨率因子（structural resolution factor）来捕捉费米海的精细拓扑结构，并展示了这些结构如何影响拓扑超导相的边界态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 费米海几何承载着独特的量子拓扑形式，但仅用欧拉特征数$χ_F$表征费米海拓扑是不充分的，因为具有相同$χ_F$的费米海可能存在本质上不同的精细拓扑结构，这些结构无法通过Lifshitz transition相互连接。

Method: 引入结构分辨率因子（structural resolution factor）来编码超越$χ_F$的精细费米海拓扑结构，并考虑费米面上的吸引Hubbard相互作用（attractive Hubbard interaction）来研究拓扑超导相。

Result: 拓扑超导相能够继承其正常填充能带（normal filled bands）的精细费米海拓扑结构，不同结构之间的差异会在金属-超导体异质结（metal-superconductor heterojunctions）界面处产生反常无能隙边界态（anomalous gapless boundary states）。

Conclusion: 这项工作为理解费米海的拓扑丰富性开辟了新途径，揭示了超越传统欧拉特征数的精细拓扑结构在量子物质研究中的重要性。

Abstract: The geometry of Fermi sea hosts a unique form of quantum topology that governs the conductance quantization of metal and is characterized by the Euler characteristic $χ_F$, offering a new perspective in the study of topological quantum matter. Here, we discover that characterizing Fermi sea topology solely by $χ_F$ is insufficient: Fermi seas with identical $χ_F$ can exhibit fundamentally different fine-grained topological structures that cannot be connected without a Lifshitz transition. To encode this hidden structure, we introduce a structural resolution factor that captures the fine-grained Fermi sea topologies beyond $χ_F$. Considering the attractive Hubbard interaction of electrons on Fermi surfaces, we further demonstrate that the resulting topological superconducting phases can inherit the fine-grained Fermi sea topology of their normal filled bands, with differences in these structures giving rise to anomalous gapless boundary states at the interface between two metal-superconductor heterojunctions. This work opens an avenue for understanding the topological richness of Fermi sea.

Conclusion: MBBE框架为贵金属中电子过程的微观描述提供了有力工具，能够揭示传统唯象模型无法捕捉的微观机制，特别是费米面几何结构对各向异性光学响应的重要影响。

Abstract: In this paper we introduce momentum-resolved metal Boltzmann-Bloch equations (MBBE) for the combined description of electronic intra- and interband processes in noble metals. This microscopic framework incorporates a full treatment of many-body electron-electron and electron-phonon interactions, relevant for relaxation and dephasing processes after optical excitation. For the example of gold, we calculate the linear optical response for near-infrared and visible energies. This provides insight into the interplay of microscopic processes hidden in phenomenological Drude-Lorentz models. The complex geometry of the Fermi surface is treated by an anisotropic electronic dispersion model, which is necessary to explain the temperature dependent spectrum over the whole frequency range of intra- and interband transitions.

### [86] [Peltier cooling in Corbino-geometry quantum Hall systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18922)
*Akira Endo,Yoshiaki Hashimoto*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究分析了Corbino几何量子霍尔系统中径向Peltier系数Π_rr的理论特性，并通过实验测量验证了大|Π_rr|值导致的Peltier效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Corbino几何的量子霍尔系统在量子霍尔平台区域预期具有大的Peltier系数Π_rr，研究旨在理论分析该系数的特性并尝试实验观测其效应。

Method: 基于自洽玻恩近似（self-consistent Born approximation）获得的光谱电导率，推导出Π_rr的解析公式；同时通过实验测量Corbino圆盘外缘的电子温度T_out，施加径向直流电流I_dc来观测Peltier效应。

Result: 理论分析显示Π_rr在整数朗道能级填充附近具有大的负（正）值，其绝对值|Π_rr|随温度降低或无序度减小而增加；实验观测到T_out随I_dc方向和Π_rr符号的变化而变化，在特定条件下T_out甚至低于环境温度。

Conclusion: 研究成功建立了Corbino几何量子霍尔系统中径向Peltier系数的理论框架，并通过实验初步验证了大|Π_rr|值导致的Peltier冷却/加热效应，为后续相关研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Quantum Hall systems having Corbino geometry are expected to have a large Peltier coefficient $Π_{rr}$ in the quantum Hall plateau region. We present an analytic formula for $Π_{rr}$ calculated employing the spectral conductivity obtained based on the self-consistent Born approximation. The coefficient $Π_{rr}$ is shown to have a large negative (positive) value just above (below) an integer Landau-level filling, with the absolute value $|Π_{rr}|$ increasing with decreasing temperature or decreasing disorder, and approaching the saw-tooth shape $- (E_{N_\mathrm{F} σ_\mathrm{F}}-ζ)/e$ in the limit of vanishing disorder, where $E_{N_\mathrm{F} σ_\mathrm{F}}$ is the highest occupied Landau level and $ζ$ is the chemical potential. As an initial attempt to experimentally observe the effect of the large $|Π_{rr}|$, we measure the electron temperature $T_\mathrm{out}$ near the outer perimeter of a Corbino disk, applying a radial dc current $I_\mathrm{dc}$. The temperature $T_\mathrm{out}$ is observed to increase or decrease depending on the direction of $I_\mathrm{dc}$ and the sign of $Π_{rr}$ as expected from the Peltier effect. Notably, $T_\mathrm{out}$ becomes lower than the bath temperature for outward (inward) $I_\mathrm{dc}$ in the region where $Π_{rr} < 0$ ($Π_{rr} > 0$).

</details>

Motivation: No AI summary available.

Method: No AI summary available.

Result: No AI summary available.

Conclusion: No AI summary available.

Abstract: The ductile-to-brittle transition (DBT) in body-centred cubic systems is a central design constraint for cryogenic structures. Performing parametric studies to enhance the understanding on DBT using fully coupled thermomechanical continuum DBT models is computationally expensive. Therefore, in this work, a lightweight phase-field surrogate is proposed. This surrogate approach captures key \emph{DBT-like} trends within a standard isothermal two-field (displacement--damage) setting by prescribing temperature dependence through three phenomenological mechanisms: (i) a temperature-dependent degradation exponent $n(T)$ that sharpens stiffness loss from gradual (ductile-like, $n=2.0$ at 293\,K) to abrupt (brittle-like, $n=3.5$ at 77\,K), (ii) temperature-dependent yield stress and elastic modulus to modulate the balance between plastic dissipation and elastic energy storage, and (iii) an effective fracture toughness and driving-force scaling to represent reduced crack-tip shielding at cryogenic temperatures. The model is implemented in FEniCSx using small-strain $J_2$ return mapping and a staggered solution scheme. Simulations of a single-edge-notched specimen over 77--293\,K demonstrate a systematic progression from brittle-like to ductile-like response, characterised by reduced displacement to unstable fracture, a transition from abrupt post-peak load drop to extended softening, and a shift from narrow, localised damage bands with confined plasticity to broader process zones. A sensitivity study comparing four interpolation schemes (linear, smoothstep, exponential, hybrid) shows that the qualitative transition trends are robust, with interpolation primarily affecting intermediate-temperature responses while endpoint behaviours remain unchanged.

</details>


### [88] [Polarization Dynamics in Ferroelectrics: Insights Enabled by Machine Learning Molecular Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18058)
*Dongyu Bai,Ri He,Junxian Liu,Liangzhi Kou*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该视角论文综述了机器学习分子动力学（MLMD）在铁电材料极化动力学模拟中的优势与应用进展，同时指出了当前方法学挑战及未来发展方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁电材料的性能与稳定性受极化动力学和畴动力学控制，但由于实验表征技术的原子级限制，需要高精度原子模拟。第一性原理计算在时空尺度上受限，难以捕捉动态过程的复杂特征。

Method: 机器学习分子动力学（machine learning molecular dynamics, MLMD）通过将量子力学精度编码到力场中，实现了具有接近第一性原理精度的大规模动态模拟。

Result: MLMD在模拟极化翻转、畴成核与迁移、拓扑极性结构以及曲率驱动铁电现象方面展现出优势，论文系统综述了这些领域的最新进展。

Conclusion: 需要解决长程静电、多铁材料中晶格-自旋耦合自由度以及大原子模型的数据高效预训练等方法学挑战，相应的进展将使MLMD成为铁电和多铁材料设计的真正预测性框架。

Abstract: Ferroelectric materials with switchable spontaneous polarization underpin non-volatile memories, transistors, sensors, and emerging neuromorphic chips. Their performance and stability are governed by polarization dynamics and domain kinetics, making a microscopic understanding of these processes and precise atomic level control of polarization domains key challenges for next-generation ferroelectric electronics. Due to the limitations of the characterization technology with atomic level in experiment, high precision atomic simulations become important. First principles calculations are inherently limited in accessible length and time scales, making it difficult to capture the complex features of dynamic processes. Machine learning molecular dynamics (MLMD) offers a compelling solution by encoding quantum-mechanical accuracy into force fields, thereby enabling large scale dynamic simulations with near first-principles fidelity. This Perspective highlights the advantages of MLMD for simulating polarization switching, domain nucleation and migration, topological polar textures and curvature-driven ferroelectric phenomena, while providing a systematic overview of recent progress in these areas. We further discuss methodological challenges that limit predictive capability, including long range electrostatics, coupled lattice-spin degrees of freedom in multiferroics, and data efficient pre-training of large atomistic models. Corresponding advances in long range aware force fields, spin dependent machine learning models, and large scale pretraining are expected to move MLMD toward a genuinely predictive framework for the design of ferroelectric and multiferroic materials.

</details>

Abstract: Halide perovskites have revolutionized optoelectronics by demonstrating that long carrier lifetime can be achieved in materials processed in relatively uncontrolled environments, whereas conventional inorganic semiconductors typically suffer from short carrier lifetime unless very carefully prepared and postprocessed. Here, we report the discovery of exceptionally long photoexcited carrier lifetime in monoclinic ZnP2, effectively bridging the carrier lifetime gap between direct-gap inorganic semiconductors and halide perovskites. Conclusion: 形态控制与优化的淬火-减压条件相结合，能够促进纳米碳同素异形体的选择性合成。该研究为极端条件下纳米碳结构的可控合成提供了理论指导和预测工具。

Here, we employ GPU-accelerated ReaxFF simulations to investigate the graphitization and structural remodeling of detonation nanodiamond under nonlinear quench and pressure-release conditions. We further investigate how the initial nanodiamond morphology influences the resulting transformation products. Evolution of nanostructure, allotrope, carbon hybridization, and ring statistics are tracked. Rapid cooling combined with slow decompression optimizes cubic diamond retention, whereas slow cooling with rapid pressure release promotes surface-to-core graphitization, producing concentric sp2 layers and hollowed inner shells. Octahedral nanodiamonds evolve into carbon nano-onions, initially forming bucky diamonds that progressively transform into full sp2 structures, while hexagonal prisms preferentially form parallel-stacked graphite layers resembling carbon dots. Lonsdaleite emerges as an interfacial phase, suggesting potential reversibility in the shock-induced graphite-to-diamond transformation pathway transformation route. To extend predictive capabilities, we trained MLP regressors on over 10^5 node-hours of simulations. Collectively, morphological control combined with optimized quench-decompression conditions promote the selective synthesis of nanocarbon allotropes.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶体中的扩散通过缺陷介导的原子跳跃已被定量理解，但玻璃中缺乏可比的定量框架。这些系统中大扩散激活能的起源仍然令人困惑，尽管局部重排涉及低势垒。

Method: 使用金属玻璃的分子动力学模拟，将扩散分解为随机行走和相关性贡献，分析前后相关运动对激活能的影响。

Result: 发现前后相关运动主导激活能，而非局部重排势垒；这种相关性源于无序能量景观中正向和反向势垒的不对称性。该机制在SiO2和单组分Lennard-Jones玻璃中同样存在，表明相关性源于结构无序而非化学复杂性。

Conclusion: 该框架建立了原子尺度动力学与宏观输运之间的直接定量联系，为无序材料中的动力学提供了预测基础，并能解释表面扩散加速现象。

Abstract: While diffusion in crystalline solids is quantitatively understood through defect-mediated atomic hops, no comparable quantitative framework exists for glasses. In these systems, the origin of large diffusion activation energies remains puzzling, despite local rearrangements involving low barriers. Using molecular dynamics simulations of metallic glasses, we decompose diffusion into random-walk and correlation contributions and find that back-and-forth correlated motion, not local rearrangement barriers, dominates the activation energy, resolving how low-barrier rearrangements yield large macroscopic activation energies. These correlations arise from asymmetry between forward and reverse barriers, a generic feature of disordered energy landscapes. We find that the correlation-driven mechanism is active beyond metallic glass alloys, including SiO2 and a single-component Lennard-Jones glass. The latter demonstrates that the correlation originates from structural disorder rather than chemical complexity. The framework also explains accelerated surface diffusion, where reduced activation energies arise primarily from weaker correlations rather than changes in local rearrangement barriers. Our results establish a direct, quantitative link between atomic-scale dynamics and macroscopic transport, providing a predictive basis for kinetics in disordered materials.

The results reveal that non-Arrhenius grain growth is a thermally activated process without a definitive characteristic temperature, which is primarily controlled by the interplay between temperature-dependent factors and the temperature-independent parameters such as grain size and its distribution. Moreover, during abnormal grain growth (AGG), the non-Arrhenius behavior of grain growth primarily occurs at lower temperatures and gradually transitions to Arrhenius-type behavior as the temperature increases.

DeePAW is currently the best OFDFT ML model according to the three criterions, 1) covering the largest number of elements, 2) having the widest application capability to diverse crystal structures, and 3) achieving the highest prediction accuracy without further fine-tuning. ### [96] [The influence of nonradiative relaxation on laser induced white emission properties in Cr:YAG nanopowders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18664)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激光诱导白光发射（Laser Induced White Emission, LIWE）虽已在全球范围内得到研究并实现工业应用，但对现象本质的理解不足限制了其潜力。本文旨在探究非辐射弛豫过程对Cr:YAG纳米粉末中LIWE特性的影响。

Conclusion: 非辐射弛豫过程对LIWE特性具有显著影响，铬浓度的变化通过改变非辐射复合概率来调控参与LIWE过程的光子数。提出的多光子电离模型为理解LIWE现象提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Laser Induced White Emission (LIWE) is the subject of research worldwide. This article is devoted to the study of the influence of nonradiative relaxation processes on the properties of laser induced white emission in Cr:YAG nanopowders. Method: 本研究提出了一种简单的度量指标"声子带中心（PBC）"，该描述符封装了与声子散射物理相关的关键因素。首先在黄铜矿类材料中建立该指标，随后使用实验晶格热导率数据在各类材料中进行验证。

Abstract: Understanding anharmonicity is crucial for designing materials with desired lattice thermal conductivity. This work proposes a simple metric that helps explain the diversity in lattice thermal conductivity (kl) among materials by quantifying their anharmonic effects. This descriptor "phonon band center" (PBC) encapsulates the critical factors associated with the physics of phonon scattering, revealing a simple inverse relationship with the Gruneisen parameter, the response of phonons with changing volume, and strong correlation with lattice thermal conductivity. This metric has been established using the chalcopyrite class of materials and subsequently validated across various classes of materials using experimental kl. Our approach effectively differentiates materials based on PBC, thereby streamlining the identification of candidates with desirable kl.

### [102] [Bridging Crystal Structure and Material Properties via Bond-Centric Descriptors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18876)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究引入了MattKeyBond数据库，这是一个以键合为中心的材料数据库，显式地映射材料的局域电子景观和键合相互作用。在此基础上提出了键合吸引性（Bonding Attractivity, BA）描述符，这是一种新颖的元素特异性描述符，用于量化原子形成共价网络的内在能力。

Result: 通过提供预先计算的、能量维度的键合描述符，MattKeyBond将隐式的"黑箱"转化为物理可解释的特征。这一策略减轻了机器学习模型从纯几何结构中推导物理规律的负担，即使在数据有限的情况下也能实现准确预测。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了电子结构理论与现代人工智能工作流的无缝集成，为数据驱动材料科学提供了物理可解释的中间特征，解决了当前机器学习模型在化学键合处理上的局限性。

Abstract: Although chemical bonding is the fundamental mechanistic bridge connecting atomic structure to macroscopic material properties, current data-driven materials science largely treats it as an implicit "black box". Existing machine learning (ML) models rely predominantly on geometric coordinates, forcing them to implicitly relearn complex quantum mechanics from scratch. This lack of intermediate physical features limits model interpretability and generalizability, particularly when training data is scarce. To solve this problem, we introduce MattKeyBond, a bond-centric materials database that explicitly maps the local electronic landscape and bonding interactions of materials. Building on this, we propose Bonding Attractivity (BA), a novel element-specific descriptor that quantifies the intrinsic capability of atoms to form covalent networks. By providing pre-calculated, energy-dimensional bonding descriptors, MattKeyBond transforms the implicit "black box" into physically interpretable features. This strategy relieves ML models from the burden of deducing physical laws from pure geometry, enabling accurate predictions even with limited data and seamlessly integrating electronic structure theory into modern AI workflows.

### [103] [Microscopic Origin of Temperature-Dependent Anisotropic Heat Transport in Ultrawide-Bandgap Rutile GeO2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18885)
*Pouria Emtenani,Marta Loletti,Felix Nippert,Eduardo Bede Barros,Zbigniew Galazka,Hans Tornatzky,Christian Thomsen,Juan Sebastian Reparaz,Riccardo Rurali,Markus R. Wagner*

TL;DR: 本文通过实验与理论结合的方法，系统研究了超宽带隙金红石相GeO₂的热输运特性，揭示了其各向异性热导率的微观起源和温度依赖性，为该材料在功率电子器件中的应用提供了热管理基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超宽带隙（ultrawide-bandgap）金红石相GeO₂作为功率电子器件的有前景半导体材料，其高效散热对于抑制自热效应和确保器件可靠性至关重要。然而，其各向异性热输运的温度依赖性和微观起源在实验上尚未得到解决。

Method: 采用温度依赖的时域热反射（time-domain thermoreflectance）测量结合第一性原理声子输运计算，量化了单晶金红石相GeO₂在80-350 K温度范围内沿[001]和[110]方向的热导率。通过模式分辨分析揭示了热输运的微观机制。

Result: 在295 K时，沿[001]方向的热导率达到47.5 W m⁻¹ K⁻¹，沿[110]方向为32.5 W m⁻¹ K⁻¹，各向异性比为1.46，与理论预测吻合良好。热导率表现出近似T^(-1.4)的温度依赖性，表明存在超出纯三声子限制输运的额外散射机制。

Conclusion: 室温下各向异性源于沿[001]方向更大的声子群速度（phonon group velocities）和方向依赖的声子寿命（phonon lifetimes）的联合效应。冷却过程中高频声子的去布居逐渐抑制了其对热输运的贡献并降低了各向异性。Al/金红石相GeO₂界面的温度依赖热边界电导表明主要为弹性界面输运，这些发现为金红石相GeO₂的体相和界面热输运建立了微观基础。

Abstract: Ultrawide-bandgap rutile GeO2 is emerging as a promising semiconductor for power electronics, where efficient heat dissipation is essential to suppress self-heating and ensure device reliability. However, the temperature dependence and microscopic origin of its anisotropic heat transport have remained experimentally unresolved. Here, temperature-dependent time-domain thermoreflectance measurements combined with first-principles phonon transport calculations are used to quantify the thermal conductivity of single-crystal rutile GeO2 from 80 to 350 K along [001] and [110]. At 295 K, the thermal conductivity reaches 47.5 W m^-1 K^-1 along [001] and 32.5 W m^-1 K^-1 along [110], corresponding to an anisotropy ratio of 1.46, in good agreement with theory. Rather than following a simple T^(-1) law, the thermal conductivity exhibits an approximate T^(-1.4) dependence, indicating additional scattering beyond purely three-phonon-limited transport. Mode-resolved analysis reveals that the room-temperature anisotropy originates from the combined effect of larger phonon group velocities along [001] and direction-dependent phonon lifetimes. Upon cooling, depopulation of high-frequency phonons progressively suppresses their contribution to heat transport and reduces the anisotropy. The temperature-dependent thermal boundary conductance of Al/rutile GeO2 interfaces is further resolved, and the scaled conductance indicates predominantly elastic interfacial transport. These findings establish the microscopic basis of bulk and interfacial heat transport in rutile GeO2 and position this material as a promising thermally robust platform for ultrawide-bandgap electronics.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子反常霍尔效应在磁性掺杂拓扑绝缘体（magnetically doped topological insulators）中已被观测到，但其磁性的确切性质仍不明确。实验证据同时支持长程和短程有序，需要澄清这些系统中的磁性本质。

Method: 采用扫描超导量子干涉仪显微镜（scanning superconducting quantum interference device microscopy）研究V掺杂(Bi,Sb)₂Te₃中的磁畴。通过成像杂散磁场（stray magnetic fields）随外加磁场的变化，映射磁反转过程中的畴形成与演化。

Result: 磁畴与晶粒尺寸相似，磁反转通过畴扩张（domain expansion）而非随机位点成核发生。测量揭示了晶粒内局部磁相互作用与晶粒间长程铁磁耦合（long-range ferromagnetic coupling）的共存。

Conclusion: V掺杂(Bi,Sb)₂Te₃的磁行为与先前报道的Cr掺杂(Bi,Sb)₂Te₃显著不同，表现为典型的铁磁体磁反转机制和独特的磁耦合特征。

Abstract: The quantum anomalous Hall effect has been observed in several magnetically doped topological insulators, where its robustness and macroscopic magnetization properties have been taken to suggest the presence of long-range ferromagnetic order. However, experiments in such systems have found evidence for both long- and short-range order, leaving the precise nature of the magnetism in these systems unclear. Here, we use scanning superconducting quantum interference device microscopy to study magnetic domains in V-doped (Bi,Sb)$_2$Te$_3$ exhibiting a quantum anomalous Hall effect with precise quantization. By imaging stray magnetic fields as a function of applied field, we map the formation and evolution of domains through magnetic reversal. We reconstruct the magnetization configuration underlying the measured stray field and find that magnetic domains and crystallographic grains are of similar size. Moreover, magnetic reversal is found to occur through domain expansion, typical of ferromagnets, rather than through nucleation at random sites. Our measurements thus reveal a coexistence of both local magnetic interactions within crystallographic grains and long-range ferromagnetic coupling between grains. This behavior in V-doped (Bi,Sb)$_2$Te$_3$ is markedly distinct from that previously reported for Cr-doped (Bi,Sb)$_2$Te$_3$.

</details>


### [105] [Deterministic nucleation of nanocrystal superlattices on 2D perovskites for light-funneling heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18959)
*Umberto Filippi,Alexander Schleusener,Simone Lauciello,Roman Krahne,Dmitry Baranov,Liberato Manna,Masaru Kuno*

Result: 异质结构可作为高效光收集系统，实现从二维微晶域到超晶格的能量转移（energy transfer），并通过调节激发通量（excitation fluence）在线性和非线性载流子复合（carrier recombination）机制间切换；利用CsPbBr3纳米晶发射寿命随温度降低而缩短的特性，确保能量转移发生在纳米晶的双激子和单激子衰减之后，有效延长了超晶格的辐射复合。

Conclusion: 该方法简单有效且具有普适性，有望扩展到多种其他材料体系，为构建复杂异质结构提供了新途径，并展示了在光收集和能量转移应用中的潜力。

Abstract: Semiconductor heterostructures that combine components with different dimensionality provide an interesting way to manipulate the physical properties of the resulting material. Two-dimensional lead halide perovskites crystallize as flat microcrystals and have efficient in-plane exciton mobility, while perovskite nanocrystals are efficient emitters with a tunable bandgap that can self-assemble into microscopic superlattices. However, combining such intricate architectures into heterostructures has been challenging due to the mismatch in solubility properties and the challenging transfer procedures. Here we realize heterostructures where CsPbBr3 nanocrystal superlattices are deterministically grown along the faces of PEA2PbBr4 two-dimensional layered perovskite microcrystals. The growth can be limited to the lateral faces of the microcrystals and result in core-crown epitaxial heterostructures, or extended to the vertical direction leading to core-shell-like structures. The growth method is simple yet effective and versatile, and promises to be expanded to a large variety of other materials. We demonstrate that these heterostructures can be employed as efficient light-harvesting systems. In fact, energy can be transferred from the two-dimensional microcrystal domain to the superlattices, enabling switching between linear and non-linear carrier recombination regimes by tuning the excitation fluence. Moreover, by exploiting the lifetime shortening of CsPbBr3 nanocrystal emission upon sample cooling, we ensure that energy transfer occurs after the biexcitonic and single-excitonic decays of the nanocrystals, effectively extending the radiative recombination of superlattices.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合自旋与磁群论（magnetic group theory）对极性对称破缺的起源进行系统分类，区分晶格、交换或自旋轨道驱动的机制。通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）验证理论预测。

Abstract: Couplings between ferroelectric and magnetic orders offer promising routes toward low-dissipation electronics. However, such couplings are notably rare, largely due to the poor compatibility between insulating band structures and ferromagnetism. Here, we study a different strategy: we identify previously overlooked time-reversal-symmetric $p$- and $f$-wave spin-polarized insulating electronic states in ferroelectrics with noncollinear magnetic sublattices. We show that combining spin and magnetic group theory enables a systematic classification of the origin of polar symmetry breaking. We distinguish crystallographic, exchange-, or spin-orbit-driven mechanisms. Furthermore, we identify more than 50 candidate materials. Using first-principles calculations, we demonstrate a pristine, time-reversal-symmetric $p$-wave spin-polarized electronic structure in the well-known multiferroic $\mathrm{GdMn_2O_5}$. We further show that its $p$-wave order can be switched electrically, opening alternative paths toward spintronic and multiferroic functionalities in this class of materials.

### [107] [Photoferroelectric Coupling and Polarization-Controlled Interfacial Band Modulation in van der Waal Compound CuInP2S6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19148)
*Subhashree Chatterjee,Rabindra Basnet,Rajeev Nepal,Ramesh C. Budhani*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用相关开尔文探针力显微镜（Kelvin probe force microscopy）、压电力显微镜（piezoresponse force microscopy）和导电原子力显微镜（conductive atomic force microscopy）在带隙以上光照条件下进行测量。这些技术揭示了光照诱导的表面功函数增强、持续表面光电压、降低的矫顽场和正印记位移。

Conclusion: 研究确立了光-铁电-离子耦合作为CuInP2S6中光控能带调制和极化稳定性的主导机制，为基于层状铁离子材料的光可寻址铁电存储器、光电子开关和神经形态器件设计提供了纳米尺度框架。

Abstract: Understanding how optical excitation couples with polarization and interfacial electrostatics in van der Waals (vdW) ferroelectrics (FEs) is essential for the development of light-programmable nanoelectronic and optoelectronic devices. Here, we present direct nanoscale evidence of photoferroionic coupling in the vdW FE semiconductor CuInP2S6 (CIPS), where optical excitation jointly modulates electronic band bending, FE switching, and Cu+ ionic relaxation. The use of correlated Kelvin probe force microscopy, piezoresponse force microscopy, and conductive atomic force microscopy under above-bandgap illumination reveals illumination-induced enhancement of surface work function, persistent surface photovoltage, reduced coercive field, and positive imprint shifts. These effects arise from synergistic photocarrier redistribution and slow Cu+ migration that reshape interfacial depletion widths and internal electric fields. Illumination-assisted barrier lowering further enhances carrier injection and produces sweep-rate-dependent ferroionic transport hysteresis. Our results establish photoferroionic coupling as the governing mechanism for light-controlled band modulation and polarization stability in CIPS, providing a nanoscale framework for designing light-addressable FE memories, optoelectronic switches, and neuromorphic devices based on layered ferroionic materials.
