### [108] [Vortex Retention Mediated Turbulent Transitions in Self-Gravitating Bosonic and Axionic Condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18880)
*Anirudh Sivakumar,Sanjay Shukla,Rahul Pandit,Pankaj Kumar Mishra,Paulsamy Muruganandam*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究比较了自引力玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（self-gravitating Bose-Einstein condensates）中玻色子与轴子（axionic）系统的湍流自旋减速动力学，发现轴子系统密度分布更均匀、尺寸更小，且随着相互作用增强，其湍流谱偏离Kolmogorov标度律的趋势更显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于比较纯玻色子与轴子（高阶相互作用）自引力量子流体在湍流自旋减速过程中的动力学差异，探究不同非线性相互作用如何影响涡旋动力学和湍流耗散。

Method: 通过Gross-Pitaevskii-Poisson系统模拟，研究被壳层势（crust potential）固定的凝聚体经历快速旋转减速的过程，分析涡旋脱钉（vortex depinning）和湍流级联（turbulent cascade）。

Result: 轴子凝聚体在相似相互作用强度下表现出更均匀的密度分布和更小的尺寸，促进更早的涡旋进入。两种系统在可比尺寸下均呈现短暂的Kolmogorov能量级联（k^{-5/3}标度）后过渡到Vinen湍流（k^{-1}标度）。随着相互作用增强，轴子系统因涡旋保留增强而显著偏离Kolmogorov标度。谱分析显示不可压缩能量增长主要由量子压力驱动。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，不同的非线性相互作用主导着自引力量子流体中的涡旋动力学和湍流耗散过程，轴子系统的增强涡旋保留特性导致其湍流谱标度行为与玻色子系统存在显著差异。

Abstract: We investigate turbulent spin-down dynamics in self-gravitating Bose-Einstein condensates, comparing purely bosonic and axionic (higher-order interacting) systems. Through simulations of the Gross-Pitaevskii-Poisson system, we study condensates pinned to a crust potential undergoing rapid rotation slowdown. We find that axionic condensates exhibit more uniform density profiles and smaller sizes compared to their bosonic counterparts for similar interaction strengths, which facilitates earlier vortex entry. The sudden spin-down triggers vortex depinning and a turbulent cascade. For comparable sizes, both systems exhibit a short-lived Kolmogorov energy cascade ($k^{-5/3}$ scaling) followed by a transition to Vinen turbulence ($k^{-1}$ scaling). Crucially, their responses diverge with increasing interaction strength (and thus condensate size): the axionic system increasingly deviates from Kolmogorov scaling because of enhanced vortex retention, a trend quantitatively confirmed by analyzing the vortex fraction and its dependence on the final rotation frequency. Spectral analysis reveals that the growth of incompressible energy is primarily driven by quantum pressure during vortex detachment, rather than by compressible flows. The compressible spectrum shows thermalization ($k$ scaling). Our results demonstrate how distinct nonlinearities govern vortex dynamics and turbulent dissipation in self-gravitating quantum fluids.

</details>


### [109] [Anomalous Topological Bloch Oscillations under Non-Abelian Gauge Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19049)
*Chunyan Li,Ce Shang,Boris A. Malomed*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过调控Rashba和Dresselhaus自旋轨道耦合的相对强度，在蜂窝状Zeeman晶格中构建非阿贝尔规范场，实现了异常拓扑Bloch振荡，其表现出不对称运动特性，包括振荡周期一半的冻结效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑Bloch振荡作为量子输运现象的标志，是探测拓扑能带几何特性的有力动力学探针。自旋轨道耦合（SOC）已成为调控材料中量子态的关键要素，而Rashba和Dresselhaus相互作用产生的规范场机制尚需深入探索。

Method: 研究在蜂窝状Zeeman晶格中，通过Gross-Pitaevskii方程描述旋量波包的传播。通过调控Rashba和Dresselhaus自旋轨道耦合的相对强度，构建非阿贝尔规范场，从而驱动异常拓扑Bloch振荡。

Result: 与常规拓扑Bloch振荡不同，异常拓扑Bloch振荡表现出不对称运动特性，包括振荡周期一半的冻结效应。该效应可通过自旋轨道耦合参数和外部力进行调控，为非阿贝尔规范场控制拓扑量子动力学提供了有力机制。

Conclusion: 基于自旋轨道耦合的非阿贝尔规范场是控制拓扑量子动力学的强大机制，对自旋电子器件和量子数据处理具有重要应用前景。

Abstract: Topological Bloch oscillations are a hallmark of quantum transport phenomenon in which wavepackets undergo oscillatory motion driven by the interplay between an external force and topological edge states and serve as a powerful dynamical probe for the geometric properties of topological bands. Spin-orbit coupling (SOC) has also emerged as a crucial ingredient for manipulating quantum states in materials, with the corresponding gauge fields arising from the Rashba and Dresselhaus interactions. In this work, we investigate the propagation of spinor wavepackets in a honeycomb Zeeman lattice governed by the Gross-Pitaevskii equation. By tuning the relative strengths of Rashba and Dresselhaus SOC, we engineer a non-Abelian gauge field that drives anomalous topological Bloch oscillations (ATBOs). Unlike conventional topological Bloch oscillation (TBOs), these ATBOs exhibit asymmetric motion, including a freezing effect in one half of the oscillation cycle, which can be tuned by the SOC parameters and external forces. Our findings establish SOC-based non-Abelian gauge fields as a powerful mechanism controlling topological quantum dynamics, with implications for spintronic devices and quantum data processing.

Abstract: Models of interacting quantum spins are used in many areas of physics ranging from the study of magnetism and strongly correlated materials to quantum sensing. ### [111] [Rotation-triggered Kelvin-Helmholtz and counter-superflow instabilities in a three-component Bose-Einstein condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19207)
*Susovan Giri,Arpana Saboo,Hari Sadhan Ghosh,Vipin,Sonjoy Majumder*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了多组分超流体中界面流体动力学不稳定性，通过选择性旋转三组分玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体，实现了对剪切和对流不稳定机制的独立调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多组分超流体中的界面流体动力学不稳定性为探索超越经典流体类比（analogues）的非平衡量子动力学提供了多功能平台。研究旨在理解三组分凝聚体中两个界面上的相对运动如何调控不稳定性机制。

Method: 采用选择性旋转（selective rotation）协议，仅对中间组分施加旋转以在内外界面产生受控相对运动。使用流体动力学压力平衡（hydrodynamic pressure-balance）方法推导开尔文-亥姆霍兹不稳定性（Kelvin-Helmholtz instability）的起始条件，并通过含时格罗斯-皮塔耶夫斯基（Gross-Pitaevskii）模拟获得非线性演化。进行博戈留波夫-德热纳（Bogoliubov-de Gennes）分析以识别主导不稳定模式。

Result: 研究考察了三种机制：强不混溶极限下的开尔文-亥姆霍兹不稳定性、部分混溶区域的对超流不稳定性（counter-superflow instability），以及两种不稳定机制共存的参数窗口。集体激发（collective excitations）的特征及其空间结构与动力学中观察到的密度调制一致。

Conclusion: 三组分凝聚体中两个界面的存在和可调组分间相互作用改变了相对于二元混合物的不稳定性机制，为研究多组分量子流体动力学（multicomponent quantum hydrodynamics）提供了受控参数体系。

Abstract: Interfacial hydrodynamic instabilities in multicomponent superfluids provide a versatile platform to explore nonequilibrium quantum dynamics beyond classical fluid analogues. We study dynamical interfacial instabilities in a quasi-two-dimensional three-component Bose-Einstein condensate confined in a harmonic trap, where rotation is applied selectively to the intermediate component to generate controlled relative motion at two interfaces. This selective rotation protocol enables the independent tuning of shear and counterflow across the inner and outer boundaries, allowing direct control over the nature and strength of the resulting instability mechanisms. Three regimes are examined: Kelvin-Helmholtz instability in the strongly immiscible limit, counter-superflow instability in the partially miscible regime, and a parameter window where both unstable mechanisms are present. The onset condition for the Kelvin-Helmholtz instability is derived using a hydrodynamic pressure-balance approach, and the subsequent nonlinear evolution is obtained from time-dependent Gross-Pitaevskii simulations. A Bogoliubov-de Gennes analysis is performed to identify the dominant unstable modes excited during the dynamical evolution of the system. The conniving features of the collective excitations and their spatial structures have been consistent with the density modulations observed during the dynamics. The results demonstrate that the presence of two interfaces and tunable intercomponent interactions in a three-component condensate modifies the instability mechanisms relative to binary mixtures and provides a controlled parameter regime to study multicomponent quantum hydrodynamics.

</details>

### [112] [Jet flavor tagging with Particle Transformer for Higgs factories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18814)
*Taikan Suehara,Takahiro Kawahara,Tomohiko Tanabe,Risako Tagami*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 本研究评估了粒子变换器（ParT）在喷注味道标记（jet flavor tagging）中的性能，使用ILD全模拟事件和快速模拟样本进行训练，在b/c标记方面相比传统BDT方法有5-10倍的提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在评估粒子变换器（Particle Transformer, ParT）在喷注味道标记任务中的性能，探索其在区分不同味道夸克喷注方面的潜力，特别是与传统基于提升决策树（BDT）的方法进行对比。

Method: 研究使用ILD全模拟事件（100万喷注）和快速模拟样本（1000万和100万喷注）进行训练，执行3类别（b/c/d）、6类别（b/c/d/u/s/g）和11类别（包括夸克-反夸克分离）的训练，并整合了来自dE/dx和飞行时间（time-of-flight）的多变量强子粒子识别信息。

Result: 对于b/c标记，观察到相比先前基于BDT的标记器有5-10倍的改进，同时在奇异夸克标记和夸克/反夸克分离方面获得了合理的性能。1000万喷注的快速模拟研究表明，通过更高的训练统计量可能实现进一步的性能提升。

Conclusion: 粒子变换器在喷注味道标记任务中表现出显著优于传统BDT方法的性能，特别是在b/c标记方面，并且通过增加训练数据量有望获得进一步的性能改进。

Abstract: We study the performance of the Particle Transformer (ParT) for jet flavor tagging using ILD full simulation events (1M jets) as well as fast simulation samples (10M and 1M jets). We perform 3-category ($b/c/d$), 6-category ($b/c/d/u/s/g$), and 11-category trainings (including quark--antiquark separation), incorporating multivariate hadron particle identification information from $dE/dx$ and time-of-flight. For $b$/$c$ tagging, we observe a factor of 5--10 improvement over previous BDT-based taggers, and we obtain reasonable performance for strange tagging and quark/antiquark separation. The 10M-jet fast simulation study indicates that further gains are possible with higher training statistics.

Abstract: We present a lithographic method for fabricating free-standing microparticles directly from SUEX dry-film epoxy resist. Unlike conventional SU-8 particle fabrication, which requires patterning on solid substrates followed by sacrificial-layer release, our approach eliminates substrate use entirely and produces particles with near 100% yields. The process supports a wide design space of in-plane geometries, including high-aspect-ratio and highly complex shapes. To enable large-scale particle libraries, we integrate the method with the Nazca Python library, allowing programmatic generation of tens of thousands of parametrically defined particle designs. This combination of substrate-free fabrication and automated design provides a scalable route to custom microparticles for materials science, microfluidics, and soft-matter applications.

### [114] [Origin of Edge Currents in Chiral Active Liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18159)
*Faisal Alsallom,David T. Limmer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过微观运动方程和分子动力学模拟，揭示了手性活性液体（chiral active liquids）在受限几何结构中产生单向边缘电流（unidirectional edge currents）的物理机制，发现其源于密集系统中的全局角动量守恒（global angular momentum conservation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性活性液体在简单几何结构中表现出单向边缘电流现象，但其物理起源一直缺乏合理解释。本研究旨在从微观层面揭示这一集体现象的产生机制。

Method: 从简单二维模型的微观运动方程出发，推导出密集相中平均边缘电流的欧姆式电导定律（Ohmic-like conductance law）。通过广泛的分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）对理论结果进行数值验证。

Result: 研究发现局部边缘电流的产生源于密集系统中的全局角动量守恒。推导出平均边缘电流的欧姆式电导定律，该电流为强度量，仅依赖于密度、活性扭矩（active torque）和基底阻力（substrate drag）。在简单几何结构中，边缘电流分布具有封闭高斯形式，其方差也为强度量，仅取决于温度、密度和系统纵横比（aspect ratio）。

Conclusion: 这些结果为通过守恒量的全局平衡（global balance of conserved quantities）研究活性物质（active matter）中的集体现象提供了新视角，揭示了手性活性液体边缘电流的微观起源。

Abstract: Chiral active liquids exhibit unidirectional edge currents when confined to simple geometries, but the origin of this phenomenon has defied explanation. Starting from the microscopic equations of motion of a simple two-dimensional model, we find that localized edge currents emerge as a consequence of global angular momentum conservation in dense systems. From these underlying equations, we derive an Ohmic-like conductance law for the mean edge current in the dense phase, and we find it to be intensive, depending only on the density, active torque and substrate drag. For simple geometries, we find the distribution of the edge currents has a closed Gaussian form, with a variance that is intensive, depending only on temperature, density and the aspect ratio of the system. These results are validated numerically using extensive molecular dynamics simulations. These results provide a new perspective for studying the collective phenomena in active matter through the global balance of conserved quantities.

</details>


### [115] [Modeling cavitation and fibrillation in elastomers and adhesives. Part I: Cohesive instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18262)
*S. Mohammad Mousavi,Sarvesh Joshi,Franck Vernerey,Nikolaos Bouklas*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个梯度增强连续介质框架，从内聚不稳定性（cohesive instability）和相变角度分析软弹性体和粘合剂中的空穴成核（cavity nucleation），无需预设缺陷。该框架基于交联范德华流体（crosslinked van der Waals fluid）模型，提供了空穴成核的内在分析判据，并再现了关键实验趋势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软弹性体和粘合剂中的空穴化（cavitation）通常被视为弹性不稳定性，是粘合剂中纤维化和最终失效的第一步。现有研究多基于不可压缩固体，缺乏从内聚不稳定性角度分析空穴成核的物理基础框架。

Method: 基于Lamont等人（2025）的工作，将弹性体材料处理为交联范德华流体（crosslinked van der Waals fluid）。引入梯度增强连续介质框架（gradient-enhanced continuum framework），从内聚不稳定性（cohesive instability）和相变角度分析空穴形成。该热力学一致推导包含相关材料长度尺度的引入以及与聚合物链解缠结（polymer chain disentanglement）相关的粘性耗散。

Result: 研究表明，对于应变硬化（strain stiffening）和应变软化（strain softening）模型（就其剪切响应而言），都能重现类似空穴化的不稳定性。模拟再现了关键实验趋势，包括粘合剂层厚度驱动的从少量大空穴到多个小空穴的纵横比驱动转变（aspect ratio-driven transition）。

Conclusion: 该框架为驱动空穴成核的内聚不稳定性提供了稳健的物理基础，未来可与损伤、断裂和耗散模型集成，以完整捕捉空穴化、纤维化和失效过程。研究未涉及材料在内聚不稳定性和从致密相到稀疏相转变过程中经历的即将发生的损伤。

Abstract: Cavitation in soft elastomers and adhesives is often viewed as an elastic instability, commonly tied to the study of incompressible solids. It is the first step prior to fibrillation and ultimate failure in adhesives. Building on the work of Lamont et al. (2025), elastomeric materials are treated as a crosslinked van der Waals fluid. The van der Waals contribution, capturing excluded volume and cohesive forces, is non-(poly)convex, readily providing an intrinsic analytical criterion for cavity nucleation. This work introduces a gradient-enhanced continuum framework that examines the emergence of cavity formation from the perspective of a cohesive instability and corresponding phase transition without requiring a pre-existing defect. The corresponding thermodynamically consistent derivation includes the introduction of a relevant material length scale as well as viscous dissipation associated with polymer chain disentanglement during the cohesive instability. This work does not study the impending damage that the material undergoes during the cohesive instability and transition from a dense to a rare phase. Interestingly, it is shown that for both strain stiffening and strain softening models (in terms of their shear response), an instability reminiscent of what is expected in the case of cavitation is recapitulated. Simulations reproduce key experimental trends, including the aspect ratio-driven transition from a few large to many small cavities depending on the thickness of an adhesive layer. The framework offers a robust, physically grounded basis for the cohesive instability that drives cavity nucleation, enabling future integration with damage, fracture, and dissipation models to capture the complete cavitation, fibrillation, and failure process.

</details>


### [116] [Synthesis, Solvent-dependent Self-Assembly and Partial Oxidation of Ultrathin Cerium Fluoride Nanoplatelets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18270)
*Chiara Moretti,Damien Alloyeau,Benjamin Aymoz Laurent Lermusiaux,Rodolphe Valleix,Benoit Mahler,Marianne Impéror-Clerc,Benjamin Abécassis*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过优化合成获得尺寸和形状分布窄的三角形铈基纳米片（NPLs），其结构为部分氧化的氟氧化铈（CeOxFy）。研究发现溶剂选择决定纳米片在溶液中的排列方式，进而影响蒸发自组装形成的超结构：促进面对面堆叠的溶剂产生垂直于界面的柱状组装体，而保持单个分散的溶剂则形成平行于界面的六方有序超晶格。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维胶体纳米片（NPLs）具有原子级精确的厚度和独特的物理性质，但理解其形成机制和组装行为对于调控其集体性质至关重要。本研究旨在优化合成铈基纳米片并探究其在不同条件下的自组装行为。

Method: 通过三氟乙酸铈的热分解优化合成了三角形纳米片，结合X射线衍射（XRD）、X射线光电子能谱（XPS）和高分辨扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）表征其结构和组成。研究油酸封端的纳米片在溶液中和界面上的组织方式，重点关注溶剂选择对蒸发自组装过程的影响。

Result: 合成的纳米片具有窄的尺寸和形状分布，其预期CeF3结构发生部分氧化，形成氟氧化铈（CeOxFy）组成。溶剂选择显著影响自组装结果：促进面对面堆叠的溶剂在蒸发时形成垂直于界面的微米级柱状组装体；而保持单个分散的溶剂则产生平行于界面的边缘对边缘堆叠的六方有序超晶格，跨度达数微米。

Conclusion: 溶剂介导的相互作用和溶液中预先存在的组织方式是决定胶体纳米晶体蒸发自组装结果的关键因素。这一发现为通过溶剂工程调控纳米材料超结构提供了重要指导。

Abstract: Two-dimensional colloidal nanoplatelets (NPLs) with atomically defined thickness exhibit unique physical properties, yet understanding their formation mechanism and assembly remains essential for tuning their collective behavior. We report an optimized synthesis of triangular cerium-based NPLs with narrow size and shape distributions via thermal decomposition of cerium trifluoroacetate. Combining X-ray diffraction, XPS, and high-resolution STEM, we show that the expected CeF3 NPL structure undergoes partial oxidation, yielding an oxyfluoride composition CeOxFy. Beyond their composition, we investigate how these oleic acid-capped NPLs organize in solution and at interfaces. The choice of solvent governs both the solution-phase organization and the resulting superstructures formed upon evaporation at the liquid--air interface. In solvents that promote face-to-face stacking in solution, evaporation produces films organized into columnar assemblies tens of micrometers long, with the NPL planes oriented perpendicular to the interface. In contrast, solvents in which NPLs remain individually dispersed yield extended hexagonally ordered superlattices with edge-to-edge stacking spanning several micrometers, where the NPLs lie parallel to the interface in an edge-to-edge arrangement. These results highlight that solvent-mediated interactions and pre-existing organization in solution are decisive factors in determining the outcome of evaporative self-assembly of colloidal nanocrystals.

</details>


### [117] [Direct measurement of osmotic pressure and interparticle interactions in colloidal dispersions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18476)
*Keita Saito,Fumito Araoka*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种基于光镊（optical tweezer）系统的实验技术，可在同一系统中同时测量胶体（colloidal）分散体系的渗透压（osmotic pressure）和粒子间相互作用（interparticle interactions），实现了从微观粒子层面到宏观渗透压的多尺度关联分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶体分散体系广泛存在于自然环境和工业材料中，其宏观性质如粘度和光散射取决于分散性，而分散性由粒子间相互作用表征。渗透压是表征分散体系的重要参数，但通常极低且测量方法有限，因此需要开发能够同时测量渗透压和粒子间相互作用的新技术。

Method: 本研究采用光镊系统作为实验平台，在同一系统中同时测量渗透压和粒子间相互作用。通过直接测量的粒子间相互作用数据，结合布朗动力学（Brownian dynamics）模拟和基于硬球模型（hard-sphere model）的理论计算进行验证。

Result: 实验直接测量的渗透压与基于实验测量的粒子间相互作用进行的布朗动力学模拟和硬球模型理论计算结果一致。这种一致性证明了该技术在多尺度研究中的适用性，能够在单一系统中将微观粒子层面的相互作用与宏观渗透压联系起来。

Conclusion: 所提出的光镊技术为研究胶体分散性质提供了有效的多尺度分析工具，实现了从微观到宏观的关联测量。该技术使通过粒子层面改性实现胶体材料的自下而上（bottom-up）设计成为可能。

Abstract: Colloidal dispersions are widely found in systems ranging from natural environments to industrial materials.Their macroscopic properties such as viscosity and light scattering depend on their dispersibility, which is characterized by interparticle interactions. Osmotic pressure is induced in a solution with a concentration gradient, in which dispersity is one of the major factors governing the behavior of solutes. Thus, examining the relationship between the interparticle interactions and osmotic pressure may reveal colloidal dispersive properties. Although measuring the osmotic pressure is useful to understand dispersion systems, osmotic pressure is usually extremely low, and only limited experimental methods are available. In this study, we demonstrate that both osmotic pressure and interparticle interactions can be measured within the same experimental system, an optical tweezer system. The directly measured pressure is consistent with both the Brownian dynamics simulation and theoretical results based on the hard-sphere model, both of which were calculated using the interparticle interactions directly measured in the experiment. This agreement demonstrates the applicability of the proposed technique for investigating dispersive properties across multiple scales, linking microscopic particle-level interactions to macroscopic osmotic pressure within a single system. The proposed technique enables bottom-up design of colloidal materials through particle-level modifications.

### [118] [Non-equilibrium (thermo)dynamics of colloids under mobile piston compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18618)
*Arturo Moncho-Jordá,José López-Molina,Joachim Dzubiella*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究采用动态密度泛函理论（dynamical density functional theory）分析受限硬球胶体流体在移动边界驱动下的非平衡压缩过程，揭示了从准静态压缩到扩散限制强驱动机制的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在定量表征边界驱动压缩过程中的热力学行为，特别是探索机械驱动与扩散弛豫相对时间尺度对系统非平衡演化的影响。

Method: 采用动态密度泛函理论（dynamical density functional theory）研究受限硬球胶体流体，系统由两个平行壁面构成，其中一个作为过阻尼活塞（overdamped piston）受外部压力突然增加驱动。活塞运动由迁移率参数K控制，该参数设定机械驱动与扩散弛豫的相对时间尺度。

Result: 通过改变K值（跨越多个数量级），识别出从准静态压缩到扩散限制强驱动机制（diffusion-limited strongly driven regime）的转变。小K值时系统接近平衡演化，总注入功接近平衡自由能差；大K值时活塞快速调整，动力学由扩散弛豫主导，导致活塞轨迹、压力-位置关系、粒子流和质心速度饱和。最大注入功率与K呈线性比例，熵产生峰值呈现从二次增长到饱和的转变，峰值时间显示1/K标度关系。

Conclusion: 研究提供了边界驱动压缩过程的定量热力学表征，揭示了构型熵和外部势能演化中限制与结构弛豫的动态解耦，包括瞬态非单调行为。熵变在可逆极限与强驱动耗散机制之间插值，反映了扩散输运施加的约束。

Abstract: We investigate the non-equilibrium compression of a confined hard-sphere colloidal fluid driven by a mobile boundary within dynamical density functional theory. The system consists of a fluid confined between two parallel walls, one acting as an overdamped piston subjected to a sudden increase in external pressure. The piston motion is controlled by a mobility parameter $K$, which sets the relative timescale between mechanical driving and diffusive relaxation. By varying $K$ over several orders of magnitude, we identify a crossover from quasi-static compression to a diffusion-limited strongly driven regime. For small $K$, the system evolves close to equilibrium and the total injected work approaches the equilibrium free-energy difference. For large $K$, the piston rapidly adjusts and the dynamics becomes governed by diffusive relaxation, leading to saturation in the piston trajectory, pressure--position relation, particle currents, and center-of-mass velocity. In this regime, the injected work and entropy production are bounded, reflecting constraints imposed by diffusive transport. The maximum injected power scales linearly with $K$, while the entropy-production peak exhibits a crossover from quadratic growth to saturation, with peak times displaying $1/K$ scaling. The entropy change of the thermal bath interpolates between a reversible limit and a strongly driven dissipative regime. Finally, the evolution of configurational entropy and external potential energy reveals a dynamical decoupling between confinement and structural relaxation, including transient non-monotonic behavior. These results provide a quantitative thermodynamic characterization of boundary-driven compression.

</details>


### [119] [Tuning polymer architecture for quasicrystal self-assembly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18694)
*D. J. Ratliff,A. Scacchi,P. Subramanian,A. J. Archer,A. M. Rucklidge*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过计算机模拟和理论分析，探究了具有"绒球"（pompom）结构的树状大分子（dendrimer）的超软相互作用，揭示了其可调控的长度尺度竞争特性，并展示了如何通过调节聚合物结构参数实现稳定的十二重准晶（dodecagonal quasicrystal）相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解由刚性连接体连接中心聚合物和柔性聚合物冠层形成的"绒球"结构树状大分子的超软相互作用（ultrasoft interactions），探索其粗粒化相互作用势的可调控特性，为软物质准晶（soft matter quasicrystal）的实验实现提供分子结构设计指导。

Method: 采用计算机模拟（computer simulations）和理论分析相结合的方法，首先研究树状大分子对的粗粒化相互作用势（coarse-grained interaction potential），然后使用加速蒙特卡洛方法（accelerated Monte Carlo methods）验证提出的简单配对势模型。

Result: 研究发现树状大分子对的相互作用势表现出基于核心和冠层聚合物性质的可调控长度尺度竞争（tunable lengthscale competition），通过特定参数选择能够实现稳定的十二重准晶相，且准晶在相图中的稳定区域大小可通过单独调节聚合物结构细节进行控制。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了树状大分子结构与介观相（mesoscopic phases）之间的关联，通过识别导致准晶稳定的整体分子结构（overall molecular architecture），为软物质准晶的实验实现铺平了道路。

Abstract: Using computer simulations and theory, we investigate the ultrasoft interactions between dendrimers formed of a central polymer connected by stiff linkers to a corona of flexible polymers, forming `pompoms' at the ends of the linkers. We show that the resulting coarse-grained interaction potential between pairs of dendrimers exhibits tunable lengthscale competition based on properties of the core and corona polymers. We present a simple model for this pair potential, which we confirm using accelerated Monte Carlo methods. We then demonstrate the connection between dendrimer structure and mesoscopic phases by presenting parameter choices that result in stable dodecagonal quasicrystals, and show that the size of the region in the phase diagram where quasicrystals are stable can be controlled by tuning details of the polymer architecture alone. These results pave the way for experimental realization of soft matter quasicrystals by identifying what overall molecular architecture leads to their stability.

</details>


### [120] [Elastocapillary lifting and encapsulation of water by a triangular elastic film under gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18824)
*Kyoko Shibata,Hana Kanda,Yoshimi Tanaka,Yutaka Sumino*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过薄弹性薄膜包裹水的实验，建立了弹性毛细自折叠与流体输运的最小模型，揭示了薄膜形态由表面能、液体重力能和薄膜弯曲能竞争决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立弹性毛细自折叠（elastocapillary self-folding）与流体输运的最小模型，通过分析薄弹性薄膜包裹水的物理过程，理解弹性薄膜在毛细作用下的形态演化机制。

Method: 采用准静态（quasi-statically）方式从水面提起等边三角形聚二甲基硅氧烷（polydimethylsiloxane）薄膜，系统改变其边长和厚度参数，观察不同参数下的薄膜形态变化。

Result: 薄膜表现出三种不同形态：折叠（folding）、回缩（recoiling）和液体包裹（liquid encapsulation）。包裹现象发生在弹性毛细长度、弹性重力长度和毛细长度尺度相交的狭窄参数区域。

Conclusion: 薄膜形态选择由表面能、液体重力能和薄膜弯曲能的竞争决定，包裹现象的出现基于弯曲能、毛细能和重力能的平衡，为弹性薄膜液体包裹提供了简单的物理判据。

Abstract: We investigate the encapsulation of water by a thin elastic film as a minimal model of elastocapillary self-folding with fluid transport. An equilateral triangular polydimethylsiloxane film is lifted quasi-statically from a water surface, while its side length and thickness are systematically varied. Depending on these parameters, the film exhibits three distinct morphologies: folding, recoiling, and liquid encapsulation. We show that the observed morphology is selected by the competition between surface energy, gravitational energy of the liquid, and bending energy of the film. In particular, encapsulation occurs in a narrow parameter region corresponding to the intersection of the elastocapillary, elastogravity, and capillary length scales. This result provides a simple physical criterion for liquid encapsulation by elastic films, based on the balance of bending, capillary, and gravitational energies.

</details>


### [121] [Guided elastic waves informed material modelling of soft incompressible media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18839)
*Pierre Chantelot,Samuel Croquette,Fabrice Lemoult*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过监测弹性波在单轴拉伸弹性体板中的传播，解决了仅凭静态测试无法区分不同超弹性模型的问题。该方法能够区分具有不同C2项函数形式的模型，但仍无法区分广义neo-Hookean模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别一个能够描述橡胶类固体在所有变形场和可达到延伸范围内的力学响应的通用本构定律（universal material constitutive law）是一个重要挑战。当前仅凭静态单轴拉伸应力-应变测量无法区分具有不同函数形式的超弹性模型（hyperelastic models）。

Method: 研究利用弹性波传播，监测在单轴拉伸下的弹性体板中增量导波（incremental guided wave）的传播。测量了三个零阶导波模式（zero-order guided modes）沿施加伸长方向平行和垂直传播的色散关系（dispersion relations）。使用Destrade等人（Proc. R. Soc. A 2017）的方法论程序，通过拟合三个连续伸长区域的单轴应力-应变曲线提取参数，并与考虑材料流变学（material rheology）的声弹性理论（acoustoelastic theory）预测进行比较。

Result: 该方法解除了具有不同C2项函数形式的超弹性模型之间的简并性（degeneracy），这些模型在静态单轴拉伸应力-应变测量中无法区分。然而，与静态测试类似，该动态测量方法仍无法区分不同的广义neo-Hookean模型（generalized neo-Hookean models）。

Conclusion: 通过监测弹性波在变形弹性体中的传播，提供了一种能够区分仅凭静态测试无法区分的超弹性模型的方法。该方法为材料本构定律的识别提供了新的动态测量途径，但仍存在对某些模型族（如广义neo-Hookean模型）的区分限制。

Abstract: Identifying a universal material constitutive law, that describes the mechanical response of rubber-like solids for all deformation fields and achievable extensions, is an outstanding challenge. Here, we propose to exploit the propagation of elastic waves and demonstrate that monitoring incremental guided wave propagation in an elastomer plate undergoing uniaxial extension reveals model sensitivities that are inaccessible in the corresponding static test. We measure the dispersion relations of the three zero-order guided modes, propagating parallel and perpendicular to the direction of imposed elongation. We compare them with predictions from the acoustoelastic theory, that also take into account material rheology, using parameters extracted from fitting the uniaxial stress-strain curve across three successive elongation regimes, following the methodical procedure of Destrade $\textit{et al.}$ (Proc. R. Soc. A 2017). We evidence that our approach lifts the degeneracy between hyperelastic models with different functional forms of the so-called $C_2$ term, which remain undistinguishable from static uniaxial tension stress-strain measurements alone. However, like their static counterpart, our dynamics measurements cannot distinguish between different generalized neo-Hookean models.

</details>


### [122] [Avalanches in the Random Organization Model with long-range interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18909)
*T. Jocteur,K. Martens,R. Mari,E. Bertin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过改进的随机组织模型（Random Organization Model）分析了振荡剪切悬浮液在吸收相变（absorbing phase transition）附近的间歇性动力学，发现雪崩（avalanche）统计呈现幂律分布，且相互作用范围影响雪崩的空间结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注振荡剪切悬浮液可逆-不可逆转变（reversible-irreversible transition）的全局量，而本研究受动力学脱钉转变（kin depinning transition）启发，聚焦于相变附近的间歇性动力学（intermittent dynamics）。

Method: 采用改进的随机组织模型（Random Organization Model, ROM），该最小粒子模型考虑了流体介导的长程相互作用（long-range interactions），并将幂律衰减指数α作为额外控制参数，通过模拟分析雪崩统计特性。

Result: 在吸收相变处，模型显示幂律分布的雪崩（power-law-distributed avalanches）。通过表征雪崩尺寸、持续时间和涉及粒子数的统计，确定了相关指数。随着α变化，雪崩的分形维度（fractal dimension）跨越空间维度d，导致雪崩空间结构从短程相互作用的紧凑型（compact avalanches）转变为长程相互作用的稀疏型（sparse avalanches）。

Conclusion: 雪崩内部簇（clusters）同样呈现幂律分布，表明振荡剪切悬浮液的吸收相变具有丰富的临界现象，且相互作用范围对雪崩空间结构产生定性影响。

Abstract: Oscillatory sheared suspensions, when observed stroboscopically, exhibit a reversible-irreversible transition as a function of the strain amplitude, which is a kind of absorbing phase transition. So far studies of this transition focused on global quantities, e.g. quantifying the irreversibility on one side of the transition or the time to reach a reversible state on the other side. Here, motivated by the kin depinning transition, we focus on the intermittent dynamics near the transition. We perform simulations of a modified Random Organization Model (ROM), a minimal particle model which we recently adapted to take into account the generic presence of long-range interactions mediated by the fluid, taking the power-law-decay exponent $α$ as an additional control parameter of the model. We show that at the absorbing phase transition, this model displays power-law-distributed avalanches. We characterize the avalanche statistics in terms of avalanche size, duration and number of particles involved, and we determine the associated exponents. By varying the exponent $α$, the fractal dimension of avalanches crosses space dimension $d$, inducing a qualitative change of the spatial structure of avalanches, from compact avalanches when interactions have a short range, to sparse avalanches when interactions are long-ranged. Finally, we characterize the clusters within the avalanches, which we also find power-law distributed.

</details>


### [123] [Navigating complex phase diagrams in soft matter systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18918)
*Michael Wassermair,Gerhard Kahl,Roland Roth,Andrew J. Archer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出利用均匀密度系统的动力学密度泛函理论（dynamical density functional theory）获得的色散关系ω(k)来预测复杂晶体相的形成区域，显著加速了复杂相图的绘制过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶体流体（colloidal fluids）表现出复杂的相行为，通过实验或计算机模拟确定相图通常非常耗时费力。因此需要开发更高效的方法来预测相图中复杂晶体形成的区域。

Method: 采用动力学密度泛函理论（dynamical density functional theory）分析均匀密度系统的色散关系ω(k)，通过ω(k)的符号判断密度模式随时间增长或衰减。同时使用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）进行验证，并通过调节相互作用势（interaction-potential）和状态点参数来设计系统。

Result: 研究表明，相图中ω(k)具有一个或多个不稳定（增长）波数的区域正是晶体相出现的区域。通过调节不稳定波数，成功设计了在相图中包含准晶（quasicrystals）的系统，并识别出一个具有特定肩宽范围（shoulder-range）的系统，该系统至少包含10种不同的相。

Conclusion: 该通用方法显著加速了复杂相图的绘制过程，对于新材料设计至关重要。色散关系ω(k)成为预测复杂晶体相形成区域的高度通用工具。

Abstract: Colloidal fluids can exhibit complex phase behavior and determining phase diagrams via experiments or computer simulations can be laborious. We demonstrate that the dispersion relation $ω(k)$, obtained from dynamical density functional theory for the uniform density system, is a highly versatile tool for {\it predicting} where in the phase diagram complex crystals form. The sign of $ω(k)$ determines whether density modes with wavenumber $k$ grow or decay over time. We demonstrate the predictive power by investigating the complex phase behavior of particles interacting via core-shoulder pair potentials. With complementary Monte Carlo simulations, we show that regions of the phase diagram where $ω(k)$ has one or several unstable (growing) wavenumbers are also where crystalline phases occur. Going further, by tuning these unstable wavenumbers via the interaction-potential and state-point parameters, we design systems with quasicrystals in the phase diagram. We identify a system with a certain shoulder-range exhibiting at least 10 different phases. Our general approach accelerates considerably the mapping of complex phase diagrams, crucial for the design of new materials.

</details>

### [124] [Open-Closed String Field Theory from Calabi-Yau Categories and its Applications to Enumerative Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18186)
*Jakob Ulmer*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 该论文开发了连接枚举几何（enumerative geometry）与大N规范理论（large N gauge theories）的范畴方法，建立了图复形（graph complexes）、Calabi-Yau A∞-范畴与Kontsevich上循环构造（cocycle construction）之间的关系，并构建了形式性L∞-态射（formality L∞-morphism）以推广范畴枚举不变量（categorical enumerative invariants）到开闭（open-closed）情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文的核心动机是发展连接镜像对称（mirror symmetry）中研究的枚举几何与大N规范理论的范畴方法。从物理学视角看，闭弦场论（closed string field theory）的配分函数编码了闭范畴枚举不变量，而研究旨在将这一框架推广到开闭情形。

Method: 方法包括建立图复形、Calabi-Yau A∞-范畴与Kontsevich上循环构造之间的关系。核心成果是构建了一个形式性L∞-态射，该态射关联了从Calabi-Yau范畴及其对象构建的代数结构，并依赖于非交换Hodge滤过（non-commutative Hodge filtration）的一个分裂（splitting）。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）建立了图复形、Calabi-Yau A∞-范畴与Kontsevich上循环构造的关系；2）构建了形式性L∞-态射，将范畴枚举不变量从闭情形推广到开闭情形；3）该开闭态射是量子化与Calabi-Yau范畴对象相关的大N开弦场论的关键成分；4）基于开闭反作用弦场论（backreacted SFT）的代数方法，提出了在配分函数层面构建"扭曲全息（Twisted Holography）"范畴表述的构想。

Conclusion: 论文发展了连接枚举几何与大N规范理论的范畴框架，通过构建形式性L∞-态射将范畴枚举不变量推广到开闭情形。该工作为量子化大N开弦场论提供了数学基础，并提出了在配分函数层面实现扭曲全息的范畴表述的新方向。

Abstract: The overarching goal of this thesis was to develop categorical methods that connect enumerative geometry, as studied in mirror symmetry, with large $N$ gauge theories. In the first part, we established a relation between graph complexes, Calabi-Yau $A_\infty$-categories, and Kontsevich's cocycle construction. The next main result is the construction of a formality $L_\infty$-morphism relating algebraic structures built from a Calabi-Yau category and one of its objects; this morphism depends on a splitting of the non-commutative Hodge filtration.This generalizes the approach of categorical enumerative invariants from the closed to the open-closed setting. From a physics perspective, closed categorical enumerative invariants are encoded by the partition function of the associated closed string field theory (SFT). We explain how our open-closed morphism is an ingredient in quantizing the large N open SFT associated to an object of a Calabi-Yau category. In the final part of this thesis, based on an algebraic approach to open and closed backreacted SFT, we propose ideas towards a categorical formulation of 'Twisted Holography' at the level of partition functions, given as input a Calabi-Yau category and one of its objects.

### [125] [$Ξ_b \to Ξ$ form factors from lattice QCD and Standard-Model predictions for $Ξ_b \to Ξμ^+μ^-$ and $Ξ_b \to Ξγ$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18438)
*Callum Farrell,Stefan Meinel*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究首次通过格点QCD（lattice QCD）计算了Ξ_b → Ξ跃迁的矢量、轴矢量和张量形状因子（form factors），为包含Ξ_b → Ξℓ⁺ℓ⁻和Ξ_b → Ξγ的稀有衰变理论提供了关键输入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ξ_b重子的稀有衰变过程（如Ξ_b → Ξℓ⁺ℓ⁻和Ξ_b → Ξγ）是检验标准模型（Standard Model）和寻找新物理（new physics）的重要探针。然而，这些衰变的理论描述需要精确的强子矩阵元信息，特别是Ξ_b → Ξ跃迁的形状因子，此前缺乏格点QCD的直接计算。

Method: 采用2+1味（flavors）的畴壁费米子（domain-wall fermions）在三种不同格距（lattice spacings）和π介子质量（从约430到230 MeV）下进行计算。底夸克（bottom quark）使用各向异性clover作用量（anisotropic clover action）实现。通过具有宽范围源-汇分离（source-sink separations）的三点函数（three-point functions）和模型平均（model averaging）提取基态贡献。使用修正的z展开（modified z expansions）拟合形状因子对动量转移（momentum transfer）、π介子质量和格距的依赖关系，并应用色散关系界限（dispersive bounds）和渐近行为约束（asymptotic-behavior constraints）来控制整个半轻运动学区域（semileptonic kinematic region）的不确定性。

Result: 研究首次确定了Ξ_b → Ξ跃迁的矢量、轴矢量和张量形状因子。基于这些形状因子结果，给出了标准模型下Ξ_b⁻ → Ξ⁻γ和Ξ_b⁻ → Ξ⁻μ⁺μ⁻的分支比（branching fractions）以及两个角分布可观测量（angular observables）的理论预言。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了首个基于格点QCD的Ξ_b → Ξ形状因子系统计算，为相关稀有衰变过程提供了精确的理论输入。通过结合多种格点参数、先进的拟合方法和理论约束，获得了在整个运动学区域内具有可控不确定性的结果，为标准模型的检验和新物理的搜寻奠定了基础。

Abstract: We present the first lattice QCD determination of the $Ξ_b \to Ξ$ vector, axial-vector, and tensor form factors, which are relevant for the theory of rare decays including $Ξ_b \to Ξ\ell^+\ell^-$ and $Ξ_b \to Ξγ$. The calculation is performed with 2+1 flavors of domain-wall fermions at three different lattice spacings and pion masses in the range from approximately 430 to 230 MeV. The bottom quark is implemented using an anisotropic clover action. Three-point functions with a wide range of source-sink separations and model averaging are used to extract the ground-state contributions. We fit the dependence of the form factors on the momentum transfer, the pion mass, and the lattice spacing using modified $z$ expansions that account for subthreshold branch cuts, and apply dispersive bounds and asymptotic-behavior constraints to achieve controlled uncertainties in the full semileptonic kinematic region. Using our form factor results, we present Standard-Model predictions for the $Ξ_b^- \to Ξ^- γ$ and $Ξ_b^- \to Ξ^- μ^+μ^-$ branching fractions and two angular observables.

</details>


### [126] [Doubly Bottom and Bottom-Strange Tetraquarks in the Isoscalar Channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18667)
*Bhabani Sankar Tripathy,Nilmani Mathur,M. Padmanath*

TL;DR: 该研究通过格点QCD（lattice QCD）计算，在等标量（isoscalar）道中发现了双底（doubly bottom）四夸克存在深度束缚态（deeply bound state）的强有力证据，但未找到底-奇异（bottom-strange）四夸克存在的确凿证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索在等标量道中双底和底-奇异四夸克（tetraquarks）是否存在可能的束缚态，以增进对奇特强子态（exotic hadronic states）的理解。

Method: 研究采用MILC合作组生成的包含粲夸克（charm quark）在内的四种不同晶格间距（lattice spacings）的动力学夸克场系综（ensembles），并使用两种体积来考虑有限体积效应（finite volume effects）。轻夸克和奇异夸克传播子（propagators）采用重叠作用量（overlap action）计算，重底夸克使用非相对论QCD（NRQCD）形式。通过变分法（variational method）结合严格的Lüscher散射振幅分析（scattering amplitude analysis）计算有限体积能量。

Result: 研究发现双底四夸克道存在深度束缚态的强有力证据，但未发现底-奇异四夸克存在的确凿证据。

Conclusion: 该格点QCD研究证实了双底四夸克束缚态的存在，但未能确定底-奇异四夸克是否形成束缚态，为进一步研究奇特强子态提供了重要参考。

Abstract: We present our recent investigation on doubly bottom and bottom-strange tetraquarks in the isoscalar channel in search of a possible tetraquark bound state. The calculations are performed on four ensembles with dynamical quark fields up to the charm quark generated by the MILC Collaboration with various lattice spacings. Two volumes have been used to account for finite volume effects. Overlap action has been employed to calculate light and strange quark propagators and NRQCD formulation is utilized for heavy bottom quarks. Finite volume energy has been calculated using the variational method followed by rigorous scattering amplitude analysis à la Lüscher. We find strong evidence for a deeply bound state in the doubly bottom tetraquark channel, but no conclusive evidence for the existence of a bottom-strange tetraquark.

### [127] [Decorated Local Systems and Character Varieties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18842)
*Benedetta Facciotti,Marta Mazzocco,Nikita Nikolaev*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文为研究带边界曲面基本广群（fundamental groupoid）表示模空间（moduli space）建立了一个范畴框架，旨在统一处理含高阶极点（higher order poles）情形的装饰贝蒂模空间（decorated Betti moduli spaces）的不同定义方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献对含高阶极点的装饰贝蒂模空间存在多种不同但本质相关的处理方法，然而这些方法之间的确切关系尚未明确建立。本文旨在为这些不同的观点提供一个系统化的统一框架。

Method: 本文发展了一个范畴框架（categorical framework），该框架允许对装饰贝蒂模空间进行系统性定义，特别针对含高阶极点的情形，并能特化为文献中遇到的不同观点。

Result: 建立了一个统一的范畴框架，能够系统定义装饰贝蒂模空间，并使其能够自然地涵盖文献中现有的不同处理方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的范畴框架为装饰贝蒂模空间的不同研究方法提供了概念上一致且明确的关系，实现了对含高阶极点情形的统一处理。

Abstract: The focus of this paper is the study of the moduli space of representations of fundamental groupoids of surfaces $Σ$ with boundaries with values in $G:=GL_n(\mathbb C)$. In absence of marked points on the boundary, this moduli space is realized in many equivalent ways: as the moduli space of linear local systems on $Σ$, as the moduli space of representations of the fundamental groupoid $Π_1 (Σ)$, as the space of monodromy data and as character variety. By adding marked points to the boundary of $Σ$ in order to capture irregular singularities, the Betti moduli space has been generalized in several ways by many authors. Although it is clear that these different approaches describe essentially the same spaces of mathematical objects, exactly how they fit together has not yet been established. Motivated by the broader programme of establishing an explicit and conceptually coherent relationship between the existing approaches to the study of the decorated Betti moduli space, in this paper, we develop a categorical framework that allows for a systematic definition of the
  \dfn{decorated Betti moduli spaces} space, in the presence of higher order poles, designed to specialize to the different points of view encountered in the literature.

### [128] [Direct observation of ultrafast defect-bound and free exciton dynamics in defect-engineered WS$_2$ monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18230)
*Tae Gwan Park,Xufan Li,Kyungnam Kang,Austin Houston,Liam Collins,Gerd Duscher,David B. Geohegan,Christopher M. Rouleau,Kai Xiao,Alexander A. Puretzky*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究首次直接观测了单层WS₂中缺陷束缚激子（defect-bound excitons）的超快动力学过程，揭示了其与自由激子（free excitons）的相干耦合及相互转换机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维过渡金属硫族化合物（TMDCs）中的缺陷显著影响其光学和电子性质。直接捕获激子陷获和缺陷束缚激子形成的超快过程对于理解和推进缺陷介导的光电子学和量子技术至关重要，但缺陷束缚激子的弱瞬态光学吸收限制了实验观测。

Method: 采用碱金属卤化物辅助化学气相沉积（alkali metal halide-assisted chemical vapor deposition）合成具有高密度单硫空位（V$_S$）和W位缺陷复合物（S$_W$V$_S$）的单层WS₂晶体，利用超快光学光谱（ultrafast optical spectroscopy）阐明缺陷束缚激子的动力学及其与自由激子的相干相互作用。

Result: 研究发现：1）在带边以上光激发下，自由激子和缺陷束缚激子在300 fs内同时形成；2）缺陷束缚激子寿命更短，导致激子态布居差异和1-100 ps窗口内的自由激子陷获；3）带边光激发显示~150 fs内的超快相互转换，表明态间可能存在相干耦合；4）缺陷束缚激子可高效上转换至比自由激子共振低~300 meV的自由激子。

Conclusion: 这些发现为理解TMDCs中缺陷束缚激子的超快动力学及其与自由激子的耦合提供了重要见解，对缺陷工程光电子学、量子光子学和谷电子学（valleytronic）应用具有重要意义。

Abstract: Defects in two-dimensional transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDCs) broadly affect their optical and electronic properties. Directly capturing the ultrafast processes of exciton trapping and defect-bound exciton formation is crucial for understanding and advancing defect-mediated optoelectronics and quantum technologies. However, the weak transient optical absorption of defect-bound excitons has limited their experimental observation to date. Here, we report the direct observation of the ultrafast dynamics of defect-bound excitons in monolayer WS$_2$ crystals with a high density of mono-sulfur vacancies (V$_S$) and W-site defect complexes (S$_W$V$_S$) resulting from synthesis by alkali metal halide-assisted chemical vapor deposition. The dynamics of excitons bound to these defects, along with their coherent interactions with free excitons, are elucidated using ultrafast optical spectroscopy. Using above band-edge photoexcitation, we find that both free and defect-bound excitons simultaneously form within 300 fs from hot carrier relaxation. The defect-bound excitons exhibit shorter lifetimes than free excitons, leading to a population difference of the corresponding excitonic states and free exciton trapping within a 1--100 ps window. Band-edge photoexcitation of free and defect-bound exciton states reveals ultrafast interconversion within ~150 fs (comparable to our temporal resolution), indicating possible coherent coupling between these states. We further demonstrate efficient up-conversion of defect-bound excitons to free excitons with photon energies up to ~300 meV below the free exciton resonance. These findings provide insights into the ultrafast dynamics of defect-bound excitons in TMDCs and their coupling with free excitons, which are relevant to defect-engineered optoelectronic, quantum photonic, and valleytronic applications.

</details>


### [129] [Phonon-modulated Kerr nonlinearity in ultrathin 2H-MoTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18830)
*Shaoxiang Sheng,Yang Luo,Chenyu Wang,Sayooj Sateesh,Yaxian Wang,Marko Burghard,Sayantan Patra,Bhumika Chauhan,Ashish Arora,Sheng Meng,Manish Garg*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种低功率相位敏感非线性光谱技术，用于实时监测和控制少层2H-MoTe2中的相干声子动力学，通过交叉相位调制实现背景自由检测，并利用双泵浦脉冲方案实现对特定声子模式的精确控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 控制光驱动量子材料中的非平衡响应对于能源转换、超快电子学和量子计算应用至关重要。传统非线性光谱方法通常需要高强度激光脉冲（>10 GW/cm²）且存在强背景干扰，限制了其在低功率条件下的应用。

Method: 开发了一种相位敏感非线性光谱技术，在低激光功率（~10 kW/cm²，脉冲能量~10 pJ）下运行，利用超短（~10 fs）泵浦脉冲实现相干声子的位移激发。通过交叉相位调制（cross-phase modulation, XPM）探测材料克尔非线性（Kerr nonlinearity）的周期性调制，结合双色非简并泵浦-探测测量和时间依赖密度泛函理论（time-dependent density-functional theory, TDDFT）计算解析耦合动力学。

Result: 该技术实现了对少层（3-5层）2H-MoTe2中相干声子的实时监测和主动控制，通过调整泵浦脉冲强度可选择性地放大或衰减非线性响应。相位调制导致探测光谱的谱宽展宽和质心（center of mass, COM）随时间振荡，实现了背景自由检测。双泵浦脉冲方案能够精确控制声子振荡，选择性激活或抑制特定声子模式并相应调制克尔非线性。

Conclusion: 所提出的低功率相位敏感非线性光谱技术为研究量子材料中的非平衡电子-声子耦合动力学提供了有效工具，实现了对相干声子的实时监测和精确控制，为超快电子学和量子计算应用奠定了基础。

Abstract: Controlling nonequilibrium responses in optically driven quantum materials is essential for advancing applications in energy conversion, ultrafast electronics, and quantum computation. Nonlinear optical spectroscopy serves as a powerful tool to investigate ultrafast electron and phonon dynamics in these systems; however, conventional nonlinear approaches often require intense laser pulses (> 10 GW/cm2) and typically encounter a strong background. Here, we introduce a phase-sensitive nonlinear spectroscopic technique that operates at low laser powers (~ 10 kW/cm2, pulse energies ~ 10 pJ) and enables real-time monitoring and active control of coherent phonons in a few-layer (three to five) thick 2H-MoTe2. Upon excitation with ultrashort (~ 10 fs) pump pulses, we achieve displacive excitation of coherent phonons, which periodically modulate the Kerr nonlinearity of the material, leading to cross-phase modulation (XPM) of a delayed probe pulse. This phase modulation induces spectral broadening and oscillations in the center of mass (COM) of the probe spectrum in time, enabling the detection of subtle nonlinear optical responses in a background-free manner. The nonlinear response can be selectively amplified or attenuated by adjusting the strength of the pump pulse, which controls the distribution of photoexcited carriers in the electronic bands. By combining two-color nondegenerate pump-probe measurements and time-dependent density-functional theory (TDDFT) calculations, we directly resolve the coupled nonequilibrium electronic and phonon dynamics. A dual-pump pulse scheme enables precise control of phonon oscillations, allowing selective activation or suppression of specific phonon modes and correspondingly the modulation of the Kerr nonlinearity.

</details>

### [130] [Robust Near-Critical Dynamics in Heavy-Tailed Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18478)
*Ryota Kojima*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出重尾（heavy-tailed）突触连接性作为生物神经网络鲁棒近临界（near-critical）动力学的一种机制，替代了传统高斯平均场理论中需要精细调谐的脆弱临界状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临界性假说（criticality hypothesis）认为生物神经网络在相变（phase transition）附近运行，但在标准高斯平均场理论（Gaussian mean-field theories）中，这一机制显得脆弱且需要精细调谐（fine tuning）。

Method: 通过发展柯西分布（Cauchy-distributed）耦合的动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory），将宏观动力学简化为具有全局李雅普诺夫势（global Lyapunov potential）的一维梯度流（one-dimensional gradient flow）。

Result: 该理论展示了一个连续相变（continuous phase transition），其中集体活动（collective activity）随临界距离的平方根增长，静态敏感性（static susceptibility）仅以平方根而非线性方式发散。这产生了自动增益控制（automatic gain control）机制。

Conclusion: 重尾突触（heavy-tailed synapses）被识别为无序神经回路（disordered neural circuits）中鲁棒近临界动力学的关键微观起源，为临界性假说提供了更稳健的理论基础。

Abstract: The criticality hypothesis posits that biological neural networks operate near a phase transition, yet within standard Gaussian mean-field theories this regime appears fragile and requires fine tuning. Here we show that heavy-tailed synaptic connectivity provides a robust alternative mechanism. By developing a dynamical mean-field theory for Cauchy-distributed couplings, we reduce the macroscopic dynamics to a one-dimensional gradient flow with a global Lyapunov potential. The resulting theory exhibits a continuous phase transition in which collective activity grows with the square root of the distance to criticality, and static susceptibility diverges only as the square root rather than linearly as in Gaussian mean-field theories. This structure gives rise to an emergent automatic gain control: activity-dependent noise fluctuations suppress the effective gain at high activity levels while preserving high susceptibility near the critical point. Extending this mechanism to general symmetric $α$-stable inputs, we identify heavy-tailed synapses as a key microscopic origin of robust near-critical dynamics in disordered neural circuits.

</details>

### [131] [Thermal relaxation asymmetry persists under inertial effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18721)
*Cai Dieball,Aljaž Godec*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究代数证明了从过阻尼（overdamped）到欠阻尼（underdamped）动力学整个范围内相空间（phase space）热弛豫的不对称性，发现远离平衡的加热过程比冷却过程更快。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索相空间热弛豫过程的不对称性，特别是在从过阻尼到欠阻尼动力学的整个范围内，分析远离平衡态（far-from-equilibrium）加热与冷却过程的差异。

Method: 采用代数证明方法，分析相空间弛豫（phase-space relaxation）过程，包括欠阻尼动力学情形。通过隔离熵产生（entropy production）中的相关弛豫贡献，研究线性驱动远离平衡态的欠阻尼动力学。

Result: 研究证明在从过阻尼到欠阻尼动力学的整个范围内，远离平衡的加热过程都比冷却过程更快。在欠阻尼动力学中，位置和速度的耦合进一步凸显了这种不经过局部平衡（local equilibria）的热弛豫过程的复杂性。

Conclusion: 广义方法揭示，在过阻尼极限下，速度自由度（velocity degrees of freedom）的超额自由能（excess free energy）贡献不会平凡消失，而是受到过阻尼系统中温度淬火（temperature quenches）精确解释的影响。

Abstract: We algebraically prove the asymmetry in thermal relaxation in phase space in the entire range from overdamped dynamics to underdamped dynamics. We show that for the same setup as for overdamped dynamics, even in the more general case of phase-space relaxation, i.e., underdamped dynamics, far-from-equilibrium heating is faster than cooling. Upon isolating the relevant relaxational contribution to the entropy production, we find that the asymmetry persist for underdamped dynamics that are linearly driven out of equilibrium. The coupling of positions and velocities emerging in this generalization further underscores, in a striking manner, the intricate dynamics of such thermal relaxation processes that do not pass through local equilibria. Investigating the overdamped limit, our generalized approach reveals, interestingly, that an excess free energy contribution from the velocity degrees of freedom does not trivially vanish in the overdamped limit, but is instead affected by the precise interpretation of temperature quenches in overdamped systems.

</details>


### [132] [Stationary $1/f^α$ noise in discrete models of the Kardar-Parisi-Zhang class](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18515)
*Rahul Chhimpa,Avinash Chand Yadav*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究在KPZ普适类离散模型中，分析了单层单元内固定位置高度涨落的时间演化，发现小系统可达到稳态，并计算了双时间自相关函数和功率谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究Kardar-Parisi-Zhang（KPZ）普适类离散模型中，固定位置高度涨落的时间相关特性，特别是在小系统中达到稳态的可能性。

Method: 方法包括在单层单元（monolayer unit）中分析固定位置高度涨落的时间演化，独立计算双时间自相关函数（two-time autocorrelation）和功率谱（power spectra），并进行有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling）。

Result: 结果显示：相关函数保持非指数形式，相关时间随系统尺寸发散；功率谱在非平凡频率区呈现1/f^α型标度，谱指数为5/3；时间相关函数遵循动态标度律；涨落具有宽平稳性（wide-sense stationary）。

Conclusion: 结论表明KPZ普适类离散模型中的高度涨落具有宽平稳性，验证了Wiener-Khinchin定理的适用性，并通过标度理论论证支持了这一发现。

Abstract: In discrete models describing growing rough interfaces of the Kardar-Parisi-Zhang universality class, we examine height fluctuations at a fixed site as a function of time in the monolayer unit. For small systems, we show that it is possible to reach the stationary state. We compute the two-time autocorrelation and power spectra independently. The correlation function remains non-exponential and vanishes after a correlation time that diverges with system size. As a result, the power spectra display a lower cutoff that maintains constant power. In the nontrivial frequency regime, we observe $1/f^α$-type scaling with the spectral exponent 5/3. Finite-size scaling reveals that the temporal correlation function follows a dynamic scaling. Our findings, supported by scaling-theoretical arguments, establish that the fluctuations are wide-sense stationary, implying applicability of the Wiener-Khinchin theorem.

</details>

*Anupam Kundu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 推导了具有长程相关性初始状态下相空间密度关联的解析结果，补充了无长程相关情况下的已知结果。基于这些结果获得了适用于两种初始状态的准粒子均值、方差和自相关表达式。

Result: 长程相关性在欧拉广义流体动力学（GHD）方程中引入了扩散尺度的修正项，改变了标准的局域平衡形式。研究发现修正项的具体形式取决于初始状态中存在的长程相关性类型。

Conclusion: 初始状态的长程相关性对硬棒气体中准粒子的随机动力学演化具有重要影响，特别是在广义流体动力学方程的扩散尺度修正方面，修正项形式与初始相关性特征直接相关。

Abstract: We investigate the stochastic dynamics of a quasiparticle within a gas of hard rods, focusing on the evolution of its mean, variance, and autocorrelation for two choices of initial states: (i) one with long-range (LR) correlations and (ii) the other without it. We derive analytical results for the phase space density correlations in the former case to complement the known results for the latter case. These results enable us to obtain expressions for the mean, variance, and autocorrelation of a quasiparticle, which are applicable to both initial states. The LR correlations introduce a diffusive-scale correction to the mean Euler generalized hydrodynamic (GHD) equations, modifying the standard local equilibrium form, and our findings reveal that the form of the correction term depends on the LR correlations present in the initial state.

*Marcin Piotr Pruszczyk,Gregory Schehr*

Method: 讲义首先简要介绍了独立同分布（IID）随机变量的极端值统计，然后讨论了强相关系统的几个范例性例子。重点关注随机游走和布朗运动生成的时间序列，以及随机矩阵理论中的特征值统计。

Conclusion: 该讲义提供了极端值统计在强相关系统中应用的全面概述，强调了EVS在统计物理和无序系统研究中的重要性。通过多个范例展示了如何将EVS方法应用于随机能量模型、随机搜索问题、涨落界面和Kardar-Parisi-Zhang普适类中的有向聚合物等基础问题。

Abstract: These notes are based on lectures delivered by G. Schehr at the XVIth School on Fundamental Problems in Statistical Physics (FPSP), held in Oropa (Italy) from 30 June to 11 July 2025. After a brief introduction to extreme value statistics (EVS) for independent and identically distributed (IID) random variables, we discuss several paradigmatic examples of strongly correlated systems where classical extreme value theory no longer applies. In particular, we focus on time series generated by random walks and Brownian motion, as well as on eigenvalue statistics in random matrix theory. Emphasis is placed on applications of EVS to fundamental problems in statistical physics and disordered systems, including the Random Energy Model, stochastic search problems, as well as fluctuating interfaces, and directed polymers in random media within the Kardar-Parisi-Zhang universality class.

Method: 研究采用光学悬浮纳米粒子在受控真空环境中进行实验。通过这种方法，系统研究了布朗回转器从过阻尼（overdamped）到欠阻尼（underdamped）动力学的转变过程。

Result: 实验表明，虽然非平衡稳态的空间特征随阻尼减小而消失，但旋转动力学和能量学在临界阻尼条件下达到最优。研究揭示了惯性对于最大化纳米机器性能的重要性。

Conclusion: 该发现为设计高效纳米热机（nano heat engines）和过程提供了基础性见解，强调了惯性在优化纳米尺度能量转换系统中的关键作用。

Abstract: Understanding the role of inertia in nanoscale heat transport is fundamental to the design of efficient nano-thermodynamics systems. In this work, we experimentally address the non-equilibrium dynamics of a Brownian gyrator, a paradigmatic model for nano-heat machines, that converts heat flow between two thermal baths into steady-state rotation. Using an optically levitated nanoparticle in a controlled vacuum environment, we study the transition from overdamped to underdamped dynamics of the gyrator. We demonstrate that, while the spatial signature of the non-equilibrium steady state vanishes as damping decreases, the rotational dynamics and energetics are optimized at a critical damping. Our findings reveal the importance of inertia for maximising the performance of nanoscale machines and provide fundamental insights into the design of efficient nano heat engines and processes.

### [136] [Resonances, Recurrence Times and Steady States in Monitored Noisy Qubit Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18996)
*Shuanger Ma,Sabine Tornow,Eli Barkai*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过完整测量（complete measurements）探究了含噪声、频闪监测（stroboscopically monitored）量子比特系统中的非平衡稳态（non-equilibrium steady states）与重现时间（recurrence times）。在无噪声极限下，重现时间呈现整数量子化（integer-quantized），但在接近与遍历性破缺（ergodicity breaking）相关的恢复条件（revival conditions）时采样会出现向低整数的下降。实验发现，远离恢复条件时量子化稳健，但接近时则剧烈破坏，弱噪声即可导致显著偏差甚至将预期下降反转为明显峰值。研究构建了一个统计物理模型来解释此现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究含噪声、受监测的量子比特系统中的非平衡稳态和重现时间特性。特别关注在接近与遍历性破缺相关的恢复条件时，噪声如何影响原本在无噪声极限下观察到的整数量子化重现时间。

Method: 研究方法结合了理论分析与实验验证。理论方面，构建了一个受监测含噪声电路的统计物理模型（statistical-physics model）。实验方面，利用IBM量子平台（IBM quantum platform）进行测量，研究噪声和采样时间对重现时间量子化的影响。

Result: 主要结果包括：在无噪声极限下，重现时间呈现整数量子化，接近恢复条件时采样会出现向低整数的下降。实验发现，远离恢复条件时量子化稳健，但接近时量子化剧烈破坏，即使弱噪声也会导致大偏差，并能将预期的下降反转为明显的峰值。模型表明，采样时间调控了有效无限温度稳态（infinite-temperature steady state）与低温极限（low-temperature limit）之间的交叉（crossover）。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，在受监测的含噪声量子系统中，采样时间调控了由监测驱动的有效无限温度稳态与由热弛豫（thermal-like relaxation）主导的低温极限之间的交叉。接近恢复条件时稳定了低温行为，远离时则恢复无限温度行为。噪声强度和失谐（detuning）在共振附近作为耦合的小参数共同作用，解释了观测到的量子化破坏和峰值反转现象。

Abstract: We study non-equilibrium steady states and recurrence times in noisy, stroboscopically monitored qubit systems using complete measurements. In the noiseless limit, recurrence times are integer-quantized, with dips to lower integers when sampling approaches revival conditions associated with ergodicity breaking. Using an IBM quantum platform, we find that quantization is robust when sampling far from revivals, but breaks down dramatically near revivals: even weak noise produces large deviations and can invert the expected dips into pronounced peaks. To explain this behavior, we formulate a statistical-physics model of monitored noisy circuits in which monitoring drives an effective infinite-temperature steady state while thermal-like relaxation competes to favor a low-temperature limit. We show that the sampling time tunes a crossover between these regimes, near revivals stabilizing low-temperature behavior, and far from revivals restoring infinite-temperature behavior -- with noise strength and detuning acting as coupled small parameters near resonance.

</details>


### [137] [Maximum entropy distributions of wavefunctions at thermal equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19060)
*Jacob T. Willson,Henrik J. Heelweg,Adam P. Willard*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了量子波函数系综在热平衡下的最大熵原理，即所谓的Scrooge系综。研究发现，除了能量期望值约束外，还必须约束测量熵等于系综相对于Gibbs态的Rényi散度，这表明Rényi散度对量子系统热平衡具有未被充分研究的物理重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子系统中波函数系综的分布物理原理尚未明确建立，特别是在热平衡条件下。例如，经典的玻尔兹曼分布无法直接应用于波函数，因为波函数缺乏确定的能量值。

Method: 本文提出了量子波函数系综在热平衡下的最大熵原理（maximum entropy principle），即所谓的Scrooge系综。该方法强调仅约束能量期望值或其本征态分布形状不足以得到有效的平衡态。

Result: 研究发现，除了能量期望值约束外，还必须约束测量熵（measurement entropy）等于系综相对于Gibbs态的Rényi散度（Rényi divergence）。这表明Rényi散度对量子系统热平衡具有重要的物理意义。

Conclusion: Rényi散度在量子系统热平衡中可能具有未被充分研究的物理重要性。Scrooge系综的最大熵原理为理解量子波函数系综在热平衡条件下的分布提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Statistical mechanics reveals that the properties of a macroscopic physical system emerge as an average over an ensemble of statistically independent microscopic subsystems, each occupying a specific microstate. In some models of quantum systems, these microstates are the wavefunction states of individual quantum systems.The physical principles that govern the distribution of a wavefunction ensemble, even under conditions of thermal equilibrium, are not well established. For instance, the canonical Boltzmann distribution cannot be applied to wavefunctions because they lack a definite energy. In this manuscript, we present a maximum entropy principle for the quantum wavefunction ensemble at thermal equilibrium, the so-called Scrooge ensemble. We highlight that a constraint on the energy expectation value, or even the shape of the associated eigenstate distribution, fails to yield a valid equilibrium state. We find that in addition to these constraints, one must also constrain the measurement entropy to be equal to the Rényi divergence of the ensemble with respect to the Gibbs state, indicating that the Rényi divergence may have uninvestigated physical importance to thermal equilibrium in quantum systems.

</details>

### [138] [Critical coupling thresholds for tilted Kuramoto-Vicsek models with a confining potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18185)
*Benedetta Bertoli,Benjamin D. Goddard,Grigorios A. Pavliotis*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了受恒定角度倾斜和约束势作用的Kuramoto-Vicsek自驱动粒子模型及其平均场行为，计算了四种相互作用核归一化变体的临界耦合，并推导了约束场存在时临界耦合与场强的显式函数关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Kuramoto-Vicsek自驱动粒子模型在周期性边界条件下，受恒定角度倾斜和约束势作用时的集体行为，特别关注约束势对系统稳定性的影响。

Method: 采用平均场（Fokker-Planck）方法分析模型行为；在无约束情况下计算四种相互作用核归一化变体的临界耦合；在约束场存在时，通过微扰法构建新稳态并应用特征值微扰理论。

Result: 无约束时均匀密度是稳态，主要不稳定性总是空间均匀的；约束场存在时均匀态不再是稳态，临界阈值随约束强度呈二次增长，倾斜通过稳态修正影响系统但无约束时不影响阈值。

Conclusion: 约束势显著改变系统的稳态特性，临界耦合与约束强度存在明确的函数关系，倾斜效应在约束场存在时通过稳态修正体现，研究还推导了具有一般多色势的稳态自洽方程。

Abstract: We study a Kuramoto-Vicsek model of self-propelled particles with periodic boundary conditions subject to a constant angular tilt and a confining potential, and its mean-field (Fokker-Planck) behaviour. In the absence of confinement, the uniform density is stationary and we compute the critical coupling for four normalisation variants of the interaction kernel, showing that the leading instability is always spatially homogeneous. When the confining field is present, the uniform state is no longer stationary. We construct the new steady state perturbatively and apply eigenvalue perturbation theory to derive an explicit formula for the critical coupling as a function of the field strength. The threshold increases quadratically with confinement strength, and the tilt enters through the steady-state correction despite having no effect on the threshold in the absence of confinement. We verify the prediction numerically and derive self-consistency equations for stationary states with general multichromatic potentials.

### [139] [A Palatini Variational Formulation of Cosserat Elasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18362)
*Lev Steinberg*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种Palatini型几何框架来表述经典Cosserat弹性理论，将标架和旋转联络作为独立变分场处理，揭示了传统度量方法中隐含的几何结构，为缺陷力学的中观理论奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于度量的Cosserat弹性理论未能明确揭示其几何结构，且将平移和旋转自由度在作用量层面混为一谈。本文旨在通过Palatini型几何表述，使这些内在结构显式化，并为后续缺陷力学扩展提供基础。

Method: 采用Palatini型几何表述，将标架（coframe）和旋转联络（rotational connection）作为独立的变分场处理。通过直接推导Euler-Lagrange方程获得控制方程，并利用Noether第一定理从作用量的空间平移和旋转不变性自然导出平衡定律。

Result: 该框架显式地分离了平移和旋转自由度，无需先验施加相容性约束即可得到Cosserat力和力矩平衡定律。无度量线性化恢复了经典应变和扭曲度量，在适当本构假设下与标准张量表述等价。联络场的作用在经典理论中隐含，在此框架下变得明确。

Conclusion: 提出的Palatini型几何框架为Cosserat连续介质提供了统一的几何设定，澄清了联络场的作用，并为后续扩展奠定了基础——其中挠率和曲率可表示演化缺陷密度，导向缺陷力学的中观理论。

Abstract: We present a Palatini-type geometric formulation of classical Cosserat elasticity in which the coframe and rotational connection are treated as independent variational fields. In contrast to conventional metric-based approaches, this formulation makes the underlying geometric structure explicit and separates translational and rotational degrees of freedom at the level of the action. The governing equations are obtained directly as Euler--Lagrange equations and yield the Cosserat force and moment balance laws without imposing compatibility constraints a priori. It is further shown that these balances arise naturally from invariance of the action under spatial translations and rotations via Noether's first theorem, providing a transparent variational interpretation of micropolar mechanics. A metric-free linearization recovers the classical strain and wryness measures and establishes equivalence with standard tensorial formulations under appropriate constitutive assumptions. The proposed framework clarifies the role of the connection field, which remains implicit in classical theories, and provides a unified geometric setting for Cosserat continua. In addition, it establishes the foundation for subsequent extensions in which torsion and curvature represent evolving defect densities and lead to mesoscopic theories of defect mechanics.

</details>


### [140] [On the Finsler variational nature of autoparallels in metric-affine geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18416)
*Lehel Csillag,Nicoleta Voicu,Salah Elgendi,Christian Pfeifer*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文解决了度量仿射几何中自平行线（autoparallels）的变分原理存在性问题，针对具有矢量非度量性（vectorial nonmetricity）的无挠仿射连接，建立了芬斯勒度量化（Finsler metrizability）的充要条件并显式构造了芬斯勒拉格朗日量（Finsler Lagrangian）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在度量仿射几何（metric-affine geometry）中，自平行线通常不具备变分性质，即它们不是任何作用量积分（action integral）的极值。自平行线参数不变作用量原理（parameter-invariant action principle）的存在性是一个长期未解决的开放问题，这等价于连接的芬斯勒度量化问题。

Method: 针对无挠仿射连接（torsion-free affine connections）且具有矢量非度量性（vectorial nonmetricity）的类别进行研究，该类别包含外尔连接（Weyl connections）和薛定谔连接（Schrödinger connections）作为重要子案例。确定了芬斯勒拉格朗日量存在且仅代数依赖于连接的充要条件。

Result: 对于这类连接，确定了芬斯勒度量化存在的充要条件。在芬斯勒拉格朗日量存在的情况下，显式地构造了该拉格朗日量。特别地，证明了广泛类别的此类连接是可芬斯勒度量化的。

Conclusion: 该研究解决了度量仿射几何中长期存在的自平行线变分原理问题，为具有矢量非度量性的无挠仿射连接建立了完整的芬斯勒度量化理论框架，并提供了显式构造方法。

Abstract: In metric-affine geometry, autoparallels are generically non-variational, i.e., they are not extremals of any action integral. The existence of a parameter-invariant action principle for autoparallels is a longstanding open problem, which is equivalent to the so-called Finsler metrizability of the connection, i.e., to the fact that these autoparallels can be interpreted as Finsler geodesics. In this article, we address this problem for the class of torsion-free affine connections with vectorial nonmetricity, which includes, as notable subcases, Weyl and Schrödinger connections. For this class, we determine the necessary and sufficient conditions for the existence of a Finsler Lagrangian that metrizes the connection and depends only algebraically on it. In the cases where such a Finsler Lagrangian exists, we construct it explicitly. In particular, we show that a broad class of such connections is Finsler metrizable.

</details>


### [141] [Radiation damping of the soliton internal mode in 1D quadratic Klein-Gordon equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18605)
*Piotr Bizoń,Tomasz Romańczukiewicz*

Main category: math-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一维二次克莱因-戈登方程（quadratic Klein-Gordon equation）中孤子（soliton）在受到小偶微扰（small even perturbations）时的长时间动力学行为，特别关注内部模（internal mode）与不稳定模（unstable mode）的相互作用。

Method: 在精细调谐初始数据（fine-tuned initial data）构成的余维一（codimension-one）流形上抑制不稳定性，采用三次共振近似（cubic resonant approximation）描述内部模的衰减过程，衰减率由费米黄金定则型系数（Fermi golden rule-type coefficient）确定。

Result: 不稳定性被成功抑制，内部模通过将能量转移至连续谱（continuum）而缓慢衰减，非线性频率偏移（nonlinear frequency shift）和衰减过程均能被三次共振近似准确捕捉，实现了内部模向色散辐射（dispersive radiation）不可逆能量转移的定量描述。

Conclusion: 该研究为孤子内部模的长时间动力学提供了定量框架，通过费米黄金定则机制解释了不可逆能量转移过程，三次共振近似有效描述了衰减率和非线性频率偏移。

Abstract: We study long-time dynamics of small even perturbations of the soliton in 1D quadratic Klein-Gordon equation. The soliton possesses both an internal mode and the unstable mode. On a codimension-one manifold of fine-tuned initial data the instability is suppressed and the internal mode decays slowly by transferring energy into the continuum. We show that this decay and the associated nonlinear frequency shift are accurately captured by a cubic resonant approximation, with the damping rate determined by a Fermi golde rule-type coefficient. This provides a quantitative description of irreversible energy transfer from the internal mode to dispersive radiation.

</details>


### [142] [The Lee-Yang property of isotropic vector ferromagnets and lattice fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18675)
*Yuri Kozitsky*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者针对各向同性自旋模型和场模型，在整数格点$\mathbs{Z}$上进行研究。通过数学证明方法，建立了这些模型在特定条件下的性质。

Result: 研究证明，对于所有偶数维度$D$，在整数格点$\mathbs{Z}$上的各向同性自旋模型和场模型都具有广义Lee-Yang性质。这一结果扩展了先前仅适用于二维情况的结论。

Abstract: The Lee-Yang property of a given spin model means that its partition function has purely imaginary zeros as a function of an external magnetic field. Its suitable generalization is used in the theory of models of isotropic $D$-dimensional spins (rotors) or $D$-component quantum lattice fields. So far, the (generalized) Lee-Yang property has been established only for two-dimensional isotropic models. In this work, we prove that isotropic spin and field models living on $\mathds{Z}$ have this property for all even $D$.

### [143] [Duality of generalized Maxwell theories as an equivalence in derived geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19161)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用导出微分几何方法，将Batalin-Vilkovisky形式体系与微分上同调相结合。通过底层上链复形层（sheaves of cochain complexes）的模型来建模微分上同调，并计算其在闭黎曼流形（closed Riemannian manifolds）上的前推（pushforward）。

Result: 成功构建了电荷量子化的模空间，并展示了不同类型广义麦克斯韦理论之间的阿贝尔对偶性。同时实现了广义麦克斯韦理论在闭黎曼流形上的紧致化（compactification）。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种统一的非微扰框架，能够同时处理广义麦克斯韦理论的模空间结构、电荷量子化和对偶性关系，为高维规范理论的研究提供了新的数学工具。

Abstract: We propose a non-perturbative description of the moduli spaces encoding p-form generalized Maxwell theories in any dimension, using derived differential geometry. Our approach synthesizes the Batalin--Vilkovisky formalism with differential cohomology. Within this framework we formulate Dirac charge quantization and show how such charge-quantized moduli spaces exhibit abelian duality between generalized Maxwell theories of different types. We also describe the compactification of generalized Maxwell theories along closed Riemannian manifolds by computing the pushforward of the underlying sheaves of cochain complexes that model differential cohomology.

Abstract: We consider the soliton solutions of a recently proposed coupled Sasa-Satsuma-mKdV equation using the Kadomtsev-Petviashvili reduction method. The system consists of a complex-valued component coupled with a real-valued one. Under zero or nonzero boundary conditions, we derive four distinct classes of soliton solutions: bright-bright, dark-dark, bright-dark, and dark-bright. We perform asymptotic analysis of soliton collisions for each class of solutions, in which inelastic collisions are observed between bright-bright solitons. ### [145] [Nonlinear Incompressible Shear Wave Models in Hyperelasticity and Viscoelasticity Frameworks, with Applications to Love Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18296)
*Shawn Samuel Carl McAdam,Samuel Opoku Agyemang,Alexei Cheviakov*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立适用于任意形式应变能密度函数的通用方程，以描述不可压缩超弹性材料中的剪切位移，并分析非线性Love型波在材料界面上的传播行为。该工作扩展了传统线性Love波理论至非线性领域，适用于广泛的超粘弹性材料类别。

Method: 提出了描述不可压缩超弹性材料剪切位移的通用方程，适用于任意形式的应变能密度函数。针对立方Yeoh模型，推导出包含三次和五次微分多项式项的剪切波方程，其中粘弹性贡献以包含混合导数$u_{xxt}$的色散项形式体现。进行了(2+1)维全数值模拟，分析双层固体中波的传播，重点关注源位置和材料力学性能的影响。

Result: 数值模拟追踪了界面非线性Love波和自由上表面剪切波。研究表明，在完全非线性情况下，界面波和表面波的可变波速通常满足线性Love波存在条件$c_1 < \abs{v} < c_2$，同时在大时间尺度下趋向于较大的材料波速$c_1$或$c_2$。对于立方Yeoh模型，剪切波方程包含三次和五次微分多项式项，体现了粘弹性效应。

Conclusion: 本文建立的通用方程框架能够有效描述不可压缩超弹性材料中的剪切位移和界面波传播。非线性Love型波在材料界面上的行为满足线性Love波的基本存在条件，但在大时间尺度下表现出向较大材料波速收敛的趋势。该模型为分析超粘弹性材料中的非线性波传播现象提供了理论工具。

Abstract: General equations describing shear displacements in incompressible hyperelastic materials, holding for an arbitrary form of strain energy density function, are presented and applied to the description of nonlinear Love-type waves propagating on an interface between materials with different mechanical properties. The model is valid for a broad class of hyper-viscoelastic materials. For a cubic Yeoh model, shear wave equations contain cubic and quintic differential polynomial terms, including viscoelasticity contributions in terms of dispersion terms that include mixed derivatives $u_{xxt}$ of the material displacement. Full (2+1)-dimensional numerical simulations of waves propagating in the bulk of a two-layered solid are undertaken and analyzed with respect to the source position and mechanical properties of the layers. Interfacial nonlinear Love waves and free upper surface shear waves are tracked; it is demonstrated that in the fully nonlinear case, the variable wave speed of interface and surface waves generally satisfies the linear Love wave existence condition $c_1 < \abs{v} < c_2$, while tending to the larger material wave speed $c_1$ or $c_2$ for large times.

</details>


### [146] [$\mathrm{PGL}(3)$-invariant integrable systems from factorisation of linear differential and difference operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18386)
*Frank Nijhoff,Linyu Peng,Cheng Zhang,Da-jun Zhang*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种统一方法，从线性谱问题及其分解出发，构建连续和离散的PGL(3)-不变可积系统。该方法推广了施瓦茨导数和交比到秩3情形，建立了Boussinesq系统的精确离散化和多维相容性，并揭示了到PGL(2)-不变方程的约化机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在建立一种统一框架，用于构造连续和离散的PGL(3)-不变可积系统。该研究动机源于将施瓦茨导数（Schwarzian derivative）和交比（cross-ratio）等经典概念推广到更高秩（rank-3）情形，并探索相关Boussinesq系统的精确离散化与多维相容性。

Method: 方法基于三阶谱问题（third-order spectral problems）及其分解。首先从线性谱问题出发，推导微分和差分不变量的显式形式；然后通过分解诱导谱问题间的对偶性，建立Boussinesq系统的精确离散化与多维相容性；最后发展几何提升-解耦机制（geometric lifting-decoupling mechanism）来解释系统约化。

Result: 研究结果包括：推导了连续和离散的PGL(3)-不变Boussinesq系统，作为施瓦茨KdV（Schwarzian KdV）和交比方程的自然秩3推广；建立了PGL(3)-不变生成偏微分方程系统及其拉格朗日结构（Lagrangian structure），其中格点参数作为独立变量，为Boussinesq层级提供生成系统。

Conclusion: 本文成功构建了统一的PGL(3)-不变可积系统框架，将经典概念推广到更高秩情形。所发展的几何提升-解耦机制解释了系统到PGL(2)-不变Boussinesq方程的约化，而生成偏微分方程系统为Boussinesq层级提供了完整描述。

Abstract: In this paper, we present a unified approach to constructing continuous and discrete $\mathrm{PGL}(3)$-invariant integrable systems, formulated in terms of the common dependent variables $z_1,z_2$, from linear spectral problems and their factorisation. Starting from third-order spectral problems, we first provide explicit forms of the differential and difference invariants, generalising the Schwarzian derivative and cross-ratio to the rank-$3$ setting. The factorisation induces dualities among linear spectral problems, underlying the exact discretisation and multi-dimensional consistency of the associated Boussinesq systems. Then, we derive both continuous and discrete $\mathrm{PGL}(3)$-invariant Boussinesq systems, representing natural rank-$3$ generalisations of the Schwarzian KdV and cross-ratio equations. A geometric lifting-decoupling mechanism is developed to explain the reduction of these systems to the $\mathrm{PGL}(2)$-invariant Boussinesq equations. Finally, we derive a ${\mathrm{PGL}}(3)$-invariant system of generating PDEs together with its Lagrangian structure, in which the lattice parameters serve as independent variables, providing the generating PDE system for the Boussinesq hierarchy.

### [147] [A stable and fast method for solving multibody scattering problems via the method of fundamental solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19113)
*Yunhui Cai,Joar Bagge,Per-Gunnar Martinsson*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种用于求解二维和三维声学多体散射问题的数值方法。该方法通过局部计算获得每个散射体的高精度散射算子近似，然后利用这些散射矩阵构建全局线性系统，即使对于包含大量散射体的问题也能保持较好的条件数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在解决声学多体散射问题的数值计算挑战，特别是当涉及大量散射体时传统方法面临的计算复杂性和数值稳定性问题。需要开发一种既能保持高精度又具有良好可扩展性的数值方法。

Method: 该方法首先通过局部计算为每个散射体构建高精度的散射矩阵（scattering matrix）近似。然后利用这些局部散射矩阵形成全局线性系统，该系统具有良好的条件数。关键创新在于允许使用潜在病态的技术（如基本解方法（MFS））构建局部散射矩阵，同时仍能保持全局求解器的可扩展性和数值稳定性。

Result: 所提出的算法能够处理包含大量散射体的声学多体散射问题，生成的全局系数矩阵具有相对良好的条件数。该线性系统适用于迭代求解器，并可通过快速算法（如快速多极子方法（fast multipole method））加速矩阵-向量乘法运算。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种简单有效的数值方案，其中基本解方法（MFS）比基于Nyström或Galerkin方法离散化边界积分方程的传统技术更易于实现。该算法在保持数值稳定性和可扩展性的同时，能够高效处理大规模多体散射问题。

Abstract: The paper describes a numerical method for solving acoustic multibody scattering problems in two and three dimensions. The idea is to compute a highly accurate approximation to the scattering operator for each body through a local computation, and then use these scattering matrices to form a global linear system. The resulting coefficient matrix is relatively well-conditioned, even for problems involving a very large number of scatterers. The linear system is amenable to iterative solvers, and can readily be accelerated via fast algorithms for the matrix-vector multiplication such as the fast multipole method. The key point of the work is that the local scattering matrices can be constructed using potentially ill-conditioned techniques such as the method of fundamental solutions (MFS), while still maintaining scalability and numerical stability of the global solver. The resulting algorithm is simple, as the MFS is far simpler to implement than alternative techniques based on discretizing boundary integral equations using Nyström or Galerkin.

The core of this work lies in the derivation of this canonical identification, the reduced Hamilton-Cartan equations, and a reduced covariant bracket that describes the dynamics. Finally, this theoretical framework is illustrated with a fundamental example: molecular strands.

### [149] [More on near-horizon charges black holes with gravitational hair in three dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18072)
*Seyed Naseh Sajadi,Supakchai Ponglertsakul,Julio Oliva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了高阶曲率引力理论中的近地平线荷（near-horizon charges），将协变相空间方法（covariant phase phase-space method）推广至包含黎曼张量（Riemann tensor）四次项的理论，并在旋转BTZ时空和毛状黑洞（hairy black holes）中检验了相关公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在继续探索高阶曲率引力中的近地平线荷，寻找导致普适行为（universal behaviors）的理论部分。研究动机源于弦理论（String Theory）中α'修正的背景，特别是在Type II理论中，爱因斯坦-希尔伯特拉格朗日量（Einstein-Hilbert Lagrangian）的一阶修正为α'³R⁴项。

Method: 首先对协变相空间方法进行了全面修订和公式化，使其适用于任意维度下包含黎曼张量四次项的引力理论。然后将这些公式应用于旋转BTZ时空的近地平线渐近对称性（near-horizon asymptotic symmetries），并在静态和旋转毛状黑洞中计算了相关荷。

Result: 在旋转BTZ时空中，黑洞热力学第一定律（first law of black hole thermodynamics）被一致地恢复。对于新大质量引力（New Massive Gravity）等理论，发现其允许具有引力毛（gravitational hair）的黑洞存在，且熵可以从微观角度解释。理论在真空线性化时获得额外的规范对称性（gauge symmetry）。

Conclusion: 本研究将先前仅包含二次项的工作扩展至四次项，为高阶曲率引力中的近地平线荷计算提供了系统框架。附录中提供了广义拉格朗日量的显式表达式，便于连续阅读和理解。

Abstract: With the aim of continuing the exploration of near-horizon charges in higher-curvature gravity, searching for sectors leading to universal behaviors, we first provide a thorough revision and formulae of the covariant phase-space method applied to arbitrary gravitational theories containing up to quartic terms in the Riemann tensor in arbitrary dimension. These results can be applied in diverse setups, in particular in the context of $α'$ corrections to String Theory, where it is known that in Type II theories, the first correction to the Einstein-Hilbert Lagrangian goes as $α'^3 \mathcal{R}^4$. Then, we test these formulae for near horizon asymptotic symmetries of the rotating BTZ spacetime where the first law of black hole thermodynamics is consistently recovered. It was recently realized that a subset of these higher curvature gravities do admit black holes with gravitational hair, whose entropy can be microscopically accounted for, as is the case of New Massive Gravity. In this case, the four maximally symmetric vacua of the theory coincide, and the theory acquires an extra gauge symmetry when linearized around such a vacuum. We study the near-horizon asymptotic symmetries and compute the associated charges, both in the static and rotating hairy black holes, extending up to $\mathcal{R}^4$, a work that was previously done only up to a quadratic term. In order to allow for a continuous lecture on the work, we report the explicit expressions of the general Lagrangians in the appendices.

Result: 分析表明Spavieri等人的主张基于循环论证，因此其声称Wang等人的实验否定了狭义相对论的结论在逻辑上不成立。

Conclusion: Spavieri等人对Wang等人干涉实验的解读存在根本性的逻辑缺陷，其否定狭义相对论的结论无效，实验本身并未提供支持绝对同时性概念的有效证据。

Abstract: In this comment, we demonstrate that the claim by Spavieri et al., asserting that Wang et al.'s interferometric experiment disproves the special theory of relativity by revealing that simultaneity must be an absolute concept independent of the observer's state of motion, is based on circular reasoning and therefore constitutes a logical fallacy.

Result: 论文将展示如何通过黎曼几何中的自然元素，将具有相等量子数的多重态转化为具有相等引力场的局部多重态。通过引入新标架，能够实现SU(N)对称性与引力场的耦合。
