Abstract: The discovery of the SU(3) symmetry was fundamental as to establishing an ordering principle in particle physics. We already studied how to couple the SU(3) symmetry to the gravitational field in four-dimensional curved Lorentzian spacetimes. The multiplets of equal quantum numbers are translated through natural elements in Riemannian geometry into local multiplets of equal gravitational field. As quark physics developed since the seventies, it was necessary to incorporate new symmetries to the models, that ensued in the incorporation of new quantum numbers like Charm, for example. Charm is an additive quantum number like isospin T3 and hypercharge Y and the standard T3-Y diagrams were extended onto another third axis. Then, instead of the fundamental triplet we have a quartet {u; d; s; c} as the smallest representation of the symmetry group, leading to the introduction of SU(4) as the new group of symmetries. In this paper we will not restrict ourselves exclusively to the symmetry group SU(4) and we will set out to analyze the coupling of the SU(N) symmetry to the gravitational field. To this end new tetrads will be introduced as we did for the SU(3) x SU(2) x U(1) case. These tetrads have outstanding properties that enable these constructions. New theorems will be proved regarding the isomorphic nature of these local symmetry gauge groups and tensor products of groups of local tetrad transformations. This is a paper about grand field uni?fication in four-dimensional curved Lorentzian spacetimes.

### [152] [The Steep Price of No Hair in Thiemann Regularized Loop Quantum Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18175)
*Meysam Motaharfar,Parampreet Singh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 基于Thiemann正则化的圈量子宇宙学（loop quantum cosmology）在各项同性模型中解决了大爆炸奇点问题并产生反弹，但在Bianchi-I时空的量子化中，虽然存在抑制各向异性剪切的机制，却导致宇宙无法真正经典化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索Thiemann正则化圈量子宇宙学在Bianchi-I时空中的普朗克尺度物理。主要动机是理解各向异性剪切（anisotropic shear）的阻尼机制及其对宇宙经典化的影响，并澄清Gan等人近期研究结果的物理起源和局限性。

Method: 采用基于Thiemann正则化程序的圈量子宇宙学方法，将其应用于Bianchi-I时空的量子化。通过分析各向异性模型中的量子引力效应，研究各向异性剪切的阻尼机制和宇宙演化特征。

Result: 研究显示，与各项同性模型类似，Bianchi-I时空中存在一个涌现的德西特相（emergent de Sitter phase），该相自然阻尼各向异性剪切并消除宇宙毛发（cosmic hair）。然而，这种各向同性化（isotropization）导致宇宙无法达到真正的经典状态，尽管能够实现宏观的后反弹（post-bounce）区域。进一步证明该各向同性化机制是非普适的（non-generic）。

Conclusion: Thiemann正则化圈量子宇宙学中的各向异性剪切阻尼机制源于一种新颖的量子引力效应，该效应独立于初始条件和物质含量。然而，这种各向同性化机制存在严重局限性，即阻止宇宙真正经典化，且该机制本身是非普适的。研究结果解释了Gan等人发现的物理机制起源及其限制条件。

Abstract: Loop quantum cosmology based on Thiemann's regularization procedure leads to the resolution of the big bang singularity and bounce in the isotropic setting. A key distinction from standard loop quantum cosmology is that, in this framework, either the pre-bounce or post-bounce epoch is necessarily characterized by an emergent Planckian de Sitter phase. In this work we explore the Planckian physics of Thiemann regularized loop quantization of the Bianchi-I spacetimes. We show that as in the isotropic model, there exists an emergent de Sitter phase which naturally dampens anisotropic shear and removes cosmic hair. However, this isotropization comes at a steep price: although a macroscopic post-bounce regime is achieved, the universe never becomes truly classical. We further demonstrate that this isotropization mechanism is non-generic. These results help clarify and reinterpret recent results by Gan et al. [1] that, in anisotropic Thiemann regularized loop quantum cosmology, quantum gravity effects generically damp anisotropic shear in a way that is independent of initial conditions and the matter content, and that this anisotropic shear damping mechanism arises from a novel quantum gravity effect. Our work explains the origin of this mechanism and its limitations.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在将四维时空中的Robinson-Trautman演化推广到(2+1)维，同时保留关键结构特征。研究动机源于四维情况下面积保持Calabi流的作用，希望在低维引力中建立一个由零辐射驱动的耗散动力学简单玩具模型。

Method: 采用最近研究的精确度规族，选择具有宇宙学常数并由零流体（null fluid）源的非稳态几何。度规完全由单个正函数P(u,φ)确定，而相应的物质内容编码在零流体密度中。受四维中面积保持Calabi流的启发，为P(u,φ)引入了四阶长度保持演化方程。

Result: 对于负宇宙学常数，稳态构型对应于boosted BTZ黑洞。数值解强烈支持一般正则初始数据P(0,φ)弛豫到稳态区域。所得系统在结构上与真实引力辐射相关现象具有多个相似性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了一个(2+1)维时空中的Robinson-Trautman演化模型，为低维引力中的零辐射驱动耗散动力学提供了一个结构简单的玩具模型，并显示出与四维情况相似的关键特征。

Abstract: We propose a Robinson-Trautman evolution in $(2+1)$-dimensional spacetime that retains key structural features of the four-dimensional case. We consider a recently studied exact family of metrics to select a nonstationary geometry with a cosmological constant, sourced by a null fluid. The metric is completely determined by a single positive function $P(u,φ)$, while the corresponding matter content is encoded in a null-fluid density. Motivated by the role of the area-preserving Calabi flow in four dimensions, we introduce a fourth-order length-preserving evolution equation for $P(u,φ)$ whose stationary configurations correspond, for negative cosmological constant, to boosted BTZ black holes. Numerical solutions strongly support the relaxation of generic regular initial data $P(0,φ)$ toward the stationary sector. The resulting system provides a simple toy model for dissipative dynamics driven by null radiation in lower-dimensional gravity, with several structural similarities to phenomena associated with genuine gravitational radiation.

</details>


### [154] [Holographic Quantum Foam: Theoretical Underpinnings and Observational Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18277)
*Eric Steinbring,Y. Jack Ng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文探讨全息量子泡沫（HQF）理论及其宇宙学意义，重点分析了GRB221009A观测数据与HQF预测的一致性，为检验量子引力效应提供了新途径。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子涨落导致时空泡沫化，全息量子泡沫（holographic quantum foam, HQF）理论预测宇宙存在暗物质/暗能量（dark sector）。当前最重要的挑战是检验HQF理论与实验/观测是否一致，特别是通过寻找普朗克尺度物理导致的遥远点源模糊化证据。

Method: 通过分析GRB221009A这一极端明亮且高能的事件，获取了从光学/近红外到X射线乃至最高能量伽马射线的全谱段观测数据。同时计算了真实望远镜观测GRB时HQF加宽的点扩散函数（point-spread function, PSF）。

Result: 观测数据显示所有谱段数据均与HQF导致的模糊化效应一致。全息量子泡沫预测的暗物质/暗能量组分在宇宙学上（至少定性）与观测相符，且其量子遵循无限统计（infinite statistics）或量子玻尔兹曼统计（quantum Boltzmann statistics）而非常见的费米或玻色统计。

Conclusion: GRB221009A的观测数据为检验全息量子泡沫理论提供了有力证据，支持了量子引力效应在宇宙尺度上的可观测性。这些发现有助于验证普朗克尺度物理对遥远天体观测的影响，推进对量子时空本质的理解。

Abstract: Spacetime is foamy due to quantum fluctuations. Various gedanken experiments show that distances fluctuate by amounts consistent with the holographic principle, hence the name "holographic quantum foam" (HQF). One important prediction of HQF is that necessarily there exists a dark sector in the universe. The resulting cosmology is found (at least qualitatively) to be consistent with observations. Interestingly the quanta of the dark sector are found not to obey the familiar (fermionic or bosonic) statistics, but the exotic statistics known as infinite statistics (or quantum Boltzmann statistics). The most important challenge now is to check if HQF is consistent with experiments/observations. One way is to look for observational evidence of blurred distant point-sources due to physics at the Planck scale. For over two decades it has been debated whether those tiny inherent uncertainties in time and path-length can accumulate in transiting electromagnetic wavefronts from quasars and Gamma-Ray Bursts (GRBs). But a recent event is special: GRB221009A was extremely bright and energetic. That allowed follow-up across the whole spectrum from the optical/near-infrared through to X-rays, and including the highest-ever-recorded energy gamma-rays; all consistent with blurring by HQF. Those data, and a calculation of the HQF-widened point-spread function (PSF) for real telescopes viewing a GRB are presented.

### [155] [Contrasting behaviour of two spherically symmetric perfect fluids near a weak null singularity in a spherically symmetric black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18340)
*Raya V. Mancheva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对比了两种球对称物质模型在具有弱零奇点（weak null singularity）的球对称时空中的行为：尘埃（dust）模型显示能量密度有界，而刚体流体（stiff perfect fluid）模型则显示能量密度发散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在对比不同物质模型在弱零奇点（weak null singularity）附近的行为差异。该研究背景基于Luk-Oh和Dafermos对爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量场系统中亚极端Reissner-Nordström扰动的强宇宙监督猜想（strong cosmic censorship conjecture）的证明工作。

Method: 采用两种不同方法：首先研究尘埃（dust）落入弱零奇点的柯西问题（Cauchy problem），分析其速度流和能量密度行为；其次研究刚体流体（stiff perfect fluid）落入弱零奇点的特征初值问题（characteristic initial value problem），通过将其速度和能量密度与满足齐次线性波动方程（homogeneous linear wave equation）的标量场相关联进行分析。

Result: 尘埃模型显示：速度流在奇点处无壳交叉（shell-crossing），速度矢量保持类时性（timelike），能量密度有界。刚体流体模型显示：能量密度在接近弱零奇点时发散，内向速度分量（ingoing component）发散而外向分量（outgoing component）趋于零，速度矢量趋近于与奇异超曲面相切的内向零矢量（ingoing null vector）。

Conclusion: 不同物质模型在弱零奇点附近表现出截然不同的行为：尘埃保持规则性而刚体流体呈现发散性。这一对比揭示了物质性质对奇点附近物理行为的重要影响，为理解强宇宙监督猜想（strong cosmic censorship conjecture）在不同物质模型下的有效性提供了新见解。

Abstract: In this work we contrast the behaviour of two spherically symmetric matter models in a class of spherically symmetric spacetimes which feature a weak null singularity. This class in particular contains spherically symmetric perturbations of subextremal Reissner-Nordström under the Einstein--Maxwell--scalar field system, a system for which a $C^2$ formulation of the strong cosmic censorship conjecture was proved by Luk-Oh, arXiv:1702.05715 and Dafermos, arXiv:1201.1797. Firstly, we consider the Cauchy problem of spherically symmetric dust falling into the weak null singularity (WNS) where the initial dust velocity is normal to a smooth spacelike curve with certain properties. We prove that the flow of the dust velocity does not experience any shell-crossing before or at the singularity, the velocity vector remains timelike, and that the dust energy density remains bounded as matter approaches the singularity. Secondly, we consider the characteristic initial value problem for stiff perfect fluid falling into the WNS. By relating the stiff fluid velocity and energy density to a scalar field satisfying the homogeneous linear wave equation, we prove that this energy density becomes infinite as we approach the weak null singularity. Furthermore, we show that the ingoing component of the stiff fluid velocity blows up while the outgoing component approaches zero at the singularity. Therefore the velocity vector approaches an ingoing null vector tangent to the singular hypersurface.

### [156] [Black Hole--Entropy Container or Creator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18374)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者采用线性放大器（linear amplifier）模型进行分析，论证该放大器本身没有熵，但在运行过程中会发射熵。该模型与黑洞行为密切相关，用于类比分析黑洞的熵产生机制。

Result: 分析表明黑洞本身不具有熵，而是在蒸发过程中创造并发射熵。总发射熵与传统黑洞熵表达式相同，与黑洞质量的平方成正比。

Conclusion: 论文得出结论：黑洞不拥有熵，而是在其运行过程中创造并发射熵。这一结论挑战了传统黑洞热力学观点，为理解黑洞熵的本质提供了新视角。

Abstract: Do black holes possess entropy or do they create it? The dominant assumption is that they possess entropy, and a they evaporate that entropy is emitted and decreases. In this paper I use a model of a linear amplifier, in which I argue that the amplifier has not entropy and yet it emits entropy in the process of it operation. This model is closely related to behaviour of black holes, resulting in answer the question of that title that black holes do not have entropy, but nevertheless them create and emit entropy with the total entropy emitted being the same as the usual expression proportional to the square of the mas of the black hole.

Abstract: We investigate multipartite quantum correlations by analyzing the mutual information of N-partite states for both free bosonic and fermionic fields in the background of a Garfinkle-Horowitz-Strominger (GHS) dilaton black hole. Focusing on multipartite GHZ and W states, we examine how the Hawking effect influences the N-partite mutual information when one observer hovers near the event horizon while the remaining observers stay in the asymptotically flat region. By tracing over the inaccessible modes inside the event horizon, we derive analytical expressions for the N-partite mutual information in dilaton spacetime for both bosonic and fermionic fields. Our results show that fermionic mutual information is larger than its bosonic counterpart under the influence of the dilaton black hole, whereas the fermionic relative entropy of coherence (REC) is smaller than the bosonic REC. Moreover, the mutual information of GHZ states is consistently larger than that of W states, while the REC of GHZ states is smaller than that of W states in curved spacetime. These findings indicate that the choice of quantum resources should be tailored to the particle species and state structure in relativistic quantum information tasks to optimize their operational efficiency.

Method: 通过选择合适的耦合函数（coupling function），使理论容纳解析的带电Taub-NUT几何作为解；分析无标量背景在特定参数区域的不稳定性，研究由此分岔出的带毛（hairy）带电Taub-NUT黑洞分支。

Abstract: We investigate the spontaneous scalarization of charged Taub-NUT black holes within the framework of Einstein-Maxwell-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity. By selecting a suitable coupling function, the theory admits the analytic charged Taub-NUT geometry as a solution. We demonstrate that this scalar-free background becomes unstable within specific parameter regimes, leading to the bifurcation of a new branch of hairy charged Taub-NUT black holes. These solutions are characterized by a two-dimensional parameter space spanned by the electric charge and the NUT parameter. We conduct a systematic study of their properties, specifically the scalar charge, temperature, and entropy. Our analysis reveals that the entropy of the scalarized solutions exhibits particularly compelling features. Two universal characteristics emerge: first, the entropy of the hairy black hole is strictly greater than that of its scalar-free counterpart; second, the entropy reaches a local maximum precisely at the bifurcation point. Notably, when the electric charge is fixed, this maximum entropy value remains universal across a specific range of the mass parameter.

### [159] [Exact pp-wave solutions in shift-symmetric higher-order scalar-tensor theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18794)
*Masato Minamitsuji*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索高阶标量-张量理论框架下的精确平面波引力波解，这些解代表了超越线性近似的完全非线性辐射时空，有助于理解修正引力理论中的非线性效应。

Method: 采用平移对称二次高阶标量-张量理论框架，通过施加耦合函数的代数条件，将引力场方程简化为波剖面的二维拉普拉斯方程。采用线性依赖于横向坐标并任意依赖于推迟零坐标的标量场假设，保持标量场动能项恒定。

Result: 在特定代数条件下，引力场方程简化为真空广义相对论的结构形式。获得了"隐形平面波"解，其中非平凡标量场轮廓与引力波共存但不反作用于时空几何。这些解与Ia类DHOST理论的简并条件完全兼容，并满足当前观测约束。

Abstract: We investigate exact plane-fronted gravitational wave (pp-wave) solutions within the framework of shift-symmetric quadratic-order higher-order scalar--tensor (HOST) theories. These solutions represent fully nonlinear radiative spacetimes that extend beyond the linearized approximation. We demonstrate that under the algebraic conditions on the coupling functions, the gravitational field equations reduce to a two-dimensional Laplace equation for the wave profile, recovering the structural form of vacuum general relativity (GR). By adopting a scalar field ansatz that depends linearly on transverse coordinates and arbitrarily on the retarded null coordinate, we maintain a constant kinetic term of the scalar field. This configuration allows for a \emph{stealth pp-wave} solution, where a nontrivial scalar field profile coexists with the gravitational wave without backreacting on the spacetime geometry. We further show that these stealth configurations are fully compatible with the degeneracy conditions of Class-Ia DHOST theories and satisfy current observational constraints. Finally, we examine the behavior of these solutions under disformal transformations, revealing that while the Brinkmann form is preserved, the stealth property is generically lost due to the mixing of scalar and tensor degrees of freedom. These results establish the robustness of pp-wave solutions in viable DHOST frameworks and highlight their utility for probing nonlinear effects in modified gravity.

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic properties of the Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson black hole, an exact Petrov type D solution of Einstein-Maxwell theory describing a rotating black hole immersed in an external electromagnetic field. While the conserved angular momentum and electric charge can be computed straightforwardly, the conserved mass cannot be obtained through standard integrability methods due to the nontrivial asymptotically uniform external electromagnetic field. To overcome this difficulty, we adopt the Christodoulou-Ruffini mass relation as a thermodynamic definition of the conserved mass, and identify the associated generator, thereby fixing the ambiguity in defining this conserved mass and constructing the thermodynamic potentials. These thermodynamic quantities naturally satisfy the first law of black-hole thermodynamics as well as the Smarr formula.

</details>


### [162] [Observational Signatures of Rotating Ayón-Beato-García Black Holes: Shadows, Accretion Disks and Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18963)
*Zhenglong Ban,Meng Chen,Rong-Jia Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了旋转Ayón-Beato-García黑洞的阴影、吸积盘和观测图像，分析了电荷参数ζ和自旋a对阴影形态的影响，并与事件视界望远镜（EHT）观测数据对比，约束了参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旋转Ayón-Beato-García黑洞的观测特征，特别是电荷参数ζ对阴影形态和吸积盘图像的影响，旨在通过理论预测与EHT观测数据的对比来约束黑洞物理参数。

Method: 将吸积盘内边缘延伸至事件视界（event horizon），并区分最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）内外粒子动力学；计算不同参数和视角下吸积盘直接辐射和透镜辐射（lensed emissions）的红移分布；使用EHT对M87*和Sgr A*的观测数据，在17°、50°和90°三种倾角下对比理论阴影直径。

Result: 阴影尺寸随电荷参数ζ增大而减小，近极端构型（a=0.95）下阴影呈现独特的"D"形形态；参数(a, ζ)与观测者倾角显著影响图像不对称性和内阴影畸变；高倾角下直接像和透镜像分离形成帽状结构；通过与EHT观测对比，得到与两个源一致的联合约束：0.132811M < ζ < 0.213607M。

Conclusion: 旋转Ayón-Beato-García黑洞的观测特征对电荷参数ζ高度敏感，理论预测与EHT观测数据的对比为约束黑洞物理参数提供了有效方法，所得参数约束与M87*和Sgr A*的观测结果一致。

Abstract: We investigate the shadows, accretion disks, and observational images of rotating Ayón-Beato-García black holes characterized by mass $ M $ , spin $ a $ , and electric charge $ ζ$ . Our analysis reveals that the shadow size decreases with increasing $ ζ$, and in near-extremal configurations (e.g., $ a = 0.95 $), the shadow adopts a distinctive ``D''-shaped morphology. For the accretion disk, we extend its inner edge to the event horizon and account for distinct particle dynamics inside and outside the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO). We find that the correlation between $ (a, ζ) $ and the observer's inclination angle significantly influences image asymmetry and inner shadow distortion. At higher inclinations, the direct and lensed images separate, forming a hat-like structure. Additionally, we compute the redshift distribution of the disk's direct and lensed emissions under varying parameters and viewing angles. By comparing theoretical shadow diameters with the Event Horizon Telescope observations of M87 $^{*}$ and Sgr A $^{*}$--using inclination angles of $17^{\circ} $, $ 50^{\circ} $, and $ 90^{\circ} $--we constrain the viable parameter space, yielding the joint bound $0.132811\,M < ζ< 0.213607\,M$ consistent with both sources.

</details>


### [163] [Revisiting $f(T)$ Teleparallel Gravity with a Parametrized Hubble Parameter and Observational Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18971)
*Khomesh R. Patle,G. P. Singh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在$f(T)$引力框架下研究宇宙加速膨胀的动力学行为，通过假设特定的哈勃参数形式构建两个宇宙学模型，利用贝叶斯统计技术确定模型参数，并分析宇宙学参数的演化及能量条件和状态诊断器的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究$f(T)$引力理论框架下宇宙加速膨胀的动力学行为，通过构建具体的宇宙学模型来探索宇宙膨胀历史和多个宇宙学参数的演化规律。

Method: 采用$f(T)$引力理论框架，假设特定的哈勃参数形式，在两种不同情况下构建两个以红移参数$H(z)$表达的宇宙学模型。使用基于$χ^{2}$最小化方法的贝叶斯统计技术，分别针对宇宙计时器数据集和联合数据集确定模型参数的中值。

Result: 确定了两个宇宙学模型在宇宙计时器和联合数据集下的参数中值，分析了减速参数、能量密度、压强和暗能量状态方程的演化。检验了能量条件的有效性并研究了状态诊断器的性质，同时估算了所提模型的当前宇宙年龄。

Conclusion: 研究在$f(T)$引力框架下成功构建了两个宇宙学模型，通过统计分析确定了模型参数，系统分析了多个宇宙学参数的演化规律，并验证了能量条件和状态诊断器的性质，为理解宇宙加速膨胀的动力学行为提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this paper, the dynamical behavior of the accelerated expansion of the universe is studied within the framework of $f(T)$ gravity by considering a well-motivated functional form of $f(T)$. A specific form of the Hubble parameter is assumed, which under two different cases, leads to two distinct cosmological models expressed in terms of the redshift parameter $H(z)$, providing insights into cosmic dynamics. These models are employed to explore the expansion history of the universe and the evolution of several cosmological parameters. Using Bayesian statistical techniques based on the $χ^{2}$-minimization method, the median values of the model parameters are determined for both the cosmic chronometer (CC) and the joint (CC + Pantheon) datasets. The evolution of the deceleration parameter, energy density, pressure and the equation of state parameter for dark energy is analyzed. Additionally, the validity of the energy conditions and the nature of the statefinder diagnostic are examined. The present age of the universe is also estimated for the proposed models.

</details>

Zhu,Z. -H. Zhu,A. B. Zimmerman,L. Zimmermann,M. E. Zucker,J. Zweizig*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文是三部曲中的首篇，基于LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA网络在GWTC-4.0目录中的91个引力波事件，对广义相对论（GR）进行一致性测试，未发现偏离GR的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）探测器灵敏度提升，探测到的致密双星并合信号数量和质量增加，这为在引力动力学和强场区域对广义相对论（general relativity, GR）进行更灵敏的测试提供了机会。

Method: 分析基于第四代引力波瞬变目录（GWTC-4.0）中的91个高置信度事件，这些事件由至少两个探测器测量且误报率≤10⁻³年⁻¹。论文重点介绍了四种一致性测试方法，包括残差分析、低频与高频波形推断的最终质量和自旋一致性、次主导引力波多极矩振幅以及非GR极化模式检验。

Result: 所有测试均未发现偏离广义相对论模型的证据：残差与噪声一致；从波形低频和高频部分推断的最终质量和最终自旋相互一致；次主导引力波多极矩振幅和非GR极化模式均符合GR预测。

Conclusion: 广义相对论在没有新物理的情况下仍与这些引力波事件一致。三部曲中另外两篇论文的结果也显示总体与真空GR一致，超过90%的事件在90%置信水平上与GR相符，尽管其中一个铃荡分析发现GR值位于其综合结果的尾部。

Abstract: The worldwide LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA network of gravitational-wave (GW) detectors continues to increase in sensitivity, thus increasing the quantity and quality of the detected GW signals from compact binary coalescences. These signals allow us to perform ever-more sensitive tests of general relativity (GR) in the dynamical and strong-field regime of gravity. This paper is the first of three, where we present the results of a suite of tests of GR using the binary signals included in the fourth GW Transient Catalog (GWTC-4.0), i.e., up to and including the first part of the fourth observing run of the detectors (O4a). We restrict our analysis to the 91 confident signals, henceforth called events, that were measured by at least two detectors, and have false alarm rates $\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$. These include 42 events from O4a. This first paper presents an overview of the methods, selection of events and GR tests, and serves as a guidemap for all three papers. Here we focus on the four general tests of consistency, where we find no evidence for deviations from our models. Specifically, for all the events considered, we find consistency of the residuals with noise. The final mass and final spin as inferred from the low- and high-frequency parts of the waveform are consistent with each other. We also find no evidence for deviations from the GR predictions for the amplitudes of subdominant GW multipole moments, or for non-GR modes of polarization. We thus find that GR, without new physics beyond it, is still consistent with these GW events. The results of the two additional papers in this trio also find overall consistency with vacuum GR, with more than 90% of the events being consistent with GR at the 90% credible level. While one of the ringdown analyses finds the GR value in the tails for its combined results, this may be due in part to catalog variance.

</details>

Zimmerman,L. Zimmermann,M. E. Zucker,J. Zweizig*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文作为广义相对论（GR）测试系列论文的第二篇，基于GWTC-4.0中的致密双星并合信号，通过参数化测试检验GR并约束视线加速度，未发现超出GR的物理证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在利用LIGO Virgo KAGRA探测器第四观测运行期（O4a）及之前的数据，通过参数化测试检验广义相对论（GR）在强引力场中的有效性，并约束可能的视线加速度效应。

Method: 研究分析了42个来自O4a的高置信度信号以及49个先前观测运行的事件，重点关注八种参数化测试，包括后牛顿（PN）参数修正、自旋诱导四极矩偏离以及色散或双折射传播效应。

Result: 未发现超出GR的物理证据，90%以上事件的90%可信区间包含零偏差结果；将GR后牛顿系数的偏差界限提高了1.2-5.5倍，并将引力子质量上限更新为$m_g \leq 1.92\times 10^{-23} \mathrm{eV}/c^2$。

Conclusion: 广义相对论在强引力场中保持有效，基于当前事件推导出的许多偏差界限达到了迄今最佳水平，为修改引力理论提供了重要约束。

Abstract: In this second of three papers on tests of general relativity (GR) applied to the compact binary coalescence signals in the fourth Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog (GWTC-4.0), we present the results of the parameterized tests of GR and constraints on line-of-sight acceleration. We include events up to and including the first part of the fourth observing run (O4a) of the LIGO Virgo KAGRA detectors. As in the other two papers in this series, we restrict our analysis to the 42 confident signals, measured by at least two detectors, that have false alarm rates $\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$ from O4a, in addition to the 49 such events from previous observing runs. This paper focuses on the eight tests that constrain parameterized deviations from the expected GR (or unaccelerated) values. These include modifications of post-Newtonian (PN) parameters, spin-induced quadrupole moments different from those of a binary black hole, and possible dispersive or birefringent propagation effects. Overall, we find no evidence for physics beyond GR, for spin-induced quadrupole moments different from those of a Kerr black hole in GR, or for line of sight acceleration, with more than 90% of the events including the null result (no deviation) within their 90% credible intervals. We discuss possible systematics affecting the other events and tests, even though they are statistically not surprising, given noise. We improve the bounds on deviations from the GR PN coefficients by factors of 1.2-5.5 and provide illustrative translations to constraints on some modified theories. Also, we update the bound on the mass of the graviton, at 90% credibility, to $m_g \leq 1.92\times 10^{-23} \mathrm{eV}/c^2$. Thus, we see that GR holds, and many of the bounds on possible deviations derived from our events are the best to date.

</details>

Yamamoto,T. Yamamoto,R. Yamazaki,T. Yan,K. Z. Yang,Y. Yang,Z. Yarbrough,J. Yebana,S. -W. Yeh,A. B. Yelikar,X. Yin,J. Yokoyama,T. Yokozawa,S. Yuan,H. Yuzurihara,M. Zanolin,M. Zeeshan,T. Zelenova,J. -P. Zendri,M. Zeoli,M. Zerrad,M. Zevin,L. Zhang,N. Zhang,R. Zhang,T. Zhang,C. Zhao,Yue Zhao,Yuhang Zhao,Z. -C. Zhao,Y. Zheng,H. Zhong,H. Zhou,H. O. Zhu,Z. -H. Zhu,A. B. Zimmerman,L. Zimmermann,M. E. Zucker,J. Zweizig*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文是广义相对论测试系列论文的第三篇，聚焦于双星并合后残骸的检验。基于GWTC-4.0引力波数据，对42个事件进行七项测试，发现残骸与广义相对论预测总体一致，未发现并合后回波证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在利用第四代引力波瞬变目录（GWTC-4.0）的数据，对双星并合后的残骸进行广义相对论（GR）测试。特别关注检验准正态模谱与克尔黑洞预测的一致性，以及探测广义相对论未预言的并合后回波（echoes）。

Method: 方法包括对LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA探测器第四次观测运行（O4）第一阶段42个事件的分析，结合先前观测数据。采用七项测试：三项检验铃荡（ringdown）及其与克尔黑洞准正态模（quasinormal mode）谱的一致性（两项时域分析，一项频域分析），四项检验可能存在的并合后回波。分析限于置信信号（至少两个探测器测量，误报率≤10⁻³ yr⁻¹）。

Result: 结果显示残骸与广义相对论总体一致。通过似然乘法的分层组合分析发现，广义相对论预测位于98.6⁺¹·⁴₋₉·₄%（99.3⁺⁰·⁷₋₄·₅%）可信区间边界，较GWTC-3.0的93.8⁺⁶·¹₋₂₀·₀%（94.9⁺⁴·⁴₋₁₈·₂%）有所提升。当纳入近期强信号事件GW250114后，显著性降至92.2%（96.2%），表明无明显广义相对论偏离证据。未发现并合后回波证据。

Conclusion: 结论表明当前引力波数据支持广义相对论对并合残骸的描述。观测到的轻微偏离可能源于有限事件样本的统计涨落，而非物理偏离。未检测到并合后回波进一步支持了广义相对论在强场引力下的有效性。

Abstract: This is the third paper of the set recording the results of the suite of tests of general relativity (GR) performed on the signals from the fourth Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog (GWTC-4.0), where we focus on the remnants of the binary mergers. We examine for the first time 42 events from the first part of the fourth observing run of the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA detectors, alongside events from the previous observation runs, restricting our analysis to the confident signals, which were measured in at least two detectors and that have false alarm rates $\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$. This paper focuses on seven tests of the coalescence remnants. Three of these are tests of the ringdown and its consistency with the expected quasinormal mode spectrum of a Kerr black hole. Specifically, two tests analyze just the ringdown in the time domain, and the third test analyzes the entire signal in the frequency domain. Four tests allow for the existence of possible echoes arriving after the end of the ringdown, which are not expected in GR. We find overall consistency of the remnants with GR. When combining events by multiplying likelihoods (hierarchically), one analysis finds that the GR prediction lies at the boundary of the $98.6^{+1.4}_{-9.4}\%$ ($99.3^{+0.7}_{-4.5}\%$) credible region, an increase from $93.8^{+6.1}_{-20.0}\%$ ($94.9^{+4.4}_{-18.2}\%$) for GWTC-3.0. Here the ranges of values comes from bootstrapping to account for the finite number of events analyzed and suggest that some of the apparently significant deviation could be attributed to variance due to the finite catalog. Since the significance also decreases to 92.2% (96.2%) when including the more recent very loud event GW250114, there is no strong evidence for a GR deviation. We find no evidence for post-merger echoes in the events that were analyzed. (Abridged)

</details>


### [167] [Thermodynamic Analysis of Charged AdS Black Holes with Cloud of Strings in Einstein-Bumblebee Gravity via Tsallis Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19034)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在Bumblebee引力框架下，由弦云包围的带电反德西特黑洞的热力学性质。研究发现弦云参数α和洛伦兹破缺参数ℓ会改变黑洞的热力学行为，系统表现出范德瓦尔斯型的小-大黑洞相变，并且Tsallis熵的非广延参数δ显著影响温度分布和稳定性窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探究在Bumblebee引力理论中，考虑弦云包围的带电反德西特黑洞的热力学性质。研究动机源于理解弦云参数、洛伦兹破缺效应以及非广延熵框架如何共同影响黑洞的热力学结构，特别是与标准Reissner-Nordström-AdS黑洞相比的差异。

Method: 研究方法基于扩展相空间描述，推导了相应的状态方程。通过分析霍金温度、自由能、比热和临界行为，研究了系统的相变特性。此外，还考察了Joule-Thomson膨胀及其相关的反转曲线和等焓曲线，并将热力学分析扩展到基于Tsallis熵的框架。

Result: 研究结果显示，系统表现出范德瓦尔斯型的小-大黑洞相变。临界量同时受到弦云和Bumblebee背景的形变影响，而普适比率则因洛伦兹对称性破缺而明显改变。形变参数会改变加热与冷却区域之间的边界，且非广延参数δ显著改变温度分布、稳定性窗口、临界体积、自由能和霍金辐射的稀疏性。

Conclusion: 弦云、洛伦兹破缺和非广延熵的联合效应导致的热力学结构比标准Reissner-Nordström-AdS黑洞显著丰富。这些参数共同塑造了黑洞的热力学行为，揭示了扩展引力理论中黑洞热力学的复杂性。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic properties of charged anti-de Sitter black holes surrounded by a cloud of strings in bumblebee gravity. In this framework, the cloud-of-strings parameter $α$ and the Lorentz-violating parameter $\ell$ modify the horizon structure, the Hawking temperature, the free energies, the specific heat, and the critical behavior in the extended phase-space description. We derive the corresponding equation of state and show that the system exhibits a small--large black-hole phase transition of Van der Waals type. In particular, the critical quantities are deformed by both the cloud of strings and the bumblebee background, while the universal ratio is explicitly altered by Lorentz symmetry breaking. We also examine the Joule--Thomson expansion and analyze the associated inversion and isenthalpic curves, showing how the deformation parameters shift the boundary between heating and cooling regions. In addition, we extend the thermodynamic analysis to a Tsallis entropy-based framework and show that the non-extensive parameter $δ$ significantly changes the temperature profile, stability windows, critical volume, free energies, and sparsity of Hawking radiation. Our results reveal that the combined effects of the string cloud, Lorentz violation, and non-extensive entropy lead to a substantially richer thermodynamic structure than that of the standard Reissner--Nordström--AdS black hole.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法基于庞加莱规范理论框架，该理论将挠率纳入时空几何描述。通过分析包含挠率的引力理论，研究者考察了狄拉克费米子在旋转黑洞背景下的行为，特别关注手征不对称性在能量提取过程中的作用。

Result: 研究结果表明，在包含挠率的时空几何中，狄拉克费米子能够通过手征不对称性从旋转黑洞中提取能量，这一过程在经典广义相对论框架下是不存在的。同时，该能量提取机制与泡利不相容原理保持兼容。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，挠率在黑洞超辐射过程中扮演关键角色，为费米子从旋转黑洞提取能量提供了新机制。这一发现拓展了我们对超越广义相对论的引力理论中黑洞物理的理解，特别是在包含挠率的引力框架下。

Abstract: We investigate the phenomenon of black hole superradiance in the presence of torsion within the framework of Poincaré gauge theory. In particular, in contrast to the classical approach of General Relativity, we show that the inclusion of torsion in the space-time geometry enables the energy extraction from rotating black holes by Dirac fermions via chiral asymmetry, while preserving the Pauli exclusion principle.

### [170] [Asymptotic Expansions for Neural Network Approximations of Quantum Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18033)
*Rômulo Damasclin Chaves dos Santos*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了量子Voronovskaya-Damasclin（QVD）定理，为量子神经网络算子在任意量子信道近似中的渐近行为提供了完整刻画。该结果将经典Voronovskaya定理从标量近似扩展到量子信息理论中的非交换算子框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为量子神经网络模型的渐近分析建立严格的数学基础，并将经典逼近理论、算子代数和量子信息科学直接联系起来。这有助于理解量子神经网络算子在量子信道近似中的收敛机制。

Method: 方法包括引入基于Liouville表示中Fréchet可微性定义的量子Sobolev和Hölder空间的严格类比，并使用完全有界（diamond）范数进行度量。在此框架下推导了近似误差的显式渐近展开。

Result: 主要结果包括建立了QVD定理，获得了近似误差的显式渐近展开，该展开分离了整数阶微分贡献、与有限正则性相关的分数阶修正以及算子代数结构产生的固有非交换效应。同时建立了具有明确依赖于信道正则性和Hilbert空间维数的尖锐余项估计。

Conclusion: 结论表明该研究为量子神经网络模型的渐近分析提供了严格的数学基础，建立了经典逼近理论、算子代数和量子信息科学之间的直接联系，对量子算法和量子机器学习具有重要影响。研究还展示了包括量子中心极限定理、基于算子几何平均的最优插值方法和受Richardson外推启发的收敛加速过程在内的多个应用。

Abstract: This paper establishes the Quantum Voronovskaya--Damasclin (QVD) Theorem, providing a complete asymptotic characterization of Quantum Neural Network Operators in the approximation of arbitrary quantum channels. The result extends the classical Voronovskaya theorem from scalar approximation to the non-commutative operator framework of quantum information theory. We introduce rigorous quantum analogues of Sobolev and Hölder spaces defined through Fréchet differentiability in the Liouville representation and measured using the completely bounded (diamond) norm. Within this framework, we derive an explicit asymptotic expansion of the approximation error and identify the fundamental mechanisms governing convergence. The expansion separates integer-order differential contributions, fractional corrections associated with limited regularity, and intrinsically non-commutative effects arising from operator algebra structure. We also establish a sharp remainder estimate with explicit dependence on the regularity of the channel and the dimension of the underlying Hilbert space. Several applications demonstrate the scope of the theory. These include a quantum central limit theorem describing the fluctuation regime of quantum neural network operators, an optimal interpolation method based on operator geometric means, and a convergence acceleration procedure inspired by Richardson extrapolation. The results provide a rigorous mathematical foundation for the asymptotic analysis of quantum neural network models and establish a direct connection between classical approximation theory, operator algebras, and quantum information science, with implications for quantum algorithms and quantum machine learning.

</details>


### [171] [Towards sample-optimal learning of bosonic Gaussian quantum states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18136)
*Senrui Chen,Francesco Anna Mele,Marco Fanizza,Alfred Li,Zachary Mann,Hsin-Yuan Huang,Yanbei Chen,John Preskill*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了学习n模玻色高斯态（bosonic Gaussian states）所需的最小样本复杂度，针对不同测量方案（高斯测量、任意测量）和状态类型（纯态、被动态）建立了紧致的上下界，并证明了非高斯测量对于最优学习被动高斯态的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续变量系统（continuous-variable systems）在量子计算、通信和传感中具有关键应用，玻色高斯态（bosonic Gaussian states）自然出现在引力波探测和暗物质探测等应用中。核心问题是如何用尽可能少的样本表征未知的玻色高斯态，但经过数十年探索，其效率极限仍不清楚。

Method: 研究通过理论分析推导了学习n模高斯态所需样本数的上下界，考虑了能量约束E和迹距离（trace distance）精度ε。分析了不同测量方案：高斯测量（Gaussian measurements）、任意测量（arbitrary measurements），以及不同状态类型：纯态（pure states）、被动态（passive states）。

Result: 对于高斯测量，证明了Ω(n³/ε²)的下界，与已知上界匹配（仅差双对数能量依赖）。对于任意测量，下界为Ω(n²/ε²)。对于纯态或被动态，上界为Õ(n²/ε²)。有趣的是，高斯测量对纯高斯态学习近乎最优，但非高斯测量对被动高斯态的最优学习是必需的。对于单模高斯态的非纠缠高斯测量，非自适应方案的界为Õ(E/ε²)，表明自适应对能量无关标度至关重要。

Conclusion: 该研究极大地推进了玻色体系中的量子学习理论（quantum learning theory），对量子传感和基准测试应用具有实际影响。作为副产品，建立了高斯态迹距离与其维格纳分布（Wigner distributions）总变差距离（total variation distance）之间的锐利界限，并获得了学习任何高斯态维格纳分布到ε总变差距离的近乎紧致的样本复杂度界。

Abstract: Continuous-variable systems enable key quantum technologies in computation, communication, and sensing. Bosonic Gaussian states emerge naturally in various such applications, including gravitational-wave and dark-matter detection. A fundamental question is how to characterize an unknown bosonic Gaussian state from as few samples as possible. Despite decades-long exploration, the ultimate efficiency limit remains unclear. In this work, we study the necessary and sufficient number of copies to learn an $n$-mode Gaussian state, with energy less than $E$, to $\varepsilon$ trace distance with high probability. We prove a lower bound of $Ω(n^3/\varepsilon^2)$ for Gaussian measurements, matching the best known upper bound up to doubly-log energy dependence, and $Ω(n^2/\varepsilon^2)$ for arbitrary measurements. We further show an upper bound of $\widetilde{O}(n^2/\varepsilon^2)$ given that the Gaussian state is promised to be either pure or passive. Interestingly, while Gaussian measurements suffice for nearly optimal learning of pure Gaussian states, non-Gaussian measurements are provably required for optimal learning of passive Gaussian states. Finally, focusing on learning single-mode Gaussian states via non-entangling Gaussian measurements, we provide a nearly tight bound of $\widetildeΘ(E/\varepsilon^2)$ for any non-adaptive schemes, showing adaptivity is indispensable for nearly energy-independent scaling. As a byproduct, we establish sharp bounds on the trace distance between Gaussian states in terms of the total variation distance between their Wigner distributions, and obtain a nearly tight sample complexity bound for learning the Wigner distribution of any Gaussian state to $\varepsilon$ total variation distance. Our results greatly advance quantum learning theory in the bosonic regimes and have practical impact in quantum sensing and benchmarking applications.

</details>


### [172] [Schrödinger Bridges via the Hacking of Bayesian Priors in Classical and Quantum Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18665)
*Clive Cenxin Aw,Peter Sidajaya*

TL;DR: 本文揭示了"先验黑客（prior hacking）"现象：通过精心设计参考先验分布，可以在固定信道和证据下使贝叶斯更新匹配任意目标分布，从而在表面上执行贝叶斯更新时任意保留预设信念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 贝叶斯规则（Bayes' rule）被广泛视为信念更新的规范方法，但本文旨在揭示其潜在的局限性。研究者发现可以通过操纵参考先验分布来表面上遵循贝叶斯更新，实际上却任意保留预设信念。

Method: 本文证明了在经典和量子设置中，只要贝叶斯逆（Bayesian inversions）定义良好（量子类比为佩茨恢复映射（Petz recovery map）），这种先验黑客通常是可行的。研究者提供了实现此目标的构造性算法，并建立了先验黑客与薛定谔桥问题（Schrödinger bridge problems）之间的对偶关系。

Result: 研究证明先验黑客在经典和量子设置中普遍可行，并建立了与薛定谔桥问题的对偶关系。在量子设置中，这种对偶关系产生了一个在候选桥中唯一、推理一致的选择，形式化地确立了薛定谔桥相对于过程而非参考先验所执行的类贝叶斯更新。

Conclusion: 本文形式化地确立了薛定谔桥在经典和量子设置中相对于过程而非参考先验所执行的类贝叶斯更新。这一发现揭示了贝叶斯更新的潜在局限性，并建立了先验操纵与统计物理中关键对象之间的理论联系。

Abstract: Bayes' rule is widely regarded as the canonical prescription for belief updating. We show, however, that one can arbitrarily preserve pre-specified beliefs while appearing to perform Bayesian updates via "prior hacking": engineering a reference prior distribution such that, for a fixed channel and evidence, the update matches a chosen target distribution. We prove that this is generically possible in both classical and quantum settings whenever Bayesian inversions are well-defined (with the Petz recovery map as the quantum analogue to Bayes' rule), and provide constructive algorithms for doing so. We further establish a duality between prior hacking and Schrödinger bridge problems (a key object in statistical physics with applications in generative modelling), yielding in the quantum setting a unique, inference-consistent selection among candidate bridges. This formally establishes the Bayes-like updating that Schrödinger bridges are performing with respect to the process as opposed to the reference prior, both in classical and quantum settings.

</details>


### [173] [Exact Law of Quantum Reversibility under Gaussian Pure Loss](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19024)
*Ammar Fayad*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究建立了高斯纯损耗（Gaussian pure-loss）动力学中量子反向扩散（quantum reverse diffusion）的精确可逆性定律，揭示了尖锐的相边界（phase boundary）和纯非经典（pure nonclassical）目标的动态奇异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典反向扩散通过在固定噪声下改变漂移项实现。本研究旨在探索量子版本的可逆性原则，特别是在光学衰减通道、压缩光干涉传感和超导玻色子架构中作为连续变量退相干（continuous-variable decoherence）典型模型的高斯纯损耗动力学。

Method: 研究分析了高斯纯损耗动力学中的量子反向扩散过程，考察了完全正性（complete positivity）要求对反向成本的影响。通过建立精确的相边界，确定了反向噪声预算（reverse-noise budget）和最优反向噪声（optimal reverse noise）的几何约束。

Result: 研究发现最小反向成本（minimum reverse cost）在临界压缩-热比（critical squeezing-to-thermal ratio）处精确消失，并在偏离该边界时严格为正。相边界两侧呈现尖锐不对称性：边界下方，标准反向方案如固定扩散贝叶斯反向（fixed-diffusion Bayes reverse）仍可行；边界上方，协方差对齐生成器（covariance-aligned generator）保持CP可行且唯一最优。最优反向噪声同时最小化了几何、计量学和热力学反转代价。

Conclusion: 该研究在典型纯损耗设定中建立了量子可逆性的精确定律，为更广泛的量子反向扩散理论提供了尖锐的基准。研究证实纯量子态（pure quantum state）的精确反转在动态上不可实现，因为最优代价以2/t发散。

Abstract: Classical reverse diffusion is generated by changing the drift at fixed noise. We show that the quantum version of this principle obeys an exact law with a sharp phase boundary. For Gaussian pure-loss dynamics -- the canonical model of continuous-variable decoherence in optical attenuation channels, squeezed-light interferometric sensing, and superconducting bosonic architectures -- complete positivity, the requirement that the dynamics remain physical even for systems entangled with an ancilla, creates an exact phase boundary at which the minimum reverse cost vanishes, fixes the reverse-noise budget on both sides, and makes pure nonclassical targets dynamically singular. The minimum reverse cost vanishes exactly at a critical squeezing-to-thermal ratio and is strictly positive away from it, with a sharp asymmetry: below the boundary, standard reverse prescriptions such as the fixed-diffusion Bayes reverse remain feasible at mild cost; above it, these prescriptions become infeasible, the covariance-aligned generator remains CP-feasible and uniquely optimal, and the cost can be severe. The optimal reverse noise is locked to the state's own fluctuation geometry and simultaneously minimizes the geometric, metrological, and thermodynamic price of reversal. For multimode trajectories, the exact cost is additive in a canonical set of mode-resolved data, and a globally continuous protocol attains this optimum on every mixed-state interval. If a pure nonclassical endpoint is included, the same pointwise law holds for every $t>0$, but the optimum diverges as $2/t$: exact reversal of a pure quantum state is dynamically unattainable. These results establish an exact law of quantum reversibility in the canonical pure-loss setting and provide a sharp benchmark for broader theories of quantum reverse diffusion.

</details>

We analyzed these solutions by deriving the energy expectation values analytically and representing those energy dynamics graphically. We also examined the explicit existence of a non-zero Berry geometric phase in the noncommutative framework and analyzed the role of noncommutativity in generating a non-trivial Berry phase when the model Hamiltonian and the noncommutative parameters are periodic in time. ### [175] [Gravitational Wave-Induced Scrambling Delay in SYK Wormhole Teleportation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18509)

Abstract: Traversable wormhole teleportation in the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model links quantum channel integrity to black hole interior dynamics, using teleportation fidelity to probe holographic scrambling. We characterize the channel response via exact numerical time evolution with disorder averaging at $βJ = 2$. The drive produces a coherent, frequency-selective fidelity suppression, yielding four main results: (i) two amplitude regimes separated near $\varepsilon \sim J$ (perturbative sensing vs.\ strong-drive); (ii) the channel acts as a low-pass filter, most sensitive at $ω\lesssim β^{-1}$ with monotone recovery above the thermal scale; (iii) an inspiral chirp drive delays the fidelity peak by $Δt_{\rm scr}^{(\rm fid)} = +0.11\, J^{-1}$, corroborated by an out-of-time-order correlator (OTOC) diagnostic ($Δt_{\rm scr}^{(\rm OTOC)} = +0.20\, J^{-1}$), establishing a genuine scrambling delay; and (iv) the effects persist across $N \in \{10, 12, 14, 16\}$ Majorana modes, indicating no systematic finite-size suppression. These results establish that holographic teleportation channels degrade gracefully under GW-inspired boundary deformations, with direct implications for near-term quantum processor implementations of traversable wormholes.

### [176] [Anomalous localization and duality in non-Hermitian quasiperiodic models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17404)
*Wenzhi Wang,Tianyu Li,Wei Yi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了非厄米准周期晶格中边界条件与局域化性质之间的反直觉关系：安德森局域态对边界敏感，而扩展-局域对偶关系在非局域态中可能失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米系统中的边界条件具有显著影响，如非厄米趋肤效应所示。研究旨在探索准周期性和非厄米趋肤效应的相互作用如何影响一维非厄米准周期晶格中的局域化性质。

Method: 研究聚焦于一维非厄米准周期晶格，从李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponents）的视角分析和设计这些现象。通过比较周期边界条件和开放边界条件下的行为来研究边界敏感性。

Result: 发现两个主要结果：周期边界条件下的安德森局域态具有边界敏感性，源于周期边界条件与准周期性的不兼容性；非局域态中，扩展-局域对偶关系可能失效，因为其对偶模型中的对应态也可能是非局域的。

Conclusion: 这些发现为非厄米准周期系统中的局域化现象提供了新的见解，揭示了边界条件、准周期性和非厄米性之间复杂的相互作用，以及传统对偶关系的局限性。

Abstract: Boundary conditions can have dramatic impact in non-Hermitian systems, as exemplified by the non-Hermitian skin effect. Focusing on one-dimensional non-Hermitian quasiperioidic lattices, we show that the interplay of quasiperiodicity and the non-Hermitian skin effect leads to counterintuitive localization properties. On the one hand, for Anderson localized states under the periodic boundary condition, we find that their localization features can be boundary-sensitive, which originates from the incompatibility of the periodic boundary condition with quasiperiodicity. On the other hand, for non-localized states, the well-known extended-localized duality relation can break down, as their counterparts in the dual model can also be nonlocal. We discuss how these remarkable phenomena can be engineered and analyzed from the perspective of Lyapunov exponents. Our findings shed new light on localization in non-Hermitian quasiperiodic systems.

### [177] [Postselection induced localization and coherence in quantum walks on heterogeneous networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17629)
*Adithya L J,Suraj S Hegde,Chandrakala Meena*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了后选择（postselection）在连续时间量子行走（CTQW）中引入的非线性效应，揭示了在两种退相干机制下的显著差异：Haken-Strobl机制中非线性贡献精确抵消，而量子随机行走（QSW）机制中后选择能在异质度网络上打破动力学平衡，诱导稳健的局域化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子轨迹的后选择（postselection）已知能有效在开放量子系统动力学中引入非线性。本研究旨在探索这种非线性在具有同质和异质度分布的网络上连续时间量子行走（continuous-time quantum walks, CTQWs）中的效应，以理解后选择如何影响量子输运和局域化。

Method: 采用最近提出的非线性Lindblad主方程（nonlinear Lindblad master equation, NLME），研究两种退相干机制下的动力学：Haken-Strobl退相干和量子随机行走（quantum stochastic walk, QSW）退相干。分析扩展到多体自旋系统，考察度异质性对自旋激发局域化的影响。

Result: 分析揭示了一个显著的二分现象：在Haken-Strobl退相干下，非线性贡献精确抵消，产生与后选择细节无关的均匀稳态。相反，QSW退相干允许后选择在异质度网络上打破动力学平衡，优先在低度（外围）节点诱导稳健的局域化，且该局域化态保持有限的量子相干性。在多体自旋系统中，度异质性同样稳定了自旋向下背景中自旋向上激发的局域化，增强了纠缠保持。

Conclusion: 这些发现确立了度异质性（degree heterogeneity）和后选择（postselection）作为在耗散动力学中调控量子输运和局域化的联合控制参数。异质网络结构结合后选择操作能够有效诱导并维持量子态的非均匀分布和相干性。

Abstract: Postselection of quantum trajectories is known effectively introduce nonlinearity into dynamics of open quantum systems. We study the effect of such non-linearity in continuous-time quantum walks (CTQWs) on networks with homogeneous and heterogeneous degree distributions. Using the recently proposed nonlinear Lindblad master equation (NLME), we investigate the dynamics under two decoherence mechanisms: Haken-Strobl and quantum stochastic walk (QSW). Our analysis reveals a striking dichotomy: under Haken-Strobl decoherence the nonlinear contributions precisely cancel, yielding a uniform steady state independent of postselection details. In stark contrast, QSW decoherence permits postselection to break dynamical balance on heterogeneous networks, inducing robust localization preferentially at low-degree (peripheral) nodes. Remarkably, this localized state maintains finite quantum coherence. Extending our results to many-body spin systems, we demonstrate that degree heterogeneity similarly stabilizes localization of spin-up excitations in spin-down backgrounds, enhancing entanglement preservation. These findings establish degree heterogeneity and postselection as joint control parameters for engineering quantum transport and localization in dissipative dynamics.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过将合适的脉冲序列（pulse sequences）应用于双量子比特传感器，在T₂光谱（T₂ spectroscopy）框架内实现响应和噪声的分离提取。该方法利用代表性示例进行验证，能够解析多体系统中关联的时空传播。

Result: 该方法产生的关联退相干信号（correlated dephasing signal）能够捕捉低能激发的色散特征，表现为关联传播中的类光锥轮廓（light-cone-like profiles）。在非平衡条件下，外部驱动会改变这一轮廓，在光锥外产生额外的条纹。该方法还能清晰区分系统中的不同输运机制，包括弹道扩散（ballistic spreading）、扩散展宽（diffusive broadening）及其交叉区域。

Conclusion: 该双量子比特传感方法不仅能够分离环境响应和噪声，还能解析多体系统中关联的时空传播特征，包括平衡和非平衡条件下的不同行为，并能区分不同的输运机制，为量子传感在多体系统研究中的应用提供了新途径。

Abstract: Multi-qubit quantum sensors are rapidly emerging as platforms that extend the capabilities of conventional single-qubit sensing. In this work we show how suitable pulse sequences applied to a two-qubit sensor enable separate extraction of the response and noise of a probed environment within a $T_2$ spectroscopy framework. By resorting to representative examples, we demonstrate that this approach can resolve the spatio-temporal spreading of correlations in a many-body system. In particular, the resulting correlated dephasing signal captures features such as the dispersion of low-energy excitations, which manifest as light-cone-like profiles in the propagation of correlations. We further show that non-equilibrium conditions, for instance those induced by external driving, can modify this profile by producing additional fringes outside the light-cone. As a complementary application, we demonstrate that the method clearly distinguishes between different transport regimes in the system, including ballistic spreading, diffusive broadening, and the crossover between them.

Abstract: Kinetically constrained models have been widely studied in the context of glass formers and non-equilibrium statistical mechanics. In this work, we investigate monitored quantum circuit models that interpolate between classical stochastic and unitary quantum dynamics. By interpreting space-time resolved records as microstates of a fictitious 1+1D spin system, we employ thermodynamic concepts that allow us to investigate the dynamical coexistence between an active and inactive phase. Abstract: Ergotropy, the maximum work extractable from a quantum system, is a central resource in quantum physics. ### [182] [Cavity Control of Strongly Correlated Electrons Beyond Resonant Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18933)
*Lukas Grunwald,Xinle Cheng,Emil Viñas Boström,Michael Ruggenthaler,Marios H. Michael,Dante M. Kennes,Angel Rubio*

TL;DR: 该研究通过非微扰计算揭示了电磁腔（electromagnetic cavity）如何通过真空涨落（vacuum fluctuations）调控强关联电子系统的磁交换相互作用（magnetic exchange interaction），建立了腔几何结构与材料响应之间的设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索电磁腔与材料界面耦合如何通过结构化的真空涨落改变平衡性质。特别是光与强关联电子（correlated electrons）的耦合缺乏特征能量尺度，使得这类系统的真空诱导修饰本质上处于非共振（off-resonant）状态，并对完整光子模式结构敏感。

Conclusion: 该研究框架建立了连接腔几何结构与材料响应的具体设计原则，特别针对非共振区域（off-resonant regime），这将指导未来的实验和理论探索。研究还揭示了静态库仑屏蔽（static Coulomb screening）与矢量势（vector potential）产生的动力学效应之间的竞争，表明同时包含这两种效应对于获得定性正确的预测至关重要。

Abstract: Interfacing materials with electromagnetic cavities offers a route to modify equilibrium properties through structured vacuum fluctuations. The coupling of light with correlated electrons lacks a characteristic energy scale, making vacuum induced modifications of such systems inherently off-resonant and sensitive to the full photon mode structure. Here, we present a non-perturbative calculation of the cavity induced modification of the magnetic exchange interaction $J$ of the half-filled Hubbard model, including all cavity modes and with parameters determined from first principles. We show that the strength of the modification is controlled by a generalized Purcell factor, proportional to the frequency integrated photonic density of states. This result identifies polaritonic surface cavities as promising platforms to modify correlated systems, while standard Fabry-Pérot resonators produce negligible effects due to spectral weight cancellations upon integration. To perform the calculation, we develop a consistent quantization scheme for materials coupled to a dielectric substrate, in the Coulomb gauge, which reveals a competition between static Coulomb screening and dynamical effects arising from the vector potential. Including both effects is essential to obtain even qualitatively correct predictions. For a gold substrate the light-matter interactions lead to a net enhancement of $J$, whose magnitude is large enough to be observable in two-magnon Raman spectroscopy. Our framework establishes a concrete design principle linking cavity geometry to material response in the off-resonant regime, which will guide future experimental and theoretical explorations.

Abstract: Spectral statistics probe integrability versus chaos and have recently been extended to Markovian open quantum systems described by Lindbladians, whose quantum-trajectory unraveling decomposes the evolution into no-jump dynamics generated by an effective non-Hermitian Hamiltonian and recycling jumps. In this work, we perform spectrum-statistics diagnostics for Lindbladians and their effective non-Hermitian Hamiltonians. We show that recycling processes, symmetry constraints, and the Liouville-space structure crucially shape the spectral correlations. In particular, we identify a family of spectrally separable Lindbladians whose spectra exhibit robust Poisson statistics, despite the effective non-Hermitian Hamiltonian varying from regular to chaotic. Our work establishes a unified spectral-statistics characterization for Lindbladians and their associated effective non-Hermitian Hamiltonians, deepening our understanding of integrable and chaotic spectral properties in open many-body systems.

Motivation: 化学和材料科学被认为是量子硬件的潜在杀手级应用领域，但量子算法发展必须适应新兴量子硬件的实际约束，同时经典波函数理论方法的持续进步缩小了量子优势的窗口。

Method: 从实用规模应用（utility-scale applications）的宏观视角探索量子计算的潜在益处，强调量子算法不仅需要处理少数强关联分子结构，还必须支持量子加速计算与高通量流程的集成。

Result: 论文提出量子算法需要支持将量子加速计算实际集成到任意分子的常规计算高通量管道中，最终为社会提供切实价值，而不仅仅是针对少数难以用传统方法描述的强关联分子结构进行精确计算。

Conclusion: 量子计算在化学领域的成功不仅取决于对少数挑战性分子的精确计算能力，更关键的是能够将量子加速计算无缝整合到实际应用的高通量工作流中，实现真正的社会价值。

Abstract: Chemistry and materials science are widely regarded as potential killer application fields for quantum hardware. While the dream of unlocking unprecedented simulation capabilities remains compelling, quantum algorithm development must adapt to the evolving constraints of the emerging quantum hardware in order to accomplish any advantage for the computational chemistry practice. At the same time, the continuous advancement of classical wavefunction-theory methods narrows the window for a broad quantum advantage. Here, we explore potential benefits of quantum computation from the broader perspective of utility-scale applications. We argue that quantum algorithms need not only enable accurate calculations for a few challenging, that is strongly correlated, molecular structures, that might be hard to describe with traditional methods. Instead, they must also support the practical integration of quantum-accelerated computations into high-throughput pipelines for routine calculations on arbitrary molecules, ultimately delivering a tangible value to society.

</details>


### [185] [Active Quantum Particles from Engineered Dissipation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19094)
*Jeanne Gipouloux,Matteo Brunelli,Leticia Cugliandolo,Rosario Fazio,Marco Schirò*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了基于工程耗散（engineered dissipation）的主动量子粒子模型，包括具有相干和耗散跃迁的晶格模型，以及量子化的主动Ornstein-Uhlenbeck过程、跑动-翻滚动力学和主动布朗粒子模型。研究显示这些模型均表现出主动运动的关键特征，包括从扩散到主动-扩散行为的交叉，以及由Liouville皮肤效应引起的边界条件敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于通过工程耗散（engineered dissipation）构建主动量子粒子模型，将经典主动物质（active matter）概念扩展到量子领域。该工作旨在探索量子系统中主动行为的微观机制和特征。

Method: 方法包括引入并表征多种主动量子粒子模型：具有相干和耗散跃迁（coherent and dissipative hopping）的晶格模型，以及量子化的主动Ornstein-Uhlenbeck过程、跑动-翻滚动力学（run-and-tumble dynamics）和主动布朗粒子（active Brownian particle）模型。这些模型均基于非平衡环境（nonequilibrium environment）的工程耗散构建。

Result: 结果显示所有模型均表现出主动运动的关键特征，包括长时间尺度下从扩散到主动-扩散行为（active-diffusive behavior）的交叉，产生有效Péclet数。研究还观察到边界条件的强敏感性，这源于开放量子系统背景下的Liouville皮肤效应（Liouville skin effect）。

Conclusion: 结论表明基于工程耗散的主动量子粒子模型能够展现主动运动的本质特征，为量子主动物质（quantum active matter）研究提供了理论框架。论文讨论了量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）的作用，并展望了超导电路或冷气体中的实验实现，以及量子主动物质中多体效应（many-body effects）的研究前景。

Abstract: We introduce and characterize different models for an active quantum particle where activity arises from engineered dissipation-- specifically, from a suitably coupled nonequilibrium environment. These include a model of a particle moving on a lattice with coherent and dissipative hopping, as well as quantum generalizations of well-studied models of active behavior, such as the active Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process, run-and-tumble dynamics, and the active Brownian particle. Despite the different microscopic mechanisms at play, we show that all these models display key features of active motion. Notably, we observe a crossover from diffusive to active-diffusive behavior at long times, leading to an effective Péclet number, as well as a strong sensitivity to boundary conditions which, in our open quantum system context, arises from the Liouville skin effect. We discuss the role of quantum fluctuations and experimental realizations with superconducting circuits or cold gases, closing with perspectives for many-body effects in quantum active matter.

</details>
